    function getResourceReadyAt(node, baseMs, resourceKey) {

        const boostedTime = parseInt(data.boostedTime || 0, 10) || 0;
        return usedAt + Math.max(0, baseMs - boostedTime);
    }

    function readDecimal(value, fallback = 0) {
        let parsed = parseFloat(value || fallback);
        if (!Number.isFinite(parsed)) {
            return fallback;
        }
        return parsed;
    }

    function calculateOraclePrice(itemName, basePrice, type = "sell") {

    function saveBuyBudgetLocks() {

    function rememberBuyBudgetLock(seed, requiredCoins) {
        let required = Math.max(0, parseFloat(requiredCoins || 0));
        if (!seed || required <= 0) {
            return;
        }

        buyBudgetLocks[seed] = required;
        saveBuyBudgetLocks();
    }

    function clearBuyBudgetLock(seed) {
        if (!seed || buyBudgetLocks[seed] === undefined) {
            return;
        }

        delete buyBudgetLocks[seed];
        saveBuyBudgetLocks();
    }

    function refreshBuyBudgetLocks() {
        let entries = Object.entries(buyBudgetLocks);
        for (let i = 0; i < entries.length; i++) {
            let seed = entries[i][0];
            let required = parseFloat(entries[i][1] || 0);
            if (required > 0 && SL_COINS >= required) {
                clearBuyBudgetLock(seed);
                log(`âœ… ${seed} alÄ±mÄ± iÃ§in bÃ¼tÃ§e limiti tamamlandÄ± (${formatCoinAmount(required)} coin). GÃ¶rev tekrar aktif.`);
            }
        }
    }

    function getSpecialEventSaleInfo(itemName, nowMs) {
        let currentEvents = {};
        if (SL_EVENTS && SL_EVENTS.current && typeof SL_EVENTS.current === "object") {
            currentEvents = SL_EVENTS.current;
        }

        let eventEntries = Object.values(currentEvents);
        for (let i = 0; i < eventEntries.length; i++) {
            let ev = eventEntries[i];
            if (!ev || !ev.isEligible) {
                continue;
            }

            let startAt = parseTimeValue(ev.startAt) || 0;
            let endAt = parseTimeValue(ev.endAt) || Infinity;
            if (startAt > nowMs || endAt <= nowMs) {
                continue;
            }

            let bonus = ev.bonus || {};
            let cropBonus = bonus[itemName] || {};
            let multiplier = parseFloat(cropBonus.saleMultiplier);
            if (Number.isFinite(multiplier) && multiplier > 0) {
                return {
                    active: true,
                    multiplier: multiplier,
                    eventName: ev.name || ev.event || ev.id || "Event",
                    startAt: startAt || 0,
                    endAt: endAt === Infinity ? 0 : endAt
                };
            }
        }

        return { active: false, multiplier: 0, eventName: "", startAt: 0, endAt: 0 };
    }

    function getSpecialEventSaleMultiplier(itemName, nowMs) {
        return getSpecialEventSaleInfo(itemName, nowMs).multiplier || 0;
    }

    function calculateClientSellPrice(itemName, basePrice, createdAt) {

    function formatCoinAmount(value) {
        return parseFloat(value || 0).toFixed(4);
    }

    function formatTimeLeftMs(endAt, nowMs = Date.now()) {
        if (!endAt || endAt <= nowMs) {
            return "";
        }

        let totalSeconds = Math.max(0, Math.floor((endAt - nowMs) / 1000));
        let hours = Math.floor(totalSeconds / 3600);
        let minutes = Math.floor((totalSeconds % 3600) / 60);
        let seconds = totalSeconds % 60;

        if (hours > 0) {
            return hours + "h " + minutes + "m";
        }

        if (minutes > 0) {
            return minutes + "m " + seconds + "s";
        }

        return seconds + "s";
    }

    function predictionsMatchActions(prediction, actions) {
        if (!prediction || !Array.isArray(prediction.actions) || !Array.isArray(actions)) {
            return false;
        }

        if (prediction.actions.length !== actions.length) {
            return false;
        }

        for (let i = 0; i < actions.length; i++) {
            let expected = prediction.actions[i];
            let actual = actions[i];
            if (!actual || expected.type !== actual.type) {
                return false;
            }

            if (expected.crop !== actual.crop || expected.item !== actual.item) {
                return false;
            }

            if (String(expected.amount) !== String(actual.amount)) {
                return false;
            }
        }

        return true;
    }

                    return "Bilinmeyen Etkinlik Tespit Edildi: [" + activeEvents[i] + "]";
                }
            }

        if (SL_BUMPKIN && SL_BUMPKIN.buffs && Object.keys(SL_BUMPKIN.buffs).length > 0) {
            return "Bilinmeyen Buff Tespit Edildi: [" + Object.keys(SL_BUMPKIN.buffs)[0] + "]";
        }

        return null;
    }

    function getMarketSeedDetails(seed) {
        if (ALL_KNOWN_SEEDS.includes(seed)) {
            let crop = seed.replace(" Seed", "");
            return {
                seed: seed,
                price: SEED_PRICES[seed] || defaultSeedPrices[seed] || 0,
                type: "Basic Crop",
                plantSeconds: Math.floor((BASE_CROP_TIMES[crop] || 0) / 1000),
                bumpkinLevel: SEED_LEVEL_REQUIREMENTS[seed] || 1,
                yield: crop,
                plantingSpot: "Crop Plot",
                supportedForBot: true
            };
        }

        if (EXTRA_MARKET_SEED_DETAILS[seed]) {
            return {
                seed: seed,
                ...EXTRA_MARKET_SEED_DETAILS[seed],
                supportedForBot: false
            };
        }

        return {
            seed: seed,
            price: null,
            type: "Unknown",
            plantSeconds: 0,
            bumpkinLevel: 1,
            yield: seed.replace(" Seed", "").replace(" Plant", ""),
            plantingSpot: "",
            supportedForBot: false
        };
    }

    function getSellCropDetails(crop) {
        let basePrice = CROP_SELL_PRICES[crop] || defaultSellPrices[crop] || 0;
        let saleInfo = getSpecialEventSaleInfo(crop, Date.now());
        let livePrice = calculateOraclePrice(crop, basePrice, "sell");
        return {
            crop: crop,
            price: livePrice,
            basePrice: basePrice,
            saleInfo: saleInfo,

            amount: getInventoryAmount(crop),
            seed: crop + " Seed"
        };

        const RULE_STORAGE_KEY = 'sl_client_contract_guard_v1';
        const INITIAL_SUPPORTED_PLOTS = { basic: 17, default: 18 };
        const WELL_PLOT_SUPPORT = 8;
        const ADVANCED_CROPS = new Set(["Eggplant", "Corn", "Onion", "Turnip", "Radish", "Wheat", "Kale", "Artichoke", "Barley"]);
        const SUMMER_CROPS = new Set(["Tomato", "Lemon", "Blueberry", "Orange", "Apple", "Banana"]);
        const AUTUMN_CROPS = new Set(["Pumpkin", "Yam", "Soybean", "Corn", "Wheat"]);
        const UNSUPPORTED_YIELD_WEARABLES = [
            "Green Amulet", "Sunflower Amulet", "Beetroot Amulet", "Eggplant Onesie",
            "Corn Onesie", "Corn Silk Hair", "Sickle", "Infernal Pitchfork",
            "Blossom Ward", "Frozen Heart"
        ];
        const UNSUPPORTED_YIELD_COLLECTIBLES = [
            "Golden Cauliflower", "Easter Bunny", "Victoria Sisters", "Scarecrow",
            "Kuebiko", "Coder", "Peeled Potato", "Potent Potato", "Stellar Sunflower",
            "Radical Radish", "Cabbage Boy", "Cabbage Girl", "Karkinos",
            "Pablo The Bunny", "Foliant", "Purple Trail", "Maximus",
            "Giant Artichoke", "Giant Yam", "Sheaf of Plenty", "Giant Kale",
            "Legendary Shrine", "Knowledge Crab", "Hoot", "Scary Mike",
            "Sir Goldensnout", "Laurie the Chuckle Crow", "Queen Cornelia", "Gnome"
        ];

        const REQUIRED_CLIENT_MARKERS = [
            "/autosave/",
            "x-amz-ttl",
            "cachedKey",
            "deviceTrackerId",
            "stateHash",
            "sessionId",
            "clientVersion",
            "tool.crafted",
            "timber.chopped",
            "stoneRock.mined",
            "ironRock.mined",
            "goldRock.mined",
            "seed.planted",
            "crop.harvested",
            "seed.bought",
            "crop.sold",
            "rod.casted",
            "rod.reeled",
            "mushroom.picked",
            "bumpkin.feed",
            "recipe.cooked"
        ];

        const OPTIONAL_CLIENT_MARKERS = [
            "FIRE_PIT_COOKABLES",
            "KITCHEN_COOKABLES",
            "BAKERY_COOKABLES",
            "DELI_COOKABLES",
            "JUICE_COOKABLES",
            "getSupportedPlots",
            "getCropPlotTime",
            "getSellPrice$1",
            "CROP_SHORTAGE_HOURS",
            "INITIAL_STOCK"
        ];

        let auditPromise = null;
        let lastAuditOk = false;

        function asNumber(value, fallback = 0) {
            const parsed = parseFloat(value);
            return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : fallback;
        }

        function getLevelThresholds() {
            return {
                1: 0, 2: 2, 3: 22, 4: 205, 5: 555, 6: 1155, 7: 2155,
                8: 3405, 9: 5405, 10: 7905, 11: 10905, 12: 14405,
                13: 18405, 14: 22905, 15: 27905, 16: 33655, 17: 40155,
                18: 47405, 19: 55405, 20: 64155, 21: 73905, 22: 84655,
                23: 96405, 24: 109155, 25: 122905, 26: 137405,
                27: 152905, 28: 169405, 29: 186905, 30: 205405,
                31: 225405, 32: 246905, 33: 269905, 34: 294405,
                35: 320405, 36: 348405, 37: 378405, 38: 410405,
                39: 444405, 40: 480405
            };
        }

        function getBumpkinLevel(experience) {
            const xp = asNumber(experience, 0);
            const thresholds = getLevelThresholds();
            let level = 1;
            for (let i = 1; i <= 40; i++) {
                if (xp >= thresholds[i]) {
                    level = i;
                } else {
                    break;
                }
            }
            return level;
        }

        function getCurrentBumpkinLevel() {
            return getBumpkinLevel((SL_BUMPKIN && SL_BUMPKIN.experience) || 0);
        }

        function getCurrentBumpkinLevelProgress() {
            const xp = asNumber((SL_BUMPKIN && SL_BUMPKIN.experience) || 0, 0);
            const level = getBumpkinLevel(xp);
            const thresholds = getLevelThresholds();
            const currentStart = thresholds[level] || 0;
            const nextStart = thresholds[level + 1] || currentStart;
            const current = Math.max(0, Math.floor(xp - currentStart));
            const needed = Math.max(0, Math.floor(nextStart - currentStart));
            const percent = needed > 0 ? Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round((current / needed) * 100))) : 100;
            return { level: level, current: current, needed: needed, percent: percent, totalXp: Math.floor(xp) };
        }

        function getSeedLevelRequirement(seed) {
            return SEED_LEVEL_REQUIREMENTS[seed] || 1;
        }

        function canBuySeed(seed) {
            return getCurrentBumpkinLevel() >= getSeedLevelRequirement(seed);
        }

        function getCurrentSeason() {
            return ((SL_SEASON && SL_SEASON.season) || "spring").toLowerCase();
        }

        function canRestockShipment(nowMs = Date.now()) {
            const last = new Date((SL_SHIPMENTS && SL_SHIPMENTS.restockedAt) || 0).toISOString().slice(0, 10);
            const today = new Date(nowMs).toISOString().slice(0, 10);
            return last !== today;
        }

        function getNextShipmentText(nowMs = Date.now()) {
            if (canRestockShipment(nowMs)) {
                return "Free ready";
            }
            const next = new Date(nowMs);
            next.setUTCHours(24, 0, 0, 0);
            const left = Math.max(0, next.getTime() - nowMs);
            return formatTimeLeftMs(nowMs + left, nowMs);
        }

        function isSeedInCurrentSeason(seed) {
            const season = getCurrentSeason();
            const allowed = SEASONAL_CROP_SEEDS[season] || SEASONAL_CROP_SEEDS.spring;
            return allowed.includes(seed);
        }

        function getVisibleMarketSeeds() {
            const season = getCurrentSeason();
            return SEASONAL_MARKET_SEEDS[season] || SEASONAL_MARKET_SEEDS.spring;
        }

        function hasSkill(name) {
            return !!(SL_BUMPKIN && SL_BUMPKIN.skills && SL_BUMPKIN.skills[name]);
        }

        function hasInventory(name) {
            return asNumber(SL_INVENTORY && SL_INVENTORY[name], 0) >= 1;
        }

        function equippedNames() {
            if (!SL_BUMPKIN || !SL_BUMPKIN.equipped) {
                return [];
            }
            return Object.values(SL_BUMPKIN.equipped).filter(Boolean);
        }

        function isWearableActive(name) {
            return equippedNames().includes(name);
        }

        function isCollectibleArrayActive(list) {
            return Array.isArray(list) && list.some(function(item) {
                return item && item.coordinates && !item.removedAt;
            });
        }

        function isCollectibleBuilt(name) {
            const farmList = SL_COLLECTIBLES && SL_COLLECTIBLES[name];
            const homeList = SL_HOME && SL_HOME.collectibles && SL_HOME.collectibles[name];
            const interiorList = SL_INTERIOR && SL_INTERIOR.ground && SL_INTERIOR.ground.collectibles && SL_INTERIOR.ground.collectibles[name];
            const levelOneList = SL_INTERIOR && SL_INTERIOR.level_one && SL_INTERIOR.level_one.collectibles && SL_INTERIOR.level_one.collectibles[name];
            return isCollectibleArrayActive(farmList) || isCollectibleArrayActive(homeList) || isCollectibleArrayActive(interiorList) || isCollectibleArrayActive(levelOneList);
        }

        function isTemporaryCollectibleActive(name) {
            return isCollectibleBuilt(name);
        }

        function isBuffActive(name) {
            return !!(SL_BUFFS && SL_BUFFS[name]);
        }

        function getPlacedCollectible(name) {
            const list = SL_COLLECTIBLES && SL_COLLECTIBLES[name];
            if (!Array.isArray(list)) return null;
            return list.find(function(item) {
                return item && item.coordinates && !item.removedAt;
            }) || null;
        }

        function isBasicScarecrowCrop(cropName) {
            const pumpkinTime = BASE_CROP_TIMES["Pumpkin"] || 0;
            const cropTime = BASE_CROP_TIMES[cropName] || 0;
            return cropTime > 0 && pumpkinTime > 0 && cropTime <= pumpkinTime;
        }

        function getBasicScarecrowBoost(cropName, plotObj) {
            const scarecrow = getPlacedCollectible("Basic Scarecrow");
            if (!scarecrow || !plotObj || plotObj.x === undefined || plotObj.y === undefined || !isBasicScarecrowCrop(cropName)) {
                return { active: false, multiplier: 1, boosts: [] };
            }

            const radius = hasSkill("Chonky Scarecrow") ? 3 : 2;
            const dx = Number(plotObj.x) - Number(scarecrow.coordinates.x);
            const dy = Number(plotObj.y) - Number(scarecrow.coordinates.y);

            if (!Number.isFinite(dx) || !Number.isFinite(dy) || Math.abs(dx) > radius || Math.abs(dy) > radius) {
                return { active: false, multiplier: 1, boosts: [] };
            }

            if (SL_AOE && SL_AOE["Basic Scarecrow"] && SL_AOE["Basic Scarecrow"][dx] && SL_AOE["Basic Scarecrow"][dx][dy] > Date.now()) {
                return { active: false, multiplier: 1, boosts: [] };
            }

            if (hasSkill("Chonky Scarecrow")) {
                return { active: true, multiplier: 0.7, boosts: ["Chonky Scarecrow x0.7", "Basic Scarecrow x0.8"], dx: dx, dy: dy };
            }

            return { active: true, multiplier: 0.8, boosts: ["Basic Scarecrow x0.8"], dx: dx, dy: dy };
        }

        function getIslandType() {
            return (SL_ISLAND && SL_ISLAND.type) || "basic";
        }

        function isWaterWellPlaced() {
            const wells = SL_BUILDINGS && SL_BUILDINGS["Water Well"];
            return Array.isArray(wells) && wells.some(function(well) {
                return well && well.coordinates && !well.removedAt;
            });
        }

        function getSupportedPlotCount(nowMs = Date.now()) {
            const islandType = getIslandType();
            const initial = islandType === "basic" ? INITIAL_SUPPORTED_PLOTS.basic : INITIAL_SUPPORTED_PLOTS.default;
            if (!isWaterWellPlaced()) {
                return initial;
            }

            let level = Math.max(1, parseInt((SL_WATER_WELL && SL_WATER_WELL.level) || 1) || 1);
            const upgradeReadyAt = parseTimeValue(SL_WATER_WELL && SL_WATER_WELL.upgradeReadyAt);
            if (upgradeReadyAt && upgradeReadyAt > nowMs) {
                level -= 1;
            }

            if (level >= 4) {
                return 99;
            }

            return initial + Math.max(0, level) * WELL_PLOT_SUPPORT;
        }

        function getWaterCapacityInfo(nowMs = Date.now()) {
            const islandType = getIslandType();
            const initial = islandType === "basic" ? INITIAL_SUPPORTED_PLOTS.basic : INITIAL_SUPPORTED_PLOTS.default;
            const wells = (SL_BUILDINGS && SL_BUILDINGS["Water Well"]) || [];
            const wellPlaced = isWaterWellPlaced();
            const rawLevel = Math.max(1, parseInt((SL_WATER_WELL && SL_WATER_WELL.level) || 1) || 1);
            const upgradeReadyAt = parseTimeValue(SL_WATER_WELL && SL_WATER_WELL.upgradeReadyAt);
            const upgrading = !!(upgradeReadyAt && upgradeReadyAt > nowMs);
            const effectiveLevel = wellPlaced ? Math.max(0, rawLevel - (upgrading ? 1 : 0)) : 0;
            const supportedByWater = getSupportedPlotCount(nowMs);
            const manualLimit = supportedByWater;
            const activeLimit = Math.max(0, supportedByWater);
            const totalPlots = Object.keys(SL_CROPS || {}).length;
            const waterLocked = Math.max(0, totalPlots - supportedByWater);
            const manualLocked = 0;

            return {
                islandType: islandType,
                initialPlots: initial,
                wellPlaced: wellPlaced,
                wellCount: Array.isArray(wells) ? wells.filter(function(well) { return well && well.coordinates && !well.removedAt; }).length : 0,
                wellLevel: rawLevel,
                effectiveWellLevel: effectiveLevel,
                upgrading: upgrading,
                upgradeReadyAt: upgradeReadyAt || 0,
                supportedByWater: supportedByWater,
                manualLimit: manualLimit,
                activeLimit: activeLimit,
                totalPlots: totalPlots,
                waterLocked: waterLocked,
                manualLocked: manualLocked,
                unlimitedWater: wellPlaced && effectiveLevel >= 4
            };
        }

        function getSafeAndQuarantinedPlotsByRules() {
            let sortedEntries = Object.entries(SL_CROPS || {}).sort(function(a, b) {
                return (a[1].createdAt || 0) - (b[1].createdAt || 0);
            });

            const supportedByWater = getSupportedPlotCount();
            const manualLimit = supportedByWater;
            const limit = Math.max(0, supportedByWater);
            let safe = [];
            let quarantined = [];

            for (let i = 0; i < sortedEntries.length; i++) {
                if (i < limit) {
                    safe.push(sortedEntries[i][0]);
                } else {
                    quarantined.push(sortedEntries[i][0]);
                }
            }

            return { safe: safe, quarantined: quarantined, supportedByWater: supportedByWater, manualLimit: manualLimit };
        }

        function getCropTimeMultiplier(cropName, plotObj, nowMs) {
            let multiplier = 1;
            let boosts = [];
            const seasonName = (SL_SEASON && SL_SEASON.season) || "spring";

            if (hasInventory("Seed Specialist")) {
                multiplier *= 0.9;
                boosts.push("Seed Specialist x0.9");
            }

            if (isCollectibleBuilt("Kuebiko")) {
                multiplier *= 0.85;
                boosts.push("Kuebiko x0.85");
            } else if (isCollectibleBuilt("Scarecrow")) {
                multiplier *= 0.85;
                boosts.push("Scarecrow x0.85");
            } else if (isCollectibleBuilt("Nancy")) {
                multiplier *= 0.85;
                boosts.push("Nancy x0.85");
            }

            if (isCollectibleBuilt("Lunar Calendar")) {
                multiplier *= 0.9;
                boosts.push("Lunar Calendar x0.9");
            }

            if (isTemporaryCollectibleActive("Super Totem")) {
                multiplier *= 0.5;
                boosts.push("Super Totem x0.5");
            } else if (isTemporaryCollectibleActive("Time Warp Totem")) {
                multiplier *= 0.5;
                boosts.push("Time Warp Totem x0.5");
            }

            if (isTemporaryCollectibleActive("Harvest Hourglass")) {
                multiplier *= 0.75;
                boosts.push("Harvest Hourglass x0.75");
            }

            if (hasSkill("Strong Roots") && ADVANCED_CROPS.has(cropName)) {
                multiplier *= 0.9;
                boosts.push("Strong Roots x0.9");
            }

            if (seasonName === "summer" && SUMMER_CROPS.has(cropName) && isWearableActive("Solflare Aegis")) {
                multiplier *= 0.5;
                boosts.push("Solflare Aegis x0.5");
            }

            if (seasonName === "autumn" && AUTUMN_CROPS.has(cropName) && isWearableActive("Autumn's Embrace")) {
                multiplier *= 0.5;
                boosts.push("Autumn's Embrace x0.5");
            }

            if (hasSkill("Green Thumb")) {
                multiplier *= 0.95;
                boosts.push("Green Thumb x0.95");
            }

            if (isBuffActive("Power hour")) {
                multiplier *= 0.5;
                boosts.push("Power hour x0.5");
            }

            if (cropName === "Parsnip" && isCollectibleBuilt("Mysterious Parsnip")) {
                multiplier *= 0.5;
                boosts.push("Mysterious Parsnip x0.5");
            }

            if (cropName === "Carrot" && isWearableActive("Carrot Amulet")) {
                multiplier *= 0.8;
                boosts.push("Carrot Amulet x0.8");
            }

            if (cropName === "Cabbage" && isCollectibleBuilt("Cabbage Girl")) {
                multiplier *= 0.5;
                boosts.push("Cabbage Girl x0.5");
            }

            if (cropName === "Eggplant" && isCollectibleBuilt("Obie")) {
                multiplier *= 0.75;
                boosts.push("Obie x0.75");
            }

            const basicScarecrowBoost = getBasicScarecrowBoost(cropName, plotObj);
            if (basicScarecrowBoost.active) {
                multiplier *= basicScarecrowBoost.multiplier;
                boosts.push(...basicScarecrowBoost.boosts);
            }

            return { multiplier: multiplier, boosts: boosts };
        }

        function getCropGrowTimeMs(cropName, plotObj, nowMs = Date.now()) {
            const learned = LEARNED_CROP_TIMES[cropName];
            const base = learned || BASE_CROP_TIMES[cropName] || 60000;
            const rule = getCropTimeMultiplier(cropName, plotObj, nowMs);
            return {
                ms: Math.max(0, Math.round(base * rule.multiplier)),
                baseMs: base,
                multiplier: rule.multiplier,
                boosts: rule.boosts
            };
        }

        function getCropReadyAt(plotObj, nowMs = Date.now()) {
            if (!plotObj || !plotObj.crop) {
                return 0;
            }

            const cropName = plotObj.crop.name;
            if (!cropName || (!BASE_CROP_TIMES[cropName] && !LEARNED_CROP_TIMES[cropName])) {
                return 0;
            }

            const readyAt = parseTimeValue(plotObj.crop.readyAt);
            if (readyAt > 0) {
                return readyAt;
            }

            const plantedAt = parseTimeValue(plotObj.crop.plantedAt);
            const learned = LEARNED_CROP_TIMES[cropName];
            const baseMs = learned || BASE_CROP_TIMES[cropName] || 0;

            return plantedAt > 0 && baseMs > 0 ? plantedAt + baseMs : 0;
        }

        function calculateSellPrice(itemName, basePrice, createdAt) {
            let nowMs = Date.now();
            if (createdAt) {
                let parsedCreatedAt = Date.parse(createdAt);
                if (Number.isFinite(parsedCreatedAt)) {
                    nowMs = parsedCreatedAt;
                }
            }

            let multiplier = 1;
            let boosts = [];

            if (readDecimal(SL_INVENTORY["Green Thumb"], 0) >= 1) {
                multiplier += 0.05;
                boosts.push("Green Thumb x1.05");
            }

            if (SL_CREATED_AT && SL_CREATED_AT + (2 * 60 * 60 * 1000) > nowMs) {
                multiplier += 1;
                boosts.push("2x Crop Shortage");
            }

            let eventMultiplier = getSpecialEventSaleMultiplier(itemName, nowMs);
            if (eventMultiplier) {
                multiplier += eventMultiplier - 1;
                boosts.push("Event x" + eventMultiplier);
            }

            if (hasSkill("Coin Swindler")) {
                multiplier += 0.10;
                boosts.push("Coin Swindler +0.10");
            }

            let price = basePrice * multiplier;
            return {
                price: parseFloat(price.toFixed(4)),
                rawPrice: price,
                multiplier: multiplier,
                boosts: boosts
            };
        }

        function getCookingTime(recipe, baseSeconds, buildingName, createdAt = Date.now()) {
            let seconds = Math.max(0, Number(baseSeconds || 0));
            let boosts = [];

            if (isWearableActive("Luna's Hat")) {
                seconds *= 0.5;
                boosts.push("Luna's Hat x0.5");
            }
            if (isWearableActive("Master Chef's Cleaver")) {
                seconds *= 0.85;
                boosts.push("Master Chef's Cleaver x0.85");
            }
            if (isTemporaryCollectibleActive("Legendary Shrine")) {
                seconds *= 0.5;
                boosts.push("Legendary Shrine x0.5");
            }
            if (isTemporaryCollectibleActive("Boar Shrine")) {
                seconds *= 0.8;
                boosts.push("Boar Shrine x0.8");
            }
            if (isTemporaryCollectibleActive("Super Totem")) {
                seconds *= 0.5;
                boosts.push("Super Totem x0.5");
            } else if (isTemporaryCollectibleActive("Time Warp Totem")) {
                seconds *= 0.5;
                boosts.push("Time Warp Totem x0.5");
            }
            if (isTemporaryCollectibleActive("Gourmet Hourglass")) {
                seconds *= 0.5;
                boosts.push("Gourmet Hourglass x0.5");
            }
            if (isCollectibleBuilt("Desert Gnome")) {
                seconds *= 0.9;
                boosts.push("Desert Gnome x0.9");
            }
            if ((buildingName === "Fire Pit" || buildingName === "Kitchen") && hasSkill("Fast Feasts")) {
                seconds *= 0.9;
                boosts.push("Fast Feasts x0.9");
            }
            if (String(recipe || "").includes("Cake") && hasSkill("Frosted Cakes")) {
                seconds *= 0.9;
                boosts.push("Frosted Cakes x0.9");
            }

            return { seconds: seconds, readyAt: createdAt + Math.round(seconds * 1000), boosts: boosts };
        }

        function hasObjectData(value) {
            return !!(value && typeof value === "object" && Object.keys(value).length > 0);
        }

        function hasActiveWeatherRisk() {
            if (!SL_CALENDAR || typeof SL_CALENDAR !== "object") {
                return false;
            }

            const weatherKeys = ["tornado", "tsunami", "greatFreeze"];
            for (let i = 0; i < weatherKeys.length; i++) {
                const item = SL_CALENDAR[weatherKeys[i]];
                if (item && item.triggeredAt && !item.protected) {
                    return true;
                }
            }
            return false;
        }

        function getUnsupportedAccountingReason() {
            if (hasActiveWeatherRisk()) {
                return "Aktif hava olayi tespit edildi. Client weather muhasebesi birebir port edilmeden bot durduruldu.";
            }

            const cropEntries = Object.entries(SL_CROPS || {});
            for (let i = 0; i < cropEntries.length; i++) {
                const plotId = cropEntries[i][0];
                const plot = cropEntries[i][1] || {};
                if (plot.fertiliser) {
                    return "Fertiliser kullanilan tarla var: " + plotId;
                }
                if (plot.beeSwarm) {
                    return "Bee swarm etkisi olan tarla var: " + plotId;
                }
                if (plot.crop && (plot.crop.amount !== undefined || plot.crop.reward !== undefined)) {
                    return "Hazir crop icinde onceden hesaplanmis amount/reward var: " + plotId;
                }
            }

            return null;
        }

        function resourceNames() {
            try {
                return performance.getEntriesByType("resource").map(function(x) { return x.name; });
            } catch(e) {
                return [];
            }
        }

        function stopForClientUpdate(reason) {
            killSwitchActivated = true;
            isBotRunning = false;
            stopRequested = true;
            const message = `<div style="margin:8px 0;padding:12px;border:2px solid #f97316;border-radius:10px;background:rgba(154,52,18,0.92);color:#fff7ed;font-weight:900;font-size:14px;line-height:1.45;text-align:center;box-shadow:0 0 18px rgba(249,115,22,0.35);">GAME UPDATED. NEXUS SAFETY STOPPED.<br>PLEASE REPORT TO NEXUS.<br><span style="font-size:11px;color:#fed7aa;">${reason}</span></div>`;
            log(message);
            const btn = document.getElementById('btn-start-auto');
            if (btn) {
                btn.innerText = "GAME UPDATED";
                btn.style.background = "linear-gradient(90deg,#ea580c,#f97316)";
                btn.disabled = true;
                btn.style.opacity = "0.85";
                btn.style.cursor = "not-allowed";
            }
        }

        async function auditClientContract() {
            const urls = resourceNames().filter(function(url) {
                return url.includes("/play/assets/") && url.includes(".js") && !url.includes("/Ph");
            }).slice(0, 12);

            let scanned = 0;
            const found = {};
            const markers = REQUIRED_CLIENT_MARKERS.concat(OPTIONAL_CLIENT_MARKERS);
            markers.forEach(function(marker) {
                found[marker] = false;
            });

            for (let i = 0; i < urls.length; i++) {
                try {
                    const text = await _window.fetch(urls[i]).then(function(r) { return r.text(); });
                    scanned++;
                    for (let j = 0; j < markers.length; j++) {
                        const marker = markers[j];
                        if (!found[marker] && text.includes(marker)) {
                            found[marker] = true;
                        }
                    }
                } catch(e) {
                    // Bir asset okunamazsa digerleriyle devam.
                }
            }

            if (scanned === 0) {
                return { ok: false, reason: "Client asset files could not be inspected." };
            }

            const missing = REQUIRED_CLIENT_MARKERS.filter(function(marker) {
                return !found[marker];
            });

            if (missing.length > 0) {
                return {
                    ok: false,
                    reason: "Critical client contract marker missing: " + missing.slice(0, 4).join(", ")
                };
            }

            return { ok: true };
        }

        async function buildClientFingerprint() {
            const audit = await auditClientContract();
            return audit.ok ? "critical-client-contract-ok-v1" : null;
        }

        async function ensureClientRulesSafe() {
            if (lastAuditOk) {
                return true;
            }
            if (auditPromise) {
                return auditPromise;
            }

            auditPromise = (async function() {
                const audit = await auditClientContract();
                if (!audit.ok) {
                    stopForClientUpdate(audit.reason || "Critical client autosave/header contract changed.");
                    return false;
                }

                try {
                    localStorage.removeItem(RULE_STORAGE_KEY);
                } catch(e) {}

                lastAuditOk = true;
                return true;

                const fingerprint = await buildClientFingerprint();
                if (!fingerprint) {
                    stopForClientUpdate("Client autosave/header signature could not be verified.");
                    return false;
                    log("âš ï¸ [GameRules] Client kural imzasÄ± okunamadÄ±; mevcut yerel kurallarla devam ediliyor.");
                    lastAuditOk = true;
                    return true;
                }

                const saved = localStorage.getItem(RULE_STORAGE_KEY);
                if (!saved) {
                    localStorage.setItem(RULE_STORAGE_KEY, fingerprint);
                    log("ğŸ§  [GameRules] Client kural imzasÄ± Ã¶ÄŸrenildi. Bundan sonra deÄŸiÅŸirse bot gÃ¼venlik iÃ§in duracak.");
                    lastAuditOk = true;
                    return true;
                }

                if (saved !== fingerprint) {
                    stopForClientUpdate("Autosave/header/action signature changed.");
                    return false;
                    triggerKillSwitch("Oyun GÃ¼ncellenmiÅŸ. GÃ¼venlik iÃ§in durduruldu.", "CLIENT_RULES_CHANGED");
                    return false;
                }

                lastAuditOk = true;
                return true;
            })();

            return auditPromise;
        }

        return {
            ensureClientRulesSafe: ensureClientRulesSafe,
            getSafeAndQuarantinedPlots: getSafeAndQuarantinedPlotsByRules,
            getSupportedPlotCount: getSupportedPlotCount,
            getWaterCapacityInfo: getWaterCapacityInfo,
            getCropReadyAt: getCropReadyAt,
            getCropGrowTimeMs: getCropGrowTimeMs,
            getBasicScarecrowBoost: getBasicScarecrowBoost,
            calculateSellPrice: calculateSellPrice,
            getCookingTime: getCookingTime,
            getUnsupportedAccountingReason: getUnsupportedAccountingReason,
            isWearableActive: isWearableActive,
            isCollectibleBuilt: isCollectibleBuilt,
            getCurrentBumpkinLevel: getCurrentBumpkinLevel,
            getCurrentBumpkinLevelProgress: getCurrentBumpkinLevelProgress,
            getSeedLevelRequirement: getSeedLevelRequirement,
            canBuySeed: canBuySeed,
            getCurrentSeason: getCurrentSeason,
            canRestockShipment: canRestockShipment,
            getNextShipmentText: getNextShipmentText,
            isSeedInCurrentSeason: isSeedInCurrentSeason,
            getVisibleMarketSeeds: getVisibleMarketSeeds,
            hasSkill: hasSkill
        };
    })();

    async function computeSHA256(data) {
        let str;
        if (typeof data === 'string') {
            str = data;
        } else {
            str = JSON.stringify(data);
        }
        const buffer = new TextEncoder().encode(str);
        const hashBuffer = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', buffer);
        const hashArray = Array.from(new Uint8Array(hashBuffer));

        let hashString = "sha256:";
        let hexMap = hashArray.map(function(b) {
            return b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0');
        });

        hashString += hexMap.join('');
        return hashString;
    }

    function modifyInventory(item, amount) {
        let currentString = SL_INVENTORY[item] || "0";
        let current = parseFloat(currentString);
        let newAmount = current + amount;

        if (newAmount <= 0) {
            delete SL_INVENTORY[item];
        } else {
            SL_INVENTORY[item] = newAmount.toString();
        }
        localStorage.setItem('sl_inventory_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_INVENTORY));
    }

    function modifyActivity(activityName, amount) {
        let currentString = SL_FARM_ACTIVITY[activityName] || 0;
        let current = parseFloat(currentString);
        let newAmount = current + amount;

        SL_FARM_ACTIVITY[activityName] = newAmount;
        localStorage.setItem('sl_activity_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY));
    }

    function modifyStock(item, amount) {
        let currentString = SL_STOCK[item] || "0";
        let current = parseInt(currentString);
        let newAmount = current + amount;

        if (newAmount < 0) {
            newAmount = 0;
        }

        SL_STOCK[item] = newAmount.toString();
        localStorage.setItem('sl_stock_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_STOCK));
    }

    function normalizeBotSettings(raw) {
        let src;
        if (raw && typeof raw === 'object') {
            src = raw;
        } else {
            src = {};
        }

        return {
            harvestMin: Math.max(100, parseInt(src.harvestMin ?? DEFAULT_BOT_SETTINGS.harvestMin) || DEFAULT_BOT_SETTINGS.harvestMin),
            harvestMax: Math.max(100, parseInt(src.harvestMax ?? DEFAULT_BOT_SETTINGS.harvestMax) || DEFAULT_BOT_SETTINGS.harvestMax),
            plantMin: Math.max(100, parseInt(src.plantMin ?? DEFAULT_BOT_SETTINGS.plantMin) || DEFAULT_BOT_SETTINGS.plantMin),
            plantMax: Math.max(100, parseInt(src.plantMax ?? DEFAULT_BOT_SETTINGS.plantMax) || DEFAULT_BOT_SETTINGS.plantMax),
            taskSwitchMin: Math.max(100, parseInt(src.taskSwitchMin ?? DEFAULT_BOT_SETTINGS.taskSwitchMin) || DEFAULT_BOT_SETTINGS.taskSwitchMin),
            taskSwitchMax: Math.max(100, parseInt(src.taskSwitchMax ?? DEFAULT_BOT_SETTINGS.taskSwitchMax) || DEFAULT_BOT_SETTINGS.taskSwitchMax),
            autoFields: src.autoFields === undefined ? true : !!src.autoFields,
            autoTree: !!src.autoTree,
            autoCraftAxe: !!src.autoCraftAxe,
            autoMine: !!src.autoMine,
            autoCraftPick: !!src.autoCraftPick,
            autoMineStone: !!(src.autoMineStone ?? src.autoMine),
            autoMineIron: !!(src.autoMineIron ?? src.autoMine),
            autoMineGold: !!(src.autoMineGold ?? src.autoMine),
            autoCraftPickaxe: !!(src.autoCraftPickaxe ?? src.autoCraftPick),
            autoCraftStonePick: !!(src.autoCraftStonePick ?? src.autoCraftPick),
            autoCraftIronPick: !!(src.autoCraftIronPick ?? src.autoCraftPick),
            autoMushroom: !!src.autoMushroom,
            autoFishing: !!src.autoFishing,
            autoDigging: !!src.autoDigging
        };
    }

    const NEXUS_ICON_CACHE = {};

    function normalizeAssetKey(value) {
        return String(value || "").toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, "");
    }

    function escapeIconAttr(value) {
        return String(value === undefined || value === null ? "" : value)
            .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
            .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
            .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
            .replace(/"/g, "&quot;");
    }

    function getItemAssetSlug(name) {
        return String(name || "")
            .replace(/\s+Seed$/i, "")
            .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/gi, "_")
            .replace(/^_+|_+$/g, "")
            .toLowerCase();
    }

    function getItemIconCandidates() {
        const urls = [];
        try {
            document.querySelectorAll('img[src], source[src], image[href]').forEach(function(el) {
                const src = el.getAttribute('src') || el.getAttribute('href');
                if (src) {
                    const label = [
                        el.getAttribute('alt'),
                        el.getAttribute('title'),
                        el.getAttribute('aria-label'),
                        el.closest('[aria-label]') && el.closest('[aria-label]').getAttribute('aria-label'),
                        el.closest('[title]') && el.closest('[title]').getAttribute('title'),
                        el.parentElement && el.parentElement.textContent
                    ].filter(Boolean).join(" ");
                    urls.push({ src: src, key: normalizeAssetKey(src + " " + label) });
                }
            });
        } catch(e) {}

        try {
            performance.getEntriesByType("resource").forEach(function(entry) {
                if (entry && entry.name && /\.(png|webp|gif|jpg|jpeg)(\?|$)|^data:image\//i.test(entry.name)) {
                    urls.push({ src: entry.name, key: normalizeAssetKey(entry.name) });
                }
            });
        } catch(e) {}

        const seen = {};
        return urls.filter(function(item) {
            if (!item || !item.src || seen[item.src]) {
                return false;
            }
            seen[item.src] = true;
            return true;
        });
    }

    function getKnownGameAssetIcon(name) {
        if (NEXUS_ICON_ASSET_HINTS[name]) {
            return NEXUS_ICON_ASSET_HINTS[name];
        }
        const slug = getItemAssetSlug(name);
        if (!slug) {
            return "";
        }
        if (String(name || "").endsWith(" Seed")) {
            return `https://sunflower-land.com/game-assets/crops/${slug}/seed.png`;
        }
        if (KNOWN_CROPS.includes(name)) {
            return `https://sunflower-land.com/game-assets/crops/${slug}/plant.png`;
        }
        if (FISH_FEED_ITEMS[name]) {
            return `https://sunflower-land.com/game-assets/fish/${slug}.png`;
        }
        if (String(name || "").includes("Mushroom")) {
            return `https://sunflower-land.com/game-assets/resources/${slug}.png`;
        }
        return "";
    }

    function getItemIconSrc(name) {
        if (!name) {
            return "";
        }
        if (NEXUS_ICON_CACHE[name] !== undefined) {
            return NEXUS_ICON_CACHE[name];
        }

        const key = normalizeAssetKey(name);
        const candidates = getItemIconCandidates();
        for (let i = 0; i < candidates.length; i++) {
            const item = candidates[i];
            if (item.key.includes(key)) {
                NEXUS_ICON_CACHE[name] = item.src;
                return item.src;
            }
        }

        const hinted = getKnownGameAssetIcon(name);
        NEXUS_ICON_CACHE[name] = hinted || "";
        return NEXUS_ICON_CACHE[name];
    }

    function getFishIconSrc(name) {
        return FISH_FEED_ITEMS[name] ? getItemIconSrc(name) : "";
    }

    function getIconWarmNames(extraNames) {
        const names = {};
        (extraNames || []).forEach(function(name) {
            if (name) names[name] = true;
        });
        try {
            KNOWN_CROPS.forEach(function(name) { names[name] = true; });
            ALL_KNOWN_SEEDS.forEach(function(name) { names[name] = true; });
            (FISHING_BAITS || []).forEach(function(name) { names[name] = true; });
            Object.keys(FISH_FEED_ITEMS || {}).forEach(function(name) { names[name] = true; });
            Object.keys(FIRE_PIT_RECIPES || {}).forEach(function(name) { names[name] = true; });
            Object.keys(TREASURE_TOOL_RULES || {}).forEach(function(name) { names[name] = true; });
            Object.keys(DIGGING_SELL_PRICES || {}).forEach(function(name) { names[name] = true; });
            Object.keys(NEXUS_ICON_ASSET_HINTS).forEach(function(name) { names[name] = true; });
        } catch(e) {}
        return Object.keys(names);
    }

    async function warmNexusIconsFromClientAssets(extraNames) {
        if (nexusIconAssetScanStarted) {
            return;
        }
        nexusIconAssetScanStarted = true;

        let urls = [];
        try {
            urls = performance.getEntriesByType("resource").map(function(entry) {
                return entry.name;
            }).filter(function(url) {
                return url.includes("/play/assets/") && url.includes(".js") && !url.includes("/Ph");
            }).slice(0, 10);
        } catch(e) {
            urls = [];
        }

        const itemNames = getIconWarmNames(extraNames);
        for (let i = 0; i < urls.length; i++) {
            try {
                const text = await _window.fetch(urls[i]).then(function(res) { return res.text(); });
                for (let j = 0; j < itemNames.length; j++) {
                    const name = itemNames[j];
                    if (NEXUS_ICON_CACHE[name] && /^data:image\//.test(NEXUS_ICON_CACHE[name])) {
                        continue;
                    }
                    const key = normalizeAssetKey(name);
                    let index = text.indexOf(name);
                    if (index < 0) index = text.indexOf("fish." + key);
                    if (index < 0) index = text.indexOf("tools." + key);
                    if (index < 0) index = text.indexOf("resources." + key);
                    if (index < 0) {
                        continue;
                    }
                    const windowText = text.slice(Math.max(0, index - 25000), Math.min(text.length, index + 25000));
                    const imageMatch = windowText.match(/data:image\/(?:png|webp|gif|jpeg);base64,[A-Za-z0-9+/=]+/);
                    if (imageMatch) {
                        NEXUS_ICON_CACHE[name] = imageMatch[0];
                    }
                }
            } catch(e) {}
        }

        if (document.getElementById('sl-character-menu') && document.getElementById('sl-character-menu').style.display !== 'none') {
            renderCharacterMenu();
        }
        if (document.getElementById('tab-buy')) {
            renderMarketTabs();
        }
        if (document.getElementById('fire-pit-recipes')) {
            renderCookingMenu();
        }
        if (document.getElementById('fishing-bait-grid')) {
            renderFishingMenu();
        }
        if (document.getElementById('digging-grid')) {
            renderDiggingMenu();
        }
    }

    async function warmFishIconsFromClientAssets() {
        return warmNexusIconsFromClientAssets(Object.keys(FISH_FEED_ITEMS || {}));
    }

    function getItemIconHtml(name, size = 26, extraStyle = "") {
        const src = getItemIconSrc(name);
        const box = Math.max(16, parseInt(size, 10) || 26);
        const safeName = escapeIconAttr(name);
        const safeStyle = escapeIconAttr(extraStyle);
        if (!src) {
            return `<span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;width:${box}px;height:${box}px;${safeStyle}"></span>`;
        }
        return `<span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;width:${box}px;height:${box}px;vertical-align:middle;${safeStyle}"><img src="${escapeIconAttr(src)}" alt="${safeName}" style="width:${box}px;height:${box}px;object-fit:contain;image-rendering:pixelated;filter:drop-shadow(0 2px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.35));" onerror="this.style.display='none';this.nextElementSibling.style.display='inline-flex';"><span style="display:none;align-items:center;justify-content:center;width:${box}px;height:${box}px;"></span></span>`;
    }

    function getCharacterFeedIconHtml(name) {
        return getItemIconHtml(name, 34);
    }

    function getTreasureToolRule(tool) {
        return TREASURE_TOOL_RULES[tool] || null;
    }

    function canBuyTreasureTool(tool) {
        const rule = getTreasureToolRule(tool);
        if (!rule) {
            return { ok: false, reason: "Unknown tool" };
        }
        if (getAvailableStock(tool) <= 0) {
            return { ok: false, reason: "Out of stock" };
        }
        if (SL_COINS < rule.price) {
            return { ok: false, reason: "Insufficient coins" };
        }
        const ingredients = rule.ingredients || {};
        for (const item in ingredients) {
            if (readDecimal(SL_INVENTORY[item], 0) < ingredients[item]) {
                return { ok: false, reason: `Need ${ingredients[item]} ${item}` };
            }
        }
        return { ok: true, reason: "Ready" };
    }

    function getDiggingSellItems() {
        return Object.keys(DIGGING_SELL_PRICES).filter(function(item) {
            return readDecimal(SL_INVENTORY[item], 0) > 0;
        });
    }

    function getDiggingBuyConfig(tool) {
        DIGGING_SETTINGS.buy = DIGGING_SETTINGS.buy || {};
        DIGGING_SETTINGS.buy[tool] = DIGGING_SETTINGS.buy[tool] || { active: false, target: 0 };
        return DIGGING_SETTINGS.buy[tool];
    }

    function getDiggingBuyTarget(tool) {
        const cfg = getDiggingBuyConfig(tool);
        const value = parseInt(cfg.target || 0, 10) || 0;
        return Math.max(0, value);
    }

    function hasDiggingBuyTargetLeft(tool) {
        const cfg = getDiggingBuyConfig(tool);
        const target = getDiggingBuyTarget(tool);
        return !!cfg.active && target > 0 && getInventoryAmount(tool) < target;
    }

    function getNextDiggingToolToBuy() {
        const tools = Object.keys(TREASURE_TOOL_RULES);
        for (let i = 0; i < tools.length; i++) {
            const tool = tools[i];
            if (hasDiggingBuyTargetLeft(tool) && canBuyTreasureTool(tool).ok) {
                return tool;
            }
        }
        return null;
    }

    function getTodayKey() {
        return new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];
    }

    function getDailyFishingLimit() {
        let limit = 20;
        let boosts = [];
        if (SL_BUMPKIN && SL_BUMPKIN.equipped && SL_BUMPKIN.equipped.pants === "Angler Waders") {
            limit += 10;
            boosts.push("Angler Waders +10");
        }
        ["Reelmaster's Chair", "Nautilus", "Deep Sea Slug"].forEach(function(name) {
            if (GameRules && GameRules.isCollectibleBuilt && GameRules.isCollectibleBuilt(name)) {
                limit += 5;
                boosts.push(name + " +5");
            }
        });
        if (SL_BUMPKIN && SL_BUMPKIN.skills) {
            if (SL_BUMPKIN.skills["Fisherman's 5 Fold"]) {
                limit += 5;
                boosts.push("Fisherman's 5 Fold +5");
            }
            if (SL_BUMPKIN.skills["Fisherman's 10 Fold"]) {
                limit += 10;
                boosts.push("Fisherman's 10 Fold +10");
            }
            if (SL_BUMPKIN.skills["More With Less"]) {
                limit += 10;
                boosts.push("More With Less +10");
            }
        }
        if (SL_BUMPKIN && SL_BUMPKIN.equipped && SL_BUMPKIN.equipped.tool === "Saw Fish") {
            limit += 5;
            boosts.push("Saw Fish +5");
        }
        return { limit: limit, boosts: boosts };
    }

    function getFishingAttemptsUsed() {
        const today = getTodayKey();
        return parseInt((SL_FISHING.dailyAttempts && SL_FISHING.dailyAttempts[today]) || 0, 10) || 0;
    }

    function getFishingReelsLeft() {
        const info = getDailyFishingLimit();
        const extra = parseInt(SL_FISHING.extraReels && SL_FISHING.extraReels.count || 0, 10) || 0;
        return Math.max(0, info.limit - getFishingAttemptsUsed()) + extra;
    }

    function getFishingRodCost(multiplier) {
        if (SL_BUMPKIN && SL_BUMPKIN.equipped && SL_BUMPKIN.equipped.tool === "Ancient Rod") {
            return 0;
        }
        return Math.max(1, parseInt(multiplier || 1, 10) || 1);
    }

    function getSelectedFishingBaits() {
        const selected = FISHING_SETTINGS.selected || {};
        return FISHING_BAITS.filter(function(bait) {
            return !!selected[bait];
        });
    }

    function getFishingBaitTarget(bait) {
        FISHING_SETTINGS.targets = FISHING_SETTINGS.targets || {};
        const value = parseInt(FISHING_SETTINGS.targets[bait] || 0, 10) || 0;
        return Math.max(0, value);
    }

    function getFishingBaitCasted(bait) {
        FISHING_SETTINGS.casted = FISHING_SETTINGS.casted || {};
        const value = parseInt(FISHING_SETTINGS.casted[bait] || 0, 10) || 0;
        return Math.max(0, value);
    }

    function hasFishingBaitTargetLeft(bait) {
        const target = getFishingBaitTarget(bait);
        if (target <= 0) {
            return true;
        }
        return getFishingBaitCasted(bait) < target;
    }

    function recordFishingBaitCast(bait) {
        FISHING_SETTINGS.casted = FISHING_SETTINGS.casted || {};
        FISHING_SETTINGS.casted[bait] = getFishingBaitCasted(bait) + 1;
        saveFishingSettings();
    }

    function getNextFishingBait() {
        const selected = getSelectedFishingBaits();
        if (selected.length === 0) {
            return null;
        }

        let start = parseInt(FISHING_SETTINGS.nextIndex || 0, 10) || 0;
        for (let i = 0; i < selected.length; i++) {
            const idx = (start + i) % selected.length;
            const bait = selected[idx];
            if (hasFishingBaitTargetLeft(bait) && readDecimal(SL_INVENTORY[bait], 0) >= 1) {
                FISHING_SETTINGS.nextIndex = (idx + 1) % selected.length;
                saveFishingSettings();
                return bait;
            }
        }
        return null;
    }

    function recordFishingCatch(caught) {
        if (!caught || typeof caught !== 'object') {
            return;
        }
        Object.keys(caught).forEach(function(name) {
            const amount = parseFloat(caught[name] || 0);
            if (amount > 0) {
                FISHING_CATCH_LOG[name] = (FISHING_CATCH_LOG[name] || 0) + amount;
            }
        });
        saveFishingLog();
    }

    _window.toggleFishingBait = function(bait) {
        FISHING_SETTINGS.selected = FISHING_SETTINGS.selected || {};
        FISHING_SETTINGS.selected[bait] = !FISHING_SETTINGS.selected[bait];
        saveFishingSettings();
        renderFishingMenu();
    };

    _window.setFishingBaitTarget = function(bait) {
        FISHING_SETTINGS.targets = FISHING_SETTINGS.targets || {};
        FISHING_SETTINGS.casted = FISHING_SETTINGS.casted || {};
        const current = getFishingBaitTarget(bait);
        _window.openNexusNumberModal({
            title: `Target casts for ${bait}`,
            description: '0 means unlimited. Bot will stop using this bait after the target.',
            value: current > 0 ? current : '',
            onApply: function(parsed) {
                if (parsed > 0) {
                    FISHING_SETTINGS.targets[bait] = parsed;
                } else {
                    delete FISHING_SETTINGS.targets[bait];
                }
                if (getFishingBaitCasted(bait) > parsed && parsed > 0) {
                    FISHING_SETTINGS.casted[bait] = parsed;
                }
                saveFishingSettings();
                renderFishingMenu();
            }
        });
    };

    function getResourceSelection(type) {
        if (!RESOURCE_SELECTIONS[type]) {
            RESOURCE_SELECTIONS[type] = {};
        }
        return RESOURCE_SELECTIONS[type];
    }

    function isResourceSelected(type, id) {
        return !!getResourceSelection(type)[id];
    }

    function getSelectedResourceEntries(type, source) {
        let selected = getResourceSelection(type);
        return Object.entries(source || {}).filter(([id]) => !!selected[id]);
    }

    function toggleResourceSelection(type, id) {
        let selected = getResourceSelection(type);
        if (selected[id]) {
            delete selected[id];
        } else {
            selected[id] = true;
        }
        saveResourceSelections();
        renderForestAndMines();
    }

    function normalizeMarketSettings(raw) {
        const base = { sell: {}, buy: {} };
        if (!raw || typeof raw !== 'object') {
            return base;
        }

        if (Array.isArray(raw.sell)) {
            raw.sell.forEach(function(crop) {
                base.sell[crop] = { active: true, minEnabled: false, min: 1 };
            });
        } else if (raw.sell && typeof raw.sell === 'object') {
            Object.entries(raw.sell).forEach(function([crop, cfg]) {
                if (cfg === true) {
                    base.sell[crop] = { active: true, minEnabled: false, min: 1 };
                } else {
                    let minVal = Math.max(1, parseInt(cfg?.min ?? 1) || 1);
                    base.sell[crop] = { active: !!cfg?.active, minEnabled: !!cfg?.minEnabled, min: minVal };
                }
            });
        }

        if (raw.buy && typeof raw.buy === 'object') {
            Object.entries(raw.buy).forEach(function([seed, cfg]) {
                if (typeof cfg === 'number') {
                    let safeVal = Math.max(1, cfg);
                    base.buy[seed] = { active: true, min: safeVal, max: safeVal, ignoreStockLimit: false, autoShipmentRestock: false };
                } else {
                    let minVal = Math.max(1, parseInt(cfg?.min ?? 10) || 10);
                    let maxVal = Math.max(minVal, parseInt(cfg?.max ?? minVal) || minVal);
                    base.buy[seed] = { active: !!cfg?.active, min: minVal, max: maxVal, ignoreStockLimit: !!cfg?.ignoreStockLimit, autoShipmentRestock: !!cfg?.autoShipmentRestock };
                }
            });
        }
        return base;
    }

    let selectedBuySeed = localStorage.getItem('sl_selected_buy_seed') || "";

    function normalizeCookingSettings(raw) {

    }

    function normalizeCharacterSettings(raw) {
        const base = { auto: false, tab: "foods", selected: {} };

    function saveMasterHeaders() {
        if (!masterHeaders) {
            return;
        }

        localStorage.setItem('sl_master_headers', JSON.stringify(masterHeaders));
    }

    function rememberMasterHeaders(headers) {
        if (!headers) {
            return;
        }

        if (!masterHeaders) {
            masterHeaders = {};
        }

        Object.keys(headers).forEach(function(key) {
            setHeaderValue(masterHeaders, key, headers[key]);
        });

        let liveTtl = getLiveAmzTtl();
        if (liveTtl) {
            setHeaderValue(masterHeaders, 'x-amz-ttl', liveTtl);
        }

        saveMasterHeaders();
    }

    function findHeaderKey(headers, wantedKey) {
        if (!headers) {
            return null;
        }

        let lowerWanted = wantedKey.toLowerCase();
        let keys = Object.keys(headers);
        for (let i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
            if (keys[i].toLowerCase() === lowerWanted) {
                return keys[i];
            }
        }
        return null;
    }

    function setHeaderValue(headers, key, value) {
        if (!headers || value === undefined || value === null || value === '') {
            return;
        }

        let lowerWanted = key.toLowerCase();
        Object.keys(headers).forEach(function(existingKey) {
            if (existingKey.toLowerCase() === lowerWanted) {
                delete headers[existingKey];
            }
        });
        headers[key] = value;
    }

    function isUsableHeaderValue(value) {
        if (value === undefined || value === null || value === '') {
            return false;
        }

        let stringValue = String(value).toLowerCase();
        return stringValue !== 'undefined' && stringValue !== 'null';
    }

    function makeTransactionId() {
        return Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 9);
    }

    function getLiveAmzTtl() {
        try {
            return _window['x-amz-ttl'] || window['x-amz-ttl'] || null;
        } catch(e) {
            return null;
        }
    }

    function makeBotHeaders() {
        if (!masterHeaders) {
            return masterHeaders;
        }

        let headers = {};
        const safeHeaderNames = ['accept', 'authorization', 'content-type', 'x-amz-ttl', 'x-fingerprint'];
        safeHeaderNames.forEach(function(headerName) {
            const sourceKey = findHeaderKey(masterHeaders, headerName);
            let value = sourceKey ? masterHeaders[sourceKey] : null;
            if (isUsableHeaderValue(value)) {
                setHeaderValue(headers, headerName, value);
            }
        });

        if (!findHeaderKey(headers, 'accept')) {
            setHeaderValue(headers, 'accept', '*/*');
        }
        if (!findHeaderKey(headers, 'content-type')) {
            setHeaderValue(headers, 'content-type', 'application/json;charset=UTF-8');
        }

        let liveTtl = getLiveAmzTtl();
        if (liveTtl) {
            setHeaderValue(headers, 'x-amz-ttl', liveTtl);
            setHeaderValue(masterHeaders, 'x-amz-ttl', liveTtl);
            saveMasterHeaders();
        }

        setHeaderValue(headers, 'x-transaction-id', makeTransactionId());

        return headers;
    }

    function runFarmHashTTL(farmHash) {
        if (!farmHash || typeof farmHash !== 'string') {
            return;
        }

        try {
            let source = atob(farmHash);
            let bufferShim = {
                from: function(value) {
                    return {
                        toString: function(format) {
                            if (format === 'base64') {
                                return btoa(String(value));
                            }
                            return String(value);
                        }
                    };
                }
            };

            let runner = _window.Function('Buffer', source);
            runner(bufferShim);

            let liveTtl = getLiveAmzTtl();
            if (liveTtl && masterHeaders) {
                setHeaderValue(masterHeaders, 'x-amz-ttl', liveTtl);
                saveMasterHeaders();
            }
        } catch(e) {
            // Dynamic TTL script failed; keep last known headers.
        }
    }

        document.getElementById('btn-hide-main-menu').onclick = function() {
            const mainMenu = document.getElementById('sl-main-menu');

        document.getElementById('sl-mini-launcher').onclick = function() {
            const mainMenu = document.getElementById('sl-main-menu');
            const miniLauncher = document.getElementById('sl-mini-launcher');
            if (mainMenu) mainMenu.style.display = 'block';
            if (miniLauncher) miniLauncher.style.display = 'none';
            localStorage.setItem('sl_main_menu_hidden', '0');
        };
        let nexusNumberModalApply = null;
        _window.openNexusNumberModal = function(options) {
            const modal = document.getElementById('nexus-number-modal');
            const title = document.getElementById('nexus-number-title');
            const sub = document.getElementById('nexus-number-sub');
            const input = document.getElementById('nexus-number-input');
            if (!modal || !title || !sub || !input) return;
            title.textContent = (options && options.title) || 'Set Target';
            sub.textContent = (options && options.description) || '0 means unlimited.';
            input.value = (options && options.value !== undefined && options.value !== null) ? String(options.value) : '';
            nexusNumberModalApply = typeof options.onApply === 'function' ? options.onApply : null;
            modal.style.display = 'flex';
            setTimeout(function() {
                input.focus();
                input.select();
            }, 30);
        };
        _window.closeNexusNumberModal = function() {
            const modal = document.getElementById('nexus-number-modal');
            if (modal) modal.style.display = 'none';
            nexusNumberModalApply = null;
        };
        document.getElementById('nexus-number-cancel').onclick = function() {
            _window.closeNexusNumberModal();
        };
        document.getElementById('nexus-number-save').onclick = function() {
            const input = document.getElementById('nexus-number-input');
            const parsed = Math.max(0, parseInt(input ? input.value : 0, 10) || 0);
            const apply = nexusNumberModalApply;
            _window.closeNexusNumberModal();
            if (apply) apply(parsed);
        };
        document.getElementById('nexus-number-modal').onclick = function(e) {
            if (e.target && e.target.id === 'nexus-number-modal') {
                _window.closeNexusNumberModal();
            }
        };
        document.getElementById('nexus-number-input').onkeydown = function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') {
                document.getElementById('nexus-number-save').click();
            }
            if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                _window.closeNexusNumberModal();
            }
        };
        document.getElementById('btn-close-settings').onclick = function() {
            document.getElementById('sl-settings-menu').style.display = 'none';
        };

        document.getElementById('btn-save-settings').onclick = function() {
            let rawObject = {
                harvestMin: Math.round(parseFloat(document.getElementById('set-harvest-min').value || 0) * 1000),
                harvestMax: Math.round(parseFloat(document.getElementById('set-harvest-max').value || 0) * 1000),

    function cleanLogMessage(msg) {
        let text = String(msg || "");
        const replacements = [
            ["â†’", "->"],
            ["Â·", "-"],
            ["âœ…", ""],
            ["âš ï¸", "Warning:"],
            ["â³", ""],
            ["â¸ï¸", ""],
            ["ğŸŒ¾", ""],
            ["ğŸ“¦", ""],
            ["ğŸ”„", ""],
            ["ğŸ›’", ""],
            ["ğŸ§ ", ""],
            ["Ä°ÅŸlem BaÅŸarÄ±lÄ±!", "Operation successful!"],
            ["Ä°ÅŸlem arasÄ± bekleme", "Task wait"],
            ["SÄ±radaki iÅŸe hazÄ±rlanÄ±yor", "Preparing next task"],
            ["GÃ¶rev geÃ§iÅŸi", "Task switch"],
            ["KÄ±sa kontrol molasÄ±", "Short control break"],
            ["AlÄ±m paketi fÄ±rlatÄ±lÄ±yor", "Sending buy package"],
            ["Hasat sepeti fÄ±rlatÄ±lÄ±yor", "Sending harvest package"],
            ["Ekim sepeti fÄ±rlatÄ±lÄ±yor", "Sending plant package"],
            ["Ekim muhasebesi hazÄ±rlanÄ±yor", "Preparing plant accounting"],
            ["AlÄ±ÅŸ hesabÄ± response ile uyuÅŸuyor", "Buy accounting matches response"],
            ["satÄ±ÅŸ fiyatÄ± canlÄ± gÃ¼ncellendi", "sell price updated from live response"],
            ["alÄ±ÅŸ fiyatÄ± canlÄ± gÃ¼ncellendi", "buy price updated from live response"],
            ["Ã–ÄŸrenim", "Learning"],
            ["ÖÄŸrenim", "Learning"],
            ["Fiyat Kontrol", "Price Check"],
            ["Toplu Paket", "Batch"],
            ["Hasat", "Harvest"],
            ["Ekim", "Plant"],
            ["AlÄ±m", "Buy"],
            ["SatÄ±ÅŸ", "Sell"],
            ["alÄ±ÅŸ", "buy"],
            ["satÄ±ÅŸ", "sell"],
            ["hasat", "harvest"],
            ["ekim", "plant"],
            ["karakter", "character"],
            ["tur tamamlandÄ±", "round complete"],
            ["baÅŸarÄ±lÄ±", "successful"],
            ["canlÄ±", "live"],
            ["gÃ¼ncellendi", "updated"],
            ["hazÄ±r", "ready"],
            ["bekleniyor", "waiting"],
            ["fÄ±rlatÄ±lÄ±yor", "sending"],
            ["eylem", "actions"],
            ["tohum", "seeds"]
        ];
        replacements.forEach(function(pair) {
            text = text.split(pair[0]).join(pair[1]);
        });
        text = text.replace(/[\u0080-\uFFFF]/g, "");
        text = text.replace(/[^\x09\x0A\x0D\x20-\x7E]/g, "");
        text = text.replace(/\s{2,}/g, " ");
        text = text.replace(/>\s+/g, ">").replace(/\s+</g, "<");
        return text.trim();
    }

    function log(msg) {
        const logger = document.getElementById('sl-logger');
        if(!logger) return;

        const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('tr-TR', {hour12:false});
        let formattedMessage = `<p style="margin:0 0 6px 0; line-height:1.45;">[${time}] ${cleanLogMessage(msg)}</p>`;

        logger.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', formattedMessage);
        logger.scrollTop = logger.scrollHeight;
    }

    function makeDraggable(id) {
        const el = document.getElementById(id);
        const header = el.querySelector('.win-header');
        if(!header) return;

        header.onmousedown = function(e) {
            if(e.target.tagName === 'BUTTON' || e.target.tagName === 'INPUT') return;

            let sx = e.clientX - el.offsetLeft;
            let sy = e.clientY - el.offsetTop;

            document.onmousemove = function(ev) {
                el.style.left = (ev.clientX - sx) + 'px';
                el.style.top = (ev.clientY - sy) + 'px';
            };
            document.onmouseup = function() {
                document.onmousemove = null;
            };
        };
    }

    function sleep(ms) {
        return new Promise(function(resolve) {
            setTimeout(resolve, ms);
        });
    }

    function randInt(min, max) {
        let diff = max - min + 1;
        let rnd = Math.random() * diff;
        return Math.floor(rnd) + min;
    }

    function getHumanBatchPlantDelay(lastSeed, targetSeed, plantCount) {
        let delay = randInt(320, 720);

        if (lastSeed && lastSeed !== targetSeed) {
            delay += randInt(250, 700);
        }

        if (plantCount > 0 && plantCount % randInt(8, 12) === 0) {
            delay += randInt(300, 900);
        }

        if (Math.random() < 0.04) {
            delay += randInt(180, 600);
        }

        return delay;
    }

    function shuffleArray(items) {
        let arr = items.slice();
        for (let i = arr.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
            let j = randInt(0, i);
            let tmp = arr[i];
            arr[i] = arr[j];
            arr[j] = tmp;
        }
        return arr;
    }

    function renderSettingsMenu() {
        if (document.getElementById('set-harvest-min')) { document.getElementById('set-harvest-min').value = (BOT_SETTINGS.harvestMin / 1000).toFixed(1); }
        if (document.getElementById('set-harvest-max')) { document.getElementById('set-harvest-max').value = (BOT_SETTINGS.harvestMax / 1000).toFixed(1); }
        if (document.getElementById('set-plant-min')) { document.getElementById('set-plant-min').value = (BOT_SETTINGS.plantMin / 1000).toFixed(1); }
        if (document.getElementById('set-plant-max')) { document.getElementById('set-plant-max').value = (BOT_SETTINGS.plantMax / 1000).toFixed(1); }
        if (document.getElementById('set-task-switch-min')) { document.getElementById('set-task-switch-min').value = (BOT_SETTINGS.taskSwitchMin / 1000).toFixed(1); }
        if (document.getElementById('set-task-switch-max')) { document.getElementById('set-task-switch-max').value = (BOT_SETTINGS.taskSwitchMax / 1000).toFixed(1); }
    }

    async function controlledSleep(ms) {
        let total = Math.max(0, parseInt(ms, 10) || 0);
        let waited = 0;

        while (waited < total) {
            if (stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                return false;
            }
            let timeToWaitThisStep = Math.min(100, total - waited);
            await sleep(timeToWaitThisStep);
            waited += 100;
        }
        return !(stopRequested || killSwitchActivated);
    }

    function getInventoryAmount(name) {
        return Math.floor(parseFloat(SL_INVENTORY[name] || 0));
    }

    async function waitTaskSwitch(reason) {
        let delay = randInt(BOT_SETTINGS.taskSwitchMin, BOT_SETTINGS.taskSwitchMax);
        if (Math.random() < 0.18) {
            delay += randInt(600, 1800);
        }

        const phrases = [
            "GÃ¶rev geÃ§iÅŸi",
            "KÄ±sa kontrol molasÄ±",
            "Ä°ÅŸlem arasÄ± bekleme",
            "SÄ±radaki iÅŸe hazÄ±rlanÄ±yor"
        ];

        let phrase = phrases[randInt(0, phrases.length - 1)];
        let logStr = `ğŸ”„ ${phrase}`;
        if (reason) {
            logStr += ` (${reason})`;
        }
        logStr += `: ${delay}ms bekleniyor...`;

        log(logStr);
        return await controlledSleep(delay);
    }

    async function waitManualForestPace(reason) {
        let delay = randInt(32000, 58000);
        if (Math.random() < 0.22) {
            delay += randInt(2500, 7000);
        }

        let logStr = `ğŸ”„ Manual forest pacing`;
        if (reason) {
            logStr += ` (${reason})`;
        }
        logStr += `: ${delay}ms waiting...`;

        log(logStr);
        return await controlledSleep(delay);
    }

    function saveMarketSettingsToStorage() {
        localStorage.setItem('sl_market_settings', JSON.stringify(MARKET_SETTINGS));
    }

    function saveCookingSettingsToStorage() {
        localStorage.setItem('sl_cooking_settings', JSON.stringify(COOKING_SETTINGS));
    }

    function saveCharacterSettingsToStorage() {
        localStorage.setItem('sl_character_settings', JSON.stringify(CHARACTER_SETTINGS));
    }

    function formatDuration(seconds) {
        let sec = Math.max(0, Math.round(Number(seconds || 0)));
        let h = Math.floor(sec / 3600);
        let m = Math.floor((sec % 3600) / 60);
        let s = sec % 60;
        if (h > 0) {
            return h + "s " + m + "d";
        }
        if (m > 0) {
            return m + "d " + s + "sn";
        }
        return s + "sn";
    }

    function getRecipeRequirements(recipeName) {
        const recipe = FIRE_PIT_RECIPES[recipeName];
        if (!recipe) {
            return {};
        }

        const multiplier = GameRules.hasSkill("Double Nom") ? 2 : 1;
        const result = {};
        Object.keys(recipe.ingredients || {}).forEach(function(item) {
            result[item] = recipe.ingredients[item] * multiplier;
        });
        return result;
    }

    function canCookRecipe(recipeName) {
        const req = getRecipeRequirements(recipeName);
        const items = Object.keys(req);
        for (let i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
            if (readDecimal(SL_INVENTORY[items[i]], 0) < req[items[i]]) {
                return false;
            }
        }
        return true;
    }

    function getFirePitBuilding() {
        const pits = SL_BUILDINGS && SL_BUILDINGS["Fire Pit"];
        if (!Array.isArray(pits)) {
            return null;
        }
        for (let i = 0; i < pits.length; i++) {
            if (pits[i] && pits[i].coordinates && !pits[i].removedAt) {
                return pits[i];
            }
        }
        return pits[0] || null;
    }

    function getCookingOilBoost(recipeName, building) {
        const recipe = FIRE_PIT_RECIPES[recipeName];
        if (!recipe || !building) {
            return { timeToCook: recipe ? recipe.cookingSeconds : 0, oilConsumed: 0, percent: 0 };
        }

        const oilNeed = recipe.cookingSeconds / 86400;
        const availableOil = Math.max(0, Number(building.oil || 0));
        const boostPercent = GameRules.hasSkill("Swift Sizzle") ? 0.4 : 0.2;
        if (oilNeed <= 0) {
            return { timeToCook: recipe.cookingSeconds, oilConsumed: 0, percent: 0 };
        }
        if (availableOil >= oilNeed) {
            return {
                timeToCook: recipe.cookingSeconds * (1 - boostPercent),
                oilConsumed: oilNeed,
                percent: boostPercent
            };
        }
        const partialPercent = (availableOil / oilNeed) * boostPercent;
        return {
            timeToCook: recipe.cookingSeconds * (1 - partialPercent),
            oilConsumed: availableOil,
            percent: partialPercent
        };
    }

    function getCookPlan(recipeName, building, createdAtMs) {
        const recipe = FIRE_PIT_RECIPES[recipeName];
        const oil = getCookingOilBoost(recipeName, building);
        const time = GameRules.getCookingTime(recipeName, oil.timeToCook, "Fire Pit", createdAtMs);
        return {
            recipe: recipe,
            oilConsumed: oil.oilConsumed,
            readyAt: time.readyAt,
            boosts: time.boosts,
            seconds: time.seconds
        };
    }

    function renderCookingMenu() {
        const root = document.getElementById('fire-pit-recipes');
        if (!root) {
            return;
        }
        warmNexusIconsFromClientAssets(Object.keys(FIRE_PIT_RECIPES || {}));

        const building = getFirePitBuilding();
        const hasFirePit = !!building;
        const crafting = hasFirePit && Array.isArray(building.crafting) ? building.crafting : [];
        const selectedCount = Object.values(COOKING_SETTINGS.selected || {}).filter(Boolean).length;
        let html = "";

        Object.keys(FIRE_PIT_RECIPES).forEach(function(name) {
            const recipe = FIRE_PIT_RECIPES[name];
            const selected = !!COOKING_SETTINGS.selected[name];
            let progressHtml = "";
            const activeCraft = crafting.find(function(item) {
                const readyAt = parseTimeValue(item && item.readyAt);
                return item && item.name === name && readyAt > Date.now();
            });
            if (activeCraft) {
                const readyAt = parseTimeValue(activeCraft.readyAt);
                const startedAt = parseTimeValue(activeCraft.startedAt || activeCraft.createdAt) || (readyAt - (recipe.cookingSeconds * 1000));
                const totalMs = Math.max(1, readyAt - startedAt);
                const doneMs = Math.max(0, Date.now() - startedAt);
                const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round((doneMs / totalMs) * 100)));
                const leftMs = Math.max(0, readyAt - Date.now());
                progressHtml = `<div class="cook-progress" title="${pct}%"><div class="cook-progress-fill" style="width:${pct}%;"></div></div><div style="font-size:9px;color:#fde68a;font-weight:900;">Cooking: ${formatTimeLeftMs(Date.now() + leftMs)}</div>`;
            }
            const readyCount = crafting.filter(function(item) {
                const readyAt = parseTimeValue(item && item.readyAt);
                return item && item.name === name && readyAt > 0 && readyAt <= Date.now();
            }).length;
            const req = getRecipeRequirements(name);
            const needText = Object.keys(req).map(function(item) {
                const have = readDecimal(SL_INVENTORY[item], 0);
                const ok = have >= req[item];
                return `<span style="color:${ok ? '#86efac' : '#fca5a5'}">${item}: ${have}/${req[item]}</span>`;
            }).join("<br>");
            const plan = getCookPlan(name, building || {}, Date.now());
            const canCook = hasFirePit && canCookRecipe(name);
            const cardClass = "cook-card" + (selected ? " selected" : "") + (canCook || readyCount > 0 ? " ready" : "");
            html += `
                <div class="${cardClass}" data-recipe="${name}">
                    <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;height:34px;margin-bottom:6px;">${getItemIconHtml(name, 30)}</div>
                    <div class="cook-name">${name}</div>
                    <div class="cook-meta">${recipe.experience} XP<br>${formatDuration(plan.seconds)}${readyCount ? `<br><span style="color:#86efac">Hazir: ${readyCount}</span>` : ""}</div>
                    ${progressHtml}
                    <div class="cook-need">${needText || "Malzeme yok"}</div>
                </div>
            `;
        });

        root.innerHTML = html || `<div class="panel-sub">Tarif bulunamadi.</div>`;
        const cards = root.querySelectorAll('.cook-card');
        cards.forEach(function(card) {
