            card.onclick = function() {
                const recipe = card.getAttribute('data-recipe');
                COOKING_SETTINGS.selected[recipe] = !COOKING_SETTINGS.selected[recipe];
                saveCookingSettingsToStorage();
                renderCookingMenu();
            };
        });

        const autoToggle = document.getElementById('toggle-auto-cook');
        if (autoToggle) {
            autoToggle.checked = !!COOKING_SETTINGS.auto;
        }
        const smartToggle = document.getElementById('toggle-smart-cook');
        if (smartToggle) {
            smartToggle.checked = !!COOKING_SETTINGS.smartReserve;
        }
        lastCookingMenuRenderAt = Date.now();

    }

    function getSelectedCookRecipes() {
        return Object.keys(COOKING_SETTINGS.selected || {}).filter(function(name) {
            return COOKING_SETTINGS.selected[name] && FIRE_PIT_RECIPES[name];
        });
    }

    function getSelectedFeedFoods() {
        return Object.keys(CHARACTER_SETTINGS.selected || {}).filter(function(name) {
            return CHARACTER_SETTINGS.selected[name] && (FIRE_PIT_RECIPES[name] || FISH_FEED_ITEMS[name]);
        });
    }

    function calculateFoodXp(foodName, createdAtMs = Date.now()) {
        const recipe = FIRE_PIT_RECIPES[foodName] || FISH_FEED_ITEMS[foodName];
        if (!recipe) {
            return { xp: 0, boosts: [] };
        }

        let xp = Number(recipe.experience || 0);
        const boosts = [];

        if (GameRules.isWearableActive("Golden Spatula")) {
            xp *= 1.1;
            boosts.push({ name: "Golden Spatula", value: "x1.1" });
        }
        if (GameRules.isCollectibleBuilt("Blossombeard")) {
            xp *= 1.1;
            boosts.push({ name: "Blossombeard", value: "x1.1" });
        }
        if (GameRules.isWearableActive("Pan")) {
            xp *= 1.25;
            boosts.push({ name: "Pan", value: "x1.25" });
        }
        if (GameRules.isCollectibleBuilt("Observatory")) {
            xp *= 1.05;
            boosts.push({ name: "Observatory", value: "x1.05" });
        }
        if (GameRules.hasSkill("Munching Mastery")) {
            xp *= 1.05;
            boosts.push({ name: "Munching Mastery", value: "x1.05" });
        }
        if (FISH_FEED_ITEMS[foodName] && GameRules.isCollectibleBuilt("Skill Shrimpy")) {
            xp *= 1.2;
            boosts.push({ name: "Skill Shrimpy", value: "x1.2" });
        }
        if (FISH_FEED_ITEMS[foodName] && GameRules.hasSkill("Fishy Feast")) {
            xp *= 1.2;
            boosts.push({ name: "Fishy Feast", value: "x1.2" });
        }
        if (["Pizza Margherita"].includes(foodName) && GameRules.isCollectibleBuilt("Swiss Whiskers")) {
            xp += 500;
            boosts.push({ name: "Swiss Whiskers", value: "+500" });
        }

        return {
            xp: Math.round(xp * 10000) / 10000,
            boosts: boosts
        };
    }

    function renderCharacterMenu() {
        const root = document.getElementById('character-foods');
        if (!root) {
            return;
        }

        let html = "";
        const isFishTab = CHARACTER_SETTINGS.tab === "fish";
        if (isFishTab) {
            warmFishIconsFromClientAssets();
        }
        const catalog = isFishTab ? FISH_FEED_ITEMS : FIRE_PIT_RECIPES;
        warmNexusIconsFromClientAssets(Object.keys(catalog || {}));
        Object.keys(catalog).forEach(function(name) {
            const recipe = catalog[name];
            const selected = !!CHARACTER_SETTINGS.selected[name];
            const have = getInventoryAmount(name);
            const xpInfo = calculateFoodXp(name, Date.now());
            const cardClass = "cook-card" + (selected ? " selected" : "") + (have > 0 ? " ready" : "");

            html += `
                <div class="${cardClass}" data-food="${name}">
                    <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;height:36px;margin-bottom:6px;">${getCharacterFeedIconHtml(name)}</div>
                    <div class="cook-name">${name}</div>
                    <div class="cook-meta">${xpInfo.xp} XP<br><span style="color:${have > 0 ? '#86efac' : '#fca5a5'}">In bag: ${have}</span></div>
                    <div class="cook-need">${selected ? "Selected" : "Off"}${xpInfo.boosts.length ? "<br>" + xpInfo.boosts.map(function(b) { return b.name + " " + b.value; }).join("<br>") : ""}</div>
                </div>
            `;
        });

        root.innerHTML = html || `<div class="panel-sub">${isFishTab ? "No fish feed data found." : "No food found."}</div>`;
        const cards = root.querySelectorAll('.cook-card');
        cards.forEach(function(card) {
            card.onclick = function() {
                const food = card.getAttribute('data-food');
                CHARACTER_SETTINGS.selected[food] = !CHARACTER_SETTINGS.selected[food];
                saveCharacterSettingsToStorage();
                renderCharacterMenu();
            };
        });

        const autoToggle = document.getElementById('toggle-auto-feed');
        if (autoToggle) {
            autoToggle.checked = !!CHARACTER_SETTINGS.auto;
        }
        const foodsTab = document.getElementById('character-tab-foods');
        const fishTab = document.getElementById('character-tab-fish');
        if (foodsTab) {
            foodsTab.classList.toggle('active', CHARACTER_SETTINGS.tab !== "fish");
            foodsTab.onclick = function() {
                CHARACTER_SETTINGS.tab = "foods";
                saveCharacterSettingsToStorage();
                renderCharacterMenu();
            };
        }
        if (fishTab) {
            fishTab.classList.toggle('active', CHARACTER_SETTINGS.tab === "fish");
            fishTab.onclick = function() {
                CHARACTER_SETTINGS.tab = "fish";
                saveCharacterSettingsToStorage();
                renderCharacterMenu();
            };
        }
        lastCharacterMenuRenderAt = Date.now();
    }

    function hasCharacterFeedPending() {
        if (!CHARACTER_SETTINGS.auto || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
            return false;
        }
        const selected = getSelectedFeedFoods();
        for (let i = 0; i < selected.length; i++) {
            if (getInventoryAmount(selected[i]) > 0) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    async function runCharacterFeedPhase() {
        if (!hasCharacterFeedPending()) {
            return false;
        }

        const selected = getSelectedFeedFoods();
        const actions = [];
        let totalXp = 0;
        let fedInfo = [];
        let usedBoosts = [];

        for (let i = 0; i < selected.length; i++) {
            const foodName = selected[i];
            const amount = getInventoryAmount(foodName);
            if (amount <= 0) {
                continue;
            }

            const createdAtMs = Date.now();
            const dateIso = new Date(createdAtMs).toISOString();
            const xpInfo = calculateFoodXp(foodName, createdAtMs);

            actions.push({
                type: "bumpkin.feed",
                food: foodName,
                amount: amount,
                createdAt: dateIso
            });

            modifyInventory(foodName, -amount);
            modifyActivity(foodName + " Fed", amount);
            SL_BUMPKIN.experience = Number(SL_BUMPKIN.experience || 0) + (xpInfo.xp * amount);
            totalXp += xpInfo.xp * amount;
            fedInfo.push(amount + "x " + foodName);

            xpInfo.boosts.forEach(function(boost) {
                usedBoosts.push(boost);
                SL_BOOSTS_USED_AT[boost.name] = createdAtMs;
            });
        }

        if (actions.length === 0) {
            return false;
        }

        localStorage.setItem('sl_bumpkin_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_BUMPKIN));
        localStorage.setItem('sl_boosts_used_at_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_BOOSTS_USED_AT));

        let payload = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(masterPayload));
        payload.actions = actions;
        payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
        payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
        if (payload.stateHash.bumpkin) {
            payload.stateHash.bumpkin = await computeSHA256(SL_BUMPKIN);
        }
        if (payload.stateHash.boostsUsedAt) {
            payload.stateHash.boostsUsedAt = await computeSHA256(SL_BOOSTS_USED_AT);
        }
        await refreshVolatileStateHashes(payload);

        log(`ğŸ½ï¸ Karakter besleniyor: ${fedInfo.join(", ")} (+${Math.round(totalXp * 100) / 100} XP)`);

        try {
            let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                body: JSON.stringify(payload)
            });

            if (res.ok) {
                log(`âœ… Karakter besleme baÅŸarÄ±lÄ±.`);
                masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                renderCharacterMenu();
                return true;
            }

            triggerKillSwitch("Sunucu karakter beslemeyi reddetti.", res.status);
            return false;
        } catch(e) {
            triggerKillSwitch("AÄŸ baÄŸlantÄ±sÄ± koptu (Karakter besleme).", "NETWORK");
            return false;
        }
    }

    function getCookingReservedIngredients() {
        const reserved = {};
        if (!COOKING_SETTINGS.smartReserve) {
            return reserved;
        }

        getSelectedCookRecipes().forEach(function(recipeName) {
            const req = getRecipeRequirements(recipeName);
            Object.keys(req).forEach(function(item) {
                reserved[item] = Math.max(reserved[item] || 0, req[item]);
            });
        });
        return reserved;
    }

    function applyCookingIngredients(recipeName) {
        const req = getRecipeRequirements(recipeName);
        Object.keys(req).forEach(function(item) {
            modifyInventory(item, -req[item]);
        });
    }

    function getReadyCraftingIndexes(building) {
        const crafting = Array.isArray(building && building.crafting) ? building.crafting : [];
        const ready = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < crafting.length; i++) {
            const readyAt = parseTimeValue(crafting[i] && crafting[i].readyAt);
            if (crafting[i] && readyAt > 0 && readyAt <= Date.now()) {
                ready.push(i);
            }
        }
        return ready;
    }

    function hasCookingWorkPending() {
        if (!COOKING_SETTINGS.auto || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
            return false;
        }

        const selected = getSelectedCookRecipes();
        if (selected.length === 0) {
            return false;
        }

        const building = getFirePitBuilding();
        if (!building || !building.id) {
            return false;
        }

        if (getReadyCraftingIndexes(building).length > 0) {
            return true;
        }

        const currentCrafting = Array.isArray(building.crafting) ? building.crafting : [];
        if (currentCrafting.length >= 1) {
            return false;
        }

        for (let i = 0; i < selected.length; i++) {
            if (canCookRecipe(selected[i])) {
                return true;
            }
        }

        return false;
    }

    async function waitCookingPacketGap(reason) {
        let delay = randInt(5000, 10000);
        log(`ÄŸÅ¸ÂÂ² Fire Pit paket aralÃ„Â±Ã„Å¸Ã„Â± (${reason}): ${delay}ms bekleniyor...`);
        return await controlledSleep(delay);
    }

    async function sendCookingPayload(actions, reason) {
        if (!actions || actions.length === 0) {
            return false;
        }

        let stringifiedMaster = JSON.stringify(masterPayload);
        let payload = JSON.parse(stringifiedMaster);
        payload.actions = actions;
        payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
        payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
        if (payload.stateHash.bumpkin) {
            payload.stateHash.bumpkin = await computeSHA256(SL_BUMPKIN);
        }
        if (payload.stateHash.buildings) {
            payload.stateHash.buildings = await computeSHA256(SL_BUILDINGS);
        }
        await refreshVolatileStateHashes(payload);

        log(`ğŸ“¦ Fire Pit paketi gÃ¶nderiliyor... (${reason})`);

        try {
            let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                body: JSON.stringify(payload)
            });

            if (res.ok) {
                log(`âœ… Fire Pit iÅŸlemi baÅŸarÄ±lÄ±.`);
                masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                renderCookingMenu();
                return true;
            }

            triggerKillSwitch("Sunucu Fire Pit iÅŸlemini reddetti.", res.status);
            return false;
        } catch(e) {
            triggerKillSwitch("AÄŸ baÄŸlantÄ±sÄ± koptu (Fire Pit).", "NETWORK");
            return false;
        }
    }

    async function runCookingAutomationPhase() {
        if (!COOKING_SETTINGS.auto || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
            return false;
        }

        const selected = getSelectedCookRecipes();
        if (selected.length === 0) {
            return false;
        }

        const building = getFirePitBuilding();
        if (!building || !building.id) {
            return false;
        }

        let performed = false;
        let readyIndexes = getReadyCraftingIndexes(building);
        if (readyIndexes.length > 0) {
            if (GameRules.hasSkill("Fiery Jackpot") || GameRules.isWearableActive("Master Chef's Cleaver")) {
                triggerKillSwitch("Fire Pit toplamada sans bonusu aktif. PRNG muhasebesi port edilmeden durduruldu.", "COOK_PRNG_GUARD");
                return false;
            }

            let dateIso = new Date().toISOString();
            let actions = [{
                type: "recipes.collected",
                building: "Fire Pit",
                buildingId: building.id,
                createdAt: dateIso
            }];

            let remaining = [];
            let crafting = Array.isArray(building.crafting) ? building.crafting : [];
            for (let i = 0; i < crafting.length; i++) {
                let item = crafting[i];
                const readyAt = parseTimeValue(item && item.readyAt);
                if (item && readyAt > 0 && readyAt <= Date.now()) {
                    let amount = 1;
                    if (item.skills && item.skills["Double Nom"]) {
                        amount += 1;
                    }
                    modifyInventory(item.name, amount);
                    modifyActivity(item.name + " Cooked", 1);
                    const recipe = FIRE_PIT_RECIPES[item.name];
                    if (recipe && SL_BUMPKIN) {
                        SL_BUMPKIN.experience = Number(SL_BUMPKIN.experience || 0) + (Number(recipe.experience || 0) * amount);
                    }
                } else if (item) {
                    remaining.push(item);
                }
            }
            building.crafting = remaining;
            localStorage.setItem('sl_buildings_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_BUILDINGS));
            localStorage.setItem('sl_bumpkin_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_BUMPKIN));

            let ok = await sendCookingPayload(actions, "collect");
            if (!ok) {
                return false;
            }
            performed = true;
        }

        if (stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
            return performed;
        }

        const currentCrafting = Array.isArray(building.crafting) ? building.crafting : [];
        const maxSlots = 1;
        if (currentCrafting.length >= maxSlots) {
            return performed;
        }

        if (performed) {
            let keepGoing = await waitCookingPacketGap('collect â†’ cook');
            if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                return performed;
            }
        }

        for (let i = 0; i < selected.length; i++) {
            const recipeName = selected[i];
            const recipe = FIRE_PIT_RECIPES[recipeName];
            if (!recipe || recipe.cookingSeconds === 0) {
                continue;
            }
            if (!canCookRecipe(recipeName)) {
                continue;
            }

            let createdAtMs = Date.now();
            let dateIso = new Date(createdAtMs).toISOString();
            let plan = getCookPlan(recipeName, building, createdAtMs);
            let action = {
                type: "recipe.cooked",
                item: recipeName,
                buildingId: building.id,
                createdAt: dateIso
            };

            applyCookingIngredients(recipeName);
            building.crafting = Array.isArray(building.crafting) ? building.crafting : [];
            building.crafting.push({
                name: recipeName,
                boost: { Oil: plan.oilConsumed },
                skills: { "Double Nom": GameRules.hasSkill("Double Nom") },
                readyAt: plan.readyAt
            });
            if (plan.oilConsumed > 0) {
                building.oil = Math.max(0, Number(building.oil || 0) - plan.oilConsumed);
            }
            localStorage.setItem('sl_buildings_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_BUILDINGS));

            log(`${recipeName} cooking. Ready in: ${formatDuration(plan.seconds)}`);
            let ok = await sendCookingPayload([action], "cook");
            if (!ok) {
                return performed;
            }
            performed = true;
            break;
        }

        return performed;
    }

    function getItemEmoji(name = '') {
        const text = String(name || "").trim();
        if (!text) return "";
        return text.split(/\s+/).slice(0, 2).map(function(part) {
            return part.charAt(0).toUpperCase();
        }).join("");
    }

    function getAvailableStock(item) {
        let rawStock = SL_STOCK && SL_STOCK[item];
        if (rawStock === undefined || rawStock === null || rawStock === "") {
            return Infinity;
        }

        let parsed = parseInt(rawStock);
        if (Number.isNaN(parsed)) {
            return Infinity;
        }

        return Math.max(0, parsed);
    }

    function buildBuyChunks(totalNeeded, maxAvailable) {
        let needed = Math.max(0, parseInt(totalNeeded) || 0);
        if (Number.isFinite(maxAvailable)) {
            needed = Math.min(needed, Math.max(0, parseInt(maxAvailable) || 0));
        }
        if (needed <= 0) return [];

        const tens = Math.floor(needed / 10) * 10;
        const remainder = needed % 10;
        let plannedTotal = tens;

        if (remainder >= 1 && remainder <= 3) {
            plannedTotal = tens + remainder;
        } else if (remainder === 4) {
            plannedTotal = tens;
        } else if (remainder === 5) {
            plannedTotal = Math.random() < 0.5 ? tens : tens + 10;
        } else if (remainder >= 6) {
            plannedTotal = tens + 10;
        }

        if (plannedTotal <= 0) {
            plannedTotal = needed;
        }

        plannedTotal = Math.min(plannedTotal, needed);
        if (Number.isFinite(maxAvailable)) {
            plannedTotal = Math.min(plannedTotal, Math.max(0, parseInt(maxAvailable) || 0));
        }

        const chunks = [];
        let remain = plannedTotal;
        while (remain >= 10) {
            chunks.push(10);
            remain -= 10;
        }
        if (remain > 0) {
            chunks.push(remain);
        }
        return chunks;
    }

    function parseTimeValue(value) {
        if (value == null) return 0;
        if (typeof value === 'number') return value;
        if (typeof value === 'string') {
            const numeric = Number(value);
            if (!Number.isNaN(numeric) && numeric > 0) {
                return numeric;
            }
            let dateMs = new Date(value).getTime();
            return Number.isNaN(dateMs) ? 0 : dateMs;
        }
        return 0;
    }

    function getCropReadyAt(plotObj) {
        return GameRules.getCropReadyAt(plotObj);
    }

    function getCropStatus(plotObj) {
        if (!plotObj || !plotObj.crop) return "EMPTY";
        const estimatedReadyAt = getCropReadyAt(plotObj);

        if (!estimatedReadyAt) return "UNKNOWN";
        return Date.now() >= estimatedReadyAt ? "READY" : "GROWING";
    }

    function getVirtualInventory() {
        let stringifiedInv = JSON.stringify(SL_INVENTORY);
        let vInv = JSON.parse(stringifiedInv);

        let plotEntries = Object.entries(PLOT_TASKS);
        for (let i = 0; i < plotEntries.length; i++) {
            let plotId = plotEntries[i][0];
            let seed = plotEntries[i][1];
            const plot = SL_CROPS[plotId];
            if (plot && !plot.crop && vInv[seed]) {
                vInv[seed] = parseFloat(vInv[seed]) - 1;
            }
        }
        return vInv;
    }

    // ==========================================
    // ğŸŒ¾ TARLA VE MARKET GÃ–RSELLEÅTÄ°RME
    // ==========================================
    function renderWaterCapacityPanel() {
        const panel = document.getElementById('water-capacity-panel');
        if (!panel) return;

        const info = GameRules.getWaterCapacityInfo();
        const plotFilters = GameRules.getSafeAndQuarantinedPlots();
        const total = info.totalPlots || parseInt(SL_INVENTORY['Crop Plot'] || 0) || 0;
        const safeCount = info.totalPlots ? plotFilters.safe.length : Math.min(total, info.activeLimit);
        const lockedCount = info.totalPlots ? plotFilters.quarantined.length : Math.max(0, total - info.activeLimit);
        const fillPercent = total > 0 ? Math.min(100, Math.round((safeCount / total) * 100)) : 0;
        const waterText = info.unlimitedWater ? "Unlimited" : String(info.supportedByWater);
        const wellText = info.wellPlaced
            ? ("Level " + info.effectiveWellLevel + (info.upgrading ? " (upgrading)" : ""))
            : "None";
        const lockClass = lockedCount > 0 ? "capacity-danger" : "capacity-ok";
        const waterLocked = Math.max(0, total - info.supportedByWater);
        const waterLockText = waterLocked > 0 ? waterLocked + " water locked" : "None";
        let upgradeText = "None";

        if (info.upgrading && info.upgradeReadyAt) {
            const leftMs = Math.max(0, info.upgradeReadyAt - Date.now());
            const mins = Math.floor(leftMs / 60000);
            const secs = Math.floor((leftMs % 60000) / 1000);
            upgradeText = mins + "m " + secs + "s";
        }

        const arrow = WATER_PANEL_OPEN ? "^" : "v";

        panel.innerHTML = `
            <div class="capacity-head capacity-toggle" onclick="toggleWaterCapacityPanel()">
                <div class="capacity-title">Water Capacity <span class="capacity-arrow">${arrow}</span></div>
                <div class="capacity-pill">${safeCount}/${total || 0}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="capacity-meter"><div class="capacity-fill" style="width:${fillPercent}%"></div></div>
            <div class="capacity-body ${WATER_PANEL_OPEN ? "open" : ""}">
            <table class="capacity-table">
                <tr>
                    <td>Island</td><td>${info.islandType}</td>
                    <td>Well</td><td>${wellText}</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                    <td>Water support</td><td>${waterText}</td>
                    <td>Game limit</td><td class="capacity-ok">${info.activeLimit}</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                    <td>Total fields</td><td>${total || "-"}</td>
                    <td>Locked</td><td class="${lockClass}">${lockedCount}</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                    <td>Water lock</td><td class="${waterLocked > 0 ? "capacity-danger" : "capacity-muted"}">${waterLockText}</td>
                    <td>Source</td><td class="capacity-muted">Session rules</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                    <td>Well upgrade</td><td class="${info.upgrading ? "capacity-warn" : "capacity-muted"}">${upgradeText}</td>
                    <td>Well count</td><td>${info.wellCount}</td>
                </tr>
            </table>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    _window.toggleWaterCapacityPanel = function() {
        WATER_PANEL_OPEN = !WATER_PANEL_OPEN;
        localStorage.setItem('sl_water_panel_open', WATER_PANEL_OPEN ? 'true' : 'false');
        renderWaterCapacityPanel();
    };

    function renderMushroomPanel() {
        const body = document.getElementById('mushroom-panel-body');
        const countEl = document.getElementById('mushroom-panel-count');
        const arrow = document.getElementById('mushroom-panel-arrow');
        if (!body || !countEl) return;

        const entries = getReadyMushroomEntries();
        countEl.textContent = String(entries.length);
        body.classList.toggle('open', MUSHROOM_PANEL_OPEN);
        if (arrow) {
            arrow.textContent = MUSHROOM_PANEL_OPEN ? '^' : 'v';
        }

        if (entries.length === 0) {
            body.innerHTML = `<div class="mushroom-empty">No visible mushrooms in cached session.</div>`;
            return;
        }

        body.innerHTML = entries.map(function(entry) {
            const id = entry[0];
            const mushroom = entry[1];
            const amount = parseFloat(mushroom.amount || 0);
            const shortId = id.slice(0, 6);
            return `
                <div class="mushroom-item">
                    <span>${getItemEmoji(mushroom.name)} ${mushroom.name}</span>
                    <span>${amount} - ${shortId}</span>
                </div>
            `;
        }).join('');
    }

    _window.toggleMushroomPanel = function() {
        MUSHROOM_PANEL_OPEN = !MUSHROOM_PANEL_OPEN;
        localStorage.setItem('sl_mushroom_panel_open', MUSHROOM_PANEL_OPEN ? 'true' : 'false');
        renderMushroomPanel();
    };

    function renderPlotGrid() {
        const grid = document.getElementById('plot-grid');
        if(!grid) return;

        renderWaterCapacityPanel();
        renderMushroomPanel();
        grid.innerHTML = "";
        const entries = Object.entries(SL_CROPS || {});

        if (!entries.length) {
            let placeholderCount = Math.max(15, parseInt(SL_INVENTORY['Crop Plot'] || 0));
            for (let i = 0; i < placeholderCount; i++) {
                let div = document.createElement('div');
                div.className = 'plot-square';
                div.innerHTML = `
                    <span class="plot-emoji">...</span>
                    <span class="plot-status" style="color:#94a3b8;">LOADING</span>
                    <span class="plot-task">Preparing</span>
                    <span class="plot-hint">Waiting for radar</span>
                `;
                grid.appendChild(div);
            }
            return;
        }

        let plotFilters = getSafeAndQuarantinedPlots();
        let safePlots = plotFilters.safe;
        let quarantinedPlots = plotFilters.quarantined;

        entries.forEach(function([id, plot]) {
            const task = PLOT_TASKS[id];
            const isQuarantined = quarantinedPlots.includes(id);
            const div = document.createElement('div');

            if (isQuarantined) {
                div.className = "plot-square plot-quarantine";
            } else if (task) {
                div.className = "plot-square plot-assigned";
            } else {
                div.className = "plot-square";
            }

            const status = getCropStatus(plot);
            let statusText = "";
            let statusColor = "";
            let hintText = "";
            let icon = "";

            if (isQuarantined) {
                statusText = "LOCKED";
                statusColor = "#ef4444";
                hintText = "Quarantined";
                icon = "LOCK";
            }
            else if (status === "EMPTY") {
                statusText = "EMPTY";
                statusColor = "#a1a1aa";
                hintText = "Choose a seed";
                if (task) {
                    icon = getItemEmoji(task.replace(" Seed", ""));
                } else {
                    icon = "";
                }
            }
            else if (status === "READY") {
                statusText = "READY";
                statusColor = "#4ade80";
                hintText = "Ready to harvest";
                if (plot.crop && plot.crop.name) {
                    icon = getItemEmoji(plot.crop.name);
                } else {
                    icon = "OK";
                }
            }
            else if (status === "GROWING") {
                let readyAt = getCropReadyAt(plot);
                let timeRemaining = readyAt - Date.now();

                if (timeRemaining > 0) {
                    let ts = Math.floor(timeRemaining / 1000);
                    let m = Math.floor(ts / 60);
                    let s = ts % 60;
                    let h = Math.floor(m / 60);
                    m = m % 60;

                    if (h > 0) {
                        statusText = h + "h " + m + "m";
                    } else {
                        statusText = m + "m " + s + "s";
                    }
                } else {
                    statusText = "GROWING";
                }

                statusColor = "#facc15";
                hintText = "Growing";

                if (plot.crop && plot.crop.name) {
                    icon = getItemEmoji(plot.crop.name);
                } else {
                    icon = "";
                }
            }

            else {
                statusText = "CHECK";
                statusColor = "#fb923c";
                hintText = "Waiting for live plant time";
                icon = plot.crop && plot.crop.name ? getItemEmoji(plot.crop.name) : "?";
            }

            let taskText = "";
            if (isQuarantined) {
                taskText = "Limit Locked";
            } else if (task) {
                taskText = task.replace(" Seed", "");
            } else {
                taskText = 'Empty';
            }

            div.innerHTML = `
                <span class="plot-emoji">${icon}</span>
                <span class="plot-status" style="color:${statusColor}">${statusText}</span>
                <span class="plot-task">${taskText}</span>
                <span class="plot-hint">${hintText}</span>
            `;

            div.onclick = function() {
                if (!isQuarantined) {
                    openSeedSelection(id);
                } else {
                    alert("This field is quarantined by the active safety limit.");
                }
            };

            grid.appendChild(div);
        });

        let stringifiedTasks = JSON.stringify(PLOT_TASKS);
        localStorage.setItem('sl_plot_tasks', stringifiedTasks);
    }

    function openSeedSelection(plotId) {
        const list = document.getElementById('seed-list');

        let titleString = `<div style="text-align:center; color:#f8fafc; font-weight:900; margin-bottom:6px; font-size:13px;">Field ${plotId.substr(0,4)}</div>`;
        let descString = `<div style="text-align:center; color:#94a3b8; font-size:10px; margin-bottom:10px;">Choose a seed for this field.</div>`;
        let emptyString = `<div class="seed-option" style="color:#fda4af;" onclick="setPlotTask('${plotId}', null)">Leave Empty</div>`;

        list.innerHTML = titleString + descString + emptyString;

        const vInv = getVirtualInventory();
        let invEntries = Object.entries(vInv);

        let availableSeeds = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < invEntries.length; i++) {
            let n = invEntries[i][0];
            let a = invEntries[i][1];
            if (n.includes('Seed') && Math.floor(parseFloat(a)) >= 1 && ALL_KNOWN_SEEDS.includes(n) && GameRules.isSeedInCurrentSeason(n) && GameRules.canBuySeed(n)) {
                availableSeeds.push([n, a]);
            }
        }

        if (availableSeeds.length === 0) {
            list.innerHTML += `<div style="color:#facc15; font-size:10px; margin-top:10px; text-align:center;">No free seeds left. Buy seeds first.</div>`;
        } else {
            availableSeeds.forEach(function([n, a]) {
                let displayAmt = Math.floor(a);
                if (PLOT_TASKS[plotId] === n) {
                    displayAmt += 1;
                }

                let emoji = getItemEmoji(n);

                list.innerHTML += `
                    <div class="seed-option" onclick="setPlotTask('${plotId}', '${n}')">
                        ${emoji} ${n}
                        <span style="float:right; color:#93c5fd;">Free: ${displayAmt}</span>
                    </div>
                `;
            });
        }

        let modalElement = document.getElementById('seed-modal');
        modalElement.style.display = 'block';
    }

    _window.setPlotTask = function(id, seed) {
        if (seed) {
            PLOT_TASKS[id] = seed;
        } else {
            delete PLOT_TASKS[id];
        }

        let stringifiedTasks = JSON.stringify(PLOT_TASKS);
        localStorage.setItem('sl_plot_tasks', stringifiedTasks);

        let modalElement = document.getElementById('seed-modal');
        modalElement.style.display = 'none';

        renderPlotGrid();
    };

    function switchTab(tabName) {
        let sellTab = document.getElementById('tab-sell');
        let buyTab = document.getElementById('tab-buy');
        let sellBtn = document.getElementById('tab-sell-btn');
        let buyBtn = document.getElementById('tab-buy-btn');

        if(sellTab) sellTab.classList.remove('active');
        if(buyTab) buyTab.classList.remove('active');
        if(sellBtn) sellBtn.classList.remove('active');
        if(buyBtn) buyBtn.classList.remove('active');

        let targetTab = document.getElementById(`tab-${tabName}`);
        let targetBtn = document.getElementById(`tab-${tabName}-btn`);

        if(targetTab) targetTab.classList.add('active');
        if(targetBtn) targetBtn.classList.add('active');
    }

    function renderMarketTabs() {
        const sellTab = document.getElementById('tab-sell');
        if(!sellTab) return;
        warmNexusIconsFromClientAssets(KNOWN_CROPS.concat(ALL_KNOWN_SEEDS));

        let saleBonusRows = KNOWN_CROPS.map(function(crop) {
            let info = getSpecialEventSaleInfo(crop, Date.now());
            if (!info.active || info.multiplier <= 1) {
                return "";
            }
            let left = formatTimeLeftMs(info.endAt);
            return `<span style="display:inline-flex; align-items:center; gap:4px; margin:2px 4px 2px 0; padding:4px 7px; border-radius:6px; background:linear-gradient(90deg,#7f1d1d,#ea580c); color:#fff7ed; font-weight:900; box-shadow:0 0 10px rgba(251,146,60,0.35);">${getItemIconHtml(crop, 18)} ${crop} x${info.multiplier}${left ? " - " + left : ""}</span>`;
        }).filter(Boolean).join("");
        let sellDesc = saleBonusRows
            ? `<div style="font-size:10px; color:#fed7aa; margin-bottom:10px; padding:8px; border:1px solid rgba(251,146,60,0.45); border-radius:7px; background:rgba(124,45,18,0.32);"><div style="font-weight:900; color:#fdba74; margin-bottom:4px;">LIVE SALE BOOST</div>${saleBonusRows}</div>`
            : `<div style="font-size:10px; color:#a1a1aa; margin-bottom:10px;">Live sale prices are shown in yellow.</div>`;

        if (selectedSellCrop && !KNOWN_CROPS.includes(selectedSellCrop)) {
            selectedSellCrop = "";
            localStorage.removeItem('sl_selected_sell_crop');
        }

        let sellGrid = `<div style="font-size:10px;color:#bfdbfe;margin-bottom:8px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;"><span>${GameRules.getCurrentSeason()} Produce</span><span>${KNOWN_CROPS.length} items</span></div><div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(5,48px);gap:6px;">`;
        KNOWN_CROPS.forEach(function(crop) {
            let defaultCfg = { active: false, minEnabled: false, min: 1 };
            const cfg = MARKET_SETTINGS.sell[crop] || defaultCfg;
            let info = getSellCropDetails(crop);
            let amount = info.amount;
            let selected = selectedSellCrop === crop;
            let safeCropName = crop.replace(/'/g, "\\'");
            let saleBadge = "";
            if (info.saleInfo.active && info.saleInfo.multiplier > 1) {
                saleBadge = `<span style="position:absolute;right:-5px;bottom:-5px;background:#ea580c;color:#fff7ed;border:1px solid #fed7aa;border-radius:4px;font-size:9px;padding:1px 3px;font-weight:900;">x${info.saleInfo.multiplier}</span>`;
            }
            sellGrid += `
                <button type="button" onclick="selectSellCrop('${safeCropName}')" title="${crop}" style="position:relative;width:48px;height:48px;border-radius:8px;border:2px solid ${selected ? '#dbeafe' : cfg.active ? '#22c55e' : 'rgba(71,85,105,0.75)'};background:${selected ? 'linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(37,99,235,0.45),rgba(15,23,42,0.8))' : 'linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(30,41,59,0.94),rgba(15,23,42,0.98))'};box-shadow:${selected ? '0 0 0 2px #1d4ed8' : 'none'};cursor:pointer;font-size:22px;">
                    ${getItemIconHtml(crop, 28)}
                    <span style="position:absolute;top:-7px;left:7px;min-width:22px;padding:1px 3px;border-radius:3px;background:${amount <= 0 ? '#64748b' : '#e0f2fe'};color:${amount <= 0 ? '#fff' : '#1e3a8a'};font-size:10px;font-weight:900;border:1px solid #1e293b;">${amount}</span>
                    ${saleBadge}
                </button>`;
        });
        sellGrid += `</div>`;

        let sellDetail = `<div style="height:100%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;color:#fef3c7;font-size:12px;text-align:center;">Select produce</div>`;
        if (selectedSellCrop) {
            let crop = selectedSellCrop;
            let cfg = MARKET_SETTINGS.sell[crop] || { active: false, min: 1 };
            let info = getSellCropDetails(crop);
            let activeChecked = cfg.active ? 'checked' : '';
            let minValue = Math.max(1, parseInt(cfg.min || 1) || 1);
            let sellableAmount = Math.max(0, info.amount - minValue);
            let saleLine = "";
            if (info.saleInfo.active && info.saleInfo.multiplier > 1) {
                let left = formatTimeLeftMs(info.saleInfo.endAt);
                saleLine = `<div style="text-align:center;color:#fed7aa;font-weight:900;background:rgba(154,52,18,0.35);border:1px solid rgba(251,146,60,0.45);border-radius:7px;padding:6px;">LIVE x${info.saleInfo.multiplier}${left ? " - " + left : ""}</div>`;
            }
            sellDetail = `
                <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:10px;color:#e5e7eb;font-size:12px;">
                    <div style="text-align:center;font-weight:900;color:#f8fafc;background:${info.amount <= 0 ? '#64748b' : '#2563eb'};align-self:center;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:4px;">${info.amount} owned</div>
                    <div style="font-size:16px;font-weight:900;text-align:center;color:#f8fafc;">${crop}</div>
                    <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;height:44px;">${getItemIconHtml(crop, 42)}</div>
                    <div style="text-align:center;color:#cbd5e1;min-height:34px;">${info.description}</div>
                    ${saleLine}
                    <div style="border-top:1px solid rgba(226,232,240,0.25);padding-top:10px;text-align:center;color:#fde047;font-weight:900;font-size:14px;">${formatCoinAmount(info.price)} coins</div>
                    <div class="mini-switch-wrapper" style="justify-content:space-between;align-self:stretch;padding:7px 10px;background:rgba(30,64,175,0.20);border-color:rgba(96,165,250,0.35);">
                        <span class="mini-label" style="font-size:10px;color:#bfdbfe;">Auto Sell</span>
                        <label class="switch">
                            <input type="checkbox" class="sell-active" data-crop="${crop}" ${activeChecked}>
                            <span class="slider"></span>
                        </label>
                    </div>
                    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:auto 1fr;gap:8px;align-items:center;">
                        <span style="font-weight:900;color:#fde68a;">Min</span>
                        <input type="number" class="sell-min" data-crop="${crop}" value="${minValue}" min="1" max="999" style="background:rgba(30,41,59,0.95);color:#f8fafc;border:1px solid rgba(96,165,250,0.45);border-radius:8px;padding:8px;">
                    </div>
                    <div style="text-align:center;color:${sellableAmount > 0 ? '#bbf7d0' : '#fca5a5'};font-size:11px;font-weight:800;">Auto can sell: ${sellableAmount}</div>
                </div>`;
        }

        sellTab.innerHTML = `
            ${sellDesc}
            <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:292px minmax(230px,1fr);gap:12px;align-items:stretch;">
                <div style="border:1px solid rgba(148,163,184,0.18);background:linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(15,23,42,0.96),rgba(30,41,59,0.88));padding:11px;border-radius:12px;min-height:390px;max-height:460px;overflow-y:auto;">${sellGrid}</div>
                <div style="border:1px solid rgba(148,163,184,0.18);background:linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(15,23,42,0.96),rgba(30,41,59,0.88));padding:12px;border-radius:12px;min-height:390px;">${sellDetail}</div>
            </div>`;

        const buyTab = document.getElementById('tab-buy');
        if(!buyTab) return;

        const visibleSeeds = GameRules.getVisibleMarketSeeds();
        if (selectedBuySeed && !visibleSeeds.includes(selectedBuySeed)) {
            selectedBuySeed = "";
            localStorage.removeItem('sl_selected_buy_seed');
        }

        let seedGrid = `<div style="font-size:10px;color:#bfdbfe;margin-bottom:8px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;"><span>${GameRules.getCurrentSeason()} Market</span><span>${visibleSeeds.length} seeds</span></div><div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(5,48px);gap:6px;">`;
        visibleSeeds.forEach(function(seed) {
            let cfg = MARKET_SETTINGS.buy[seed] || { active: false, min: 10, max: 20, ignoreStockLimit: false, autoShipmentRestock: false };
            let seedInfo = getMarketSeedDetails(seed);
            let supportedSeed = !!seedInfo.supportedForBot;
            let stock = getAvailableStock(seed);
            let stockText = Number.isFinite(stock) ? stock : 0;
            let levelLocked = GameRules.getCurrentBumpkinLevel() < (seedInfo.bumpkinLevel || 1);
            let selected = selectedBuySeed === seed;
            let active = cfg.active;
            let safeSeedName = seed.replace(/'/g, "\\'");
            let badge = stockText;
            let opacity = levelLocked ? "0.48" : "1";
            seedGrid += `
                <button type="button" onclick="selectBuySeed('${safeSeedName}')" title="${seed}" style="position:relative;width:48px;height:48px;border-radius:8px;border:2px solid ${selected ? '#dbeafe' : active ? '#22c55e' : 'rgba(71,85,105,0.75)'};background:${selected ? 'linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(37,99,235,0.45),rgba(15,23,42,0.8))' : 'linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(30,41,59,0.94),rgba(15,23,42,0.98))'};opacity:${opacity};box-shadow:${selected ? '0 0 0 2px #1d4ed8' : 'none'};cursor:pointer;font-size:22px;">
                    ${getItemIconHtml(seed, 28)}
                    <span style="position:absolute;top:-7px;left:7px;min-width:22px;padding:1px 3px;border-radius:3px;background:${stockText === "0" ? '#ef4444' : '#e0f2fe'};color:${stockText === "0" ? '#fff' : '#1e3a8a'};font-size:10px;font-weight:900;border:1px solid #1e293b;">${badge}</span>
                    ${!supportedSeed ? '<span style="position:absolute;right:-4px;bottom:-4px;background:#1f2937;color:#e5e7eb;border:1px solid #e5e7eb;border-radius:4px;font-size:9px;padding:1px 3px;">Info</span>' : levelLocked ? '<span style="position:absolute;right:-4px;bottom:-4px;background:#7f1d1d;color:#fecaca;border:1px solid #fecaca;border-radius:4px;font-size:9px;padding:1px 3px;">Lv</span>' : ''}
                </button>`;
        });
        seedGrid += `</div>`;

        let detail = `<div style="height:100%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;color:#fef3c7;font-size:12px;text-align:center;">Select a seed</div>`;
        if (selectedBuySeed) {
            let seed = selectedBuySeed;
            let cfg = MARKET_SETTINGS.buy[seed] || { active: false, min: 10, max: 20, ignoreStockLimit: false, autoShipmentRestock: false };
            let seedInfo = getMarketSeedDetails(seed);
            let supportedSeed = !!seedInfo.supportedForBot;
            let stock = getAvailableStock(seed);
            let stockText = Number.isFinite(stock) ? stock : 0;
            let activeChecked = cfg.active ? 'checked' : '';
            let riskChecked = cfg.ignoreStockLimit ? 'checked' : '';
            let autoChecked = cfg.autoShipmentRestock ? 'checked' : '';
            let price = Number.isFinite(parseFloat(seedInfo.price)) ? parseFloat(seedInfo.price).toFixed(4) : "?";
            let growMs = Math.max(0, parseInt(seedInfo.plantSeconds || 0) * 1000);
            let levelReq = seedInfo.bumpkinLevel || 1;
            let levelLocked = GameRules.getCurrentBumpkinLevel() < levelReq;
            let seasonBad = !GameRules.isSeedInCurrentSeason(seed);
            let riskDisabledText = !supportedSeed ? "Info only: bot does not plant this seed yet" : !Number.isFinite(stock) ? "Unknown stock. Enable Market Limit (Risk) to buy." : stock <= 0 ? "Sold out" : "";
            let requirementText = levelLocked ? 'Level ' + levelReq + ' required' : 'Level ' + levelReq + '+';
            let growText = growMs > 0 ? formatTimeLeftMs(Date.now() + growMs) : "?";
            detail = `
                <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:9px;color:#e5e7eb;font-size:12px;">
                    <div style="text-align:center;font-weight:900;color:#f8fafc;background:${stockText === "0" ? '#ef4444' : '#2563eb'};align-self:center;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:4px;">${stockText === "0" ? 'Sold out' : stockText + ' in stock'}</div>
                    <div style="font-size:15px;font-weight:900;text-align:center;color:#f8fafc;">${seed}</div>
                    <div style="text-align:center;color:#cbd5e1;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:5px;">${getItemIconHtml(seedInfo.yield || seed, 20)} <span>${seedInfo.type || 'Unknown'}${seedInfo.yield ? ' - yields ' + seedInfo.yield : ''}</span></div>
                    <div style="text-align:center;color:${levelLocked ? '#fecaca' : '#bbf7d0'};font-weight:800;">${requirementText}${seasonBad ? ' - wrong season' : ''}</div>
                    ${seedInfo.plantingSpot ? `<div style="text-align:center;color:#fca5a5;font-weight:900;">${seedInfo.plantingSpot} Needed</div>` : ''}
                    ${seedInfo.harvests ? `<div style="text-align:center;color:#bbf7d0;font-weight:800;">${seedInfo.harvests}</div>` : ''}
                    <div style="text-align:center;color:#fde68a;">${growText} - ${price} coins</div>
                    ${riskDisabledText ? `<div style="text-align:center;color:#991b1b;font-weight:900;">${riskDisabledText}</div>` : ''}
                    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:auto 1fr auto 1fr;gap:7px;align-items:center;">
                        <span>Min</span><input type="number" class="buy-min" data-seed="${seed}" value="${cfg.min}" min="1" max="999">
                        <span>Max</span><input type="number" class="buy-max" data-seed="${seed}" value="${cfg.max}" min="1" max="999">
                    </div>
                    <div class="mini-switch-wrapper" style="justify-content:space-between;padding:7px 9px;background:rgba(30,64,175,0.20);border-color:rgba(96,165,250,0.35);">
                        <span class="mini-label" style="font-size:10px;color:#bfdbfe;">Auto Buy</span>
                        <label class="switch">
                            <input type="checkbox" class="buy-active" data-seed="${seed}" ${activeChecked}>
                            <span class="slider"></span>
                        </label>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mini-switch-wrapper" style="justify-content:space-between;padding:7px 9px;background:rgba(20,83,45,0.22);border-color:rgba(74,222,128,0.35);">
                        <span class="mini-label" style="font-size:10px;color:#bbf7d0;">Auto Limit Boost - ${GameRules.getNextShipmentText()}</span>
                        <label class="switch">
                            <input type="checkbox" class="buy-auto-shipment" data-seed="${seed}" ${autoChecked}>
                            <span class="slider"></span>
                        </label>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mini-switch-wrapper" style="justify-content:space-between;padding:7px 9px;background:rgba(127,29,29,0.20);border-color:rgba(248,113,113,0.35);">
                        <span class="mini-label" style="font-size:10px;color:#fecaca;">Market Limit (Risk)</span>
                        <label class="switch">
                            <input type="checkbox" class="buy-ignore-stock-limit" data-seed="${seed}" ${riskChecked}>
                            <span class="slider"></span>
                        </label>
                    </div>
                    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr auto;gap:6px;opacity:${masterPayload ? '1' : '0.45'};">
                        <input id="manual-buy-amount" type="number" min="1" max="999" value="1" ${masterPayload ? '' : 'disabled'} style="background:rgba(30,41,59,0.95);color:#f8fafc;border:1px solid rgba(96,165,250,0.45);border-radius:8px;padding:8px;">
                        <button type="button" onclick="manualBuySelectedSeed()" ${masterPayload ? '' : 'disabled'} style="background:linear-gradient(90deg,#f59e0b,#facc15);color:#111827;border:1px solid rgba(251,191,36,0.6);border-radius:8px;padding:8px 12px;font-weight:900;cursor:${masterPayload ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed'};">Buy</button>
                    </div>
                    ${masterPayload ? '' : '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#fca5a5;text-align:center;">Manual buy unlocks after bot control is captured.</div>'}
                </div>`;
        }

        buyTab.innerHTML = `
            <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:292px minmax(230px,1fr);gap:12px;align-items:stretch;">
                <div style="border:1px solid rgba(148,163,184,0.18);background:linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(15,23,42,0.96),rgba(30,41,59,0.88));padding:11px;border-radius:12px;min-height:390px;max-height:460px;overflow-y:auto;">${seedGrid}</div>
                <div style="border:1px solid rgba(148,163,184,0.18);background:linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(15,23,42,0.96),rgba(30,41,59,0.88));padding:12px;border-radius:12px;min-height:390px;">${detail}</div>
            </div>`;
    }

    function safeRenderPlotGrid(reason = '') {
        try {
            if (typeof renderPlotGrid === 'function') {
                renderPlotGrid();
            }
        } catch (e) {
            log(`âš ï¸ Tarla paneli yenilenemedi${reason ? " (" + reason + ")" : ""}: ${e && e.message ? e.message : e}`);
        }
    }

    function handleMarketSettingsInput(e) {
        const target = e?.target;
        if (!target) return;

        if (target.matches('.sell-active') || target.matches('.sell-min') || target.matches('.buy-active') || target.matches('.buy-min') || target.matches('.buy-max') || target.matches('.buy-ignore-stock-limit') || target.matches('.buy-auto-shipment')) {
            saveMarketSettings();
            if (target.matches('.sell-active') || target.matches('.buy-active') || target.matches('.buy-ignore-stock-limit') || target.matches('.buy-auto-shipment')) {
                renderMarketTabs();
            }
        }
    }

    function closeMarketMenu() {
        saveMarketSettings();
        let marketMenu = document.getElementById('sl-market-menu');
        if(marketMenu) {
            marketMenu.style.display = 'none';
        }
    }

    function saveMarketSettings() {
        const sellObj = {};

        KNOWN_CROPS.forEach(function(crop) {
            let defaultCfg = { active: false, min: 1 };
            let currentCfg = MARKET_SETTINGS.sell[crop] || defaultCfg;

            let activeEl = document.querySelector(`.sell-active[data-crop="${crop}"]`);
            let activeSell = activeEl ? !!activeEl.checked : !!currentCfg.active;

            let minInputEl = document.querySelector(`.sell-min[data-crop="${crop}"]`);
            let parsedMin = parseInt(minInputEl ? minInputEl.value : (currentCfg.min || 1));
            let min = Math.max(1, parsedMin || 1);

            if (activeSell || min > 1) {
                sellObj[crop] = {
                    active: activeSell,
                    minEnabled: min > 1,
                    min: min
                };
            }
        });

        const buyObj = {};

        GameRules.getVisibleMarketSeeds().forEach(function(seed) {
            let defaultCfg = { active: false, ignoreStockLimit: false };
            let currentCfg = MARKET_SETTINGS.buy[seed] || defaultCfg;

            let minInputEl = document.querySelector(`.buy-min[data-seed="${seed}"]`);
            let parsedMin = parseInt(minInputEl ? minInputEl.value : 10);
            let min = Math.max(1, parsedMin || 10);

            let maxInputEl = document.querySelector(`.buy-max[data-seed="${seed}"]`);
            let parsedMax = parseInt(maxInputEl ? maxInputEl.value : min);
            let safeMaxRaw = Math.max(1, parsedMax || min);
            let max = Math.max(min, safeMaxRaw);
            let activeEl = document.querySelector(`.buy-active[data-seed="${seed}"]`);
            let activeBuy = activeEl ? !!activeEl.checked : !!currentCfg.active;
            let riskEl = document.querySelector(`.buy-ignore-stock-limit[data-seed="${seed}"]`);
            let ignoreStockLimit = !!(riskEl && riskEl.checked);
            let autoEl = document.querySelector(`.buy-auto-shipment[data-seed="${seed}"]`);
            let autoShipmentRestock = !!(autoEl && autoEl.checked);

            if (activeBuy || ignoreStockLimit || autoShipmentRestock) {
                buyObj[seed] = {
                    active: activeBuy,
                    min: min,
                    max: max,
                    ignoreStockLimit: ignoreStockLimit,
                    autoShipmentRestock: autoShipmentRestock
                };
            }
        });

        let newMarketSettings = { sell: sellObj, buy: buyObj };
        MARKET_SETTINGS = normalizeMarketSettings(newMarketSettings);

        let stringifiedData = JSON.stringify(MARKET_SETTINGS);
        localStorage.setItem('sl_market_settings', stringifiedData);
    }

    _window.selectSellCrop = function(crop) {
        selectedSellCrop = selectedSellCrop === crop ? "" : crop;
        if (selectedSellCrop) {
            localStorage.setItem('sl_selected_sell_crop', selectedSellCrop);
        } else {
            localStorage.removeItem('sl_selected_sell_crop');
        }
        renderMarketTabs();
    };

    _window.toggleSellItem = function(crop) {
        _window.selectSellCrop(crop);
    };

    _window.toggleBuyItem = function(seed) {
        if (!ALL_KNOWN_SEEDS.includes(seed)) {
            log(`âš ï¸ ${seed} has unknown bot rules. Enable Risk and use manual buy only for testing.`);
            return;
        }

        if (!GameRules.isSeedInCurrentSeason(seed)) {
            log(`âš ï¸ ${seed} is not available in ${GameRules.getCurrentSeason()} season.`);
            return;
        }

        if (!GameRules.canBuySeed(seed)) {
            log(`âš ï¸ ${seed} is locked. Bumpkin level ${GameRules.getSeedLevelRequirement(seed)} required.`);
            return;
        }

        let defaultCfg = { active: false, min: 10, max: 20, ignoreStockLimit: false, autoShipmentRestock: false };
        let cfg = MARKET_SETTINGS.buy[seed] || defaultCfg;

        cfg.active = !cfg.active;
        MARKET_SETTINGS.buy[seed] = cfg;

        saveMarketSettings();
        renderMarketTabs();
    };

    _window.selectBuySeed = function(seed) {
        selectedBuySeed = selectedBuySeed === seed ? "" : seed;
        if (selectedBuySeed) {
            localStorage.setItem('sl_selected_buy_seed', selectedBuySeed);
        } else {
            localStorage.removeItem('sl_selected_buy_seed');
        }
        renderMarketTabs();
    };

    function applyShipmentRestockLocally(createdAtMs) {
        Object.keys(INITIAL_MARKET_STOCK).forEach(function(item) {
            let current = parseInt(SL_STOCK[item] || "0") || 0;
            let max = INITIAL_MARKET_STOCK[item] || current;
            let add = SHIPMENT_STOCK[item] || 0;
            SL_STOCK[item] = Math.min(max, current + add).toString();
        });
        SL_SHIPMENTS = { ...(SL_SHIPMENTS || {}), restockedAt: createdAtMs };
        modifyActivity("Shipment Restocked", 1);
        localStorage.setItem('sl_stock_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_STOCK));
        localStorage.setItem('sl_shipments_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_SHIPMENTS));
    }

    async function sendShipmentRestockIfFree() {
        if (!GameRules.canRestockShipment()) {
            return false;
        }
        if (!masterPayload || !SL_FARM_ID) {
            log("âš ï¸ Free shipment requires bot control first.");
            return false;
        }

        let payload = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(masterPayload));
        let createdAtMs = Date.now();
        payload.actions = [{ type: "shipment.restocked", createdAt: new Date(createdAtMs).toISOString() }];
        applyShipmentRestockLocally(createdAtMs);
        payload.stateHash.stock = await computeSHA256(SL_STOCK);
        payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
        if (payload.stateHash.shipments) {
            payload.stateHash.shipments = await computeSHA256(SL_SHIPMENTS);
        }

        let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: makeBotHeaders(),
            body: JSON.stringify(payload)
        });
        if (!res.ok) {
            triggerKillSwitch("Free shipment restock rejected.", res.status);
            return false;
        }
        masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
        log("âœ… Free shipment restock applied.");
        renderMarketTabs();
        return true;
    }

    async function runAutoShipmentRestockPhase(buyEntriesArr) {
        const candidates = (buyEntriesArr || []).filter(function(entry) {
            const cfg = entry && entry[1];
            return cfg && cfg.autoShipmentRestock;
        });

        if (candidates.length === 0 || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
            return false;
        }

        const picked = shuffleArray(candidates.slice())[0];
        const seed = picked ? picked[0] : "selected seed";

        await forceRadarRefresh('free shipment check');

        if (!GameRules.canRestockShipment()) {
            log(`ğŸ›’ Free shipment is on cooldown. Skipping auto limit boost this turn.`);
            return false;
        }

        log(`ğŸ›’ Auto Limit Boost picked ${seed}. Applying one free shipment restock...`);
        const ok = await sendShipmentRestockIfFree();
        if (ok) {
            await forceRadarRefresh('free shipment restock');
        }
        return ok;
    }

    async function sendSeedBuy(seed, amount, ignoreStockLimit) {
        if (!masterPayload || !SL_FARM_ID) {
            log("âš ï¸ Manual buy requires bot control first.");
            return false;
        }
        if (!ignoreStockLimit && (!ALL_KNOWN_SEEDS.includes(seed) || !GameRules.isSeedInCurrentSeason(seed) || !GameRules.canBuySeed(seed))) {
            log(`âš ï¸ ${seed} buy blocked by client rules.`);
            return false;
        }
        let stock = getAvailableStock(seed);
        if (!ignoreStockLimit) {
            if (!Number.isFinite(stock)) {
                log(`âš ï¸ ${seed} seed limit reached or stock is unknown. Enable Market Limit (Risk) to bypass.`);
                return false;
            }
            if (stock <= 0) {
                log(`âš ï¸ ${seed} seed limit reached. Buy skipped.`);
                return false;
            }
            amount = Math.min(amount, stock);
        }
        amount = Math.max(1, parseInt(amount) || 1);
        let seedInfo = getMarketSeedDetails(seed);
        let baseBuyPrice = Number.isFinite(parseFloat(seedInfo.price)) ? parseFloat(seedInfo.price) : (SEED_PRICES[seed] || defaultSeedPrices[seed] || 0.01);
        let price = calculateOraclePrice(seed, baseBuyPrice, "buy");
        let cost = price * amount;
        if (SL_COINS < cost) {
            log(`âš ï¸ Not enough coins for ${amount}x ${seed}. Required ${formatCoinAmount(cost)}.`);
            return false;
        }

        let payload = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(masterPayload));
        let createdAt = new Date().toISOString();
        payload.actions = [{ type: "seed.bought", item: seed, amount: amount, createdAt: createdAt }];
        modifyInventory(seed, amount);
        modifyActivity(seed + " Bought", amount);
        modifyActivity("Coins Spent", cost);
        modifyStock(seed, -amount);
        SL_COINS -= cost;
        payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
        payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
        payload.stateHash.stock = await computeSHA256(SL_STOCK);
        if (payload.stateHash.coins) {
            payload.stateHash.coins = await computeSHA256(SL_COINS);
        }
        lastBotMarketPrediction = { type: "buy", actions: [{ type: "seed.bought", item: seed, amount: amount }], coinsDelta: -cost, boosts: [] };

        let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: makeBotHeaders(),
            body: JSON.stringify(payload)
        });
        if (!res.ok) {
            triggerKillSwitch("Manual seed buy rejected.", res.status);
            return false;
        }
        masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
        log(`âœ… Manual buy completed: ${amount}x ${seed}`);
        renderMarketTabs();
        updateHud();
        return true;
    }

    _window.manualBuySelectedSeed = async function() {
        if (!selectedBuySeed) return;
        saveMarketSettings();
        let cfg = MARKET_SETTINGS.buy[selectedBuySeed] || {};
        if (cfg.autoShipmentRestock && GameRules.canRestockShipment()) {
            await sendShipmentRestockIfFree();
        }
        let input = document.getElementById('manual-buy-amount');
        let amount = parseInt(input ? input.value : 1) || 1;
        await sendSeedBuy(selectedBuySeed, amount, !!cfg.ignoreStockLimit);
    };

    function getBaitIcon(bait) {
        const text = String(bait || "").trim();
        return text.split(/\s+/).slice(0, 2).map(function(part) {
            return part.charAt(0).toUpperCase();
        }).join("") || "B";
    }

    function escapePanelText(value) {
        return String(value === undefined || value === null ? "" : value)
            .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
            .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
            .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
            .replace(/"/g, "&quot;")
            .replace(/'/g, "&#39;");
    }

    function getDiggingRewardName(cell) {
        const items = cell && cell.items ? cell.items : {};
        const names = Object.keys(items);
        return names.length ? names[0] : "";
    }

    function getDiggingCellMap() {
        const digging = SL_DESERT && SL_DESERT.digging ? SL_DESERT.digging : {};
        const grid = Array.isArray(digging.grid) ? digging.grid : [];
        return grid.reduce(function(map, cell) {
            if (!cell || cell.x === undefined || cell.y === undefined) {
                return map;
            }
            map[`${cell.x},${cell.y}`] = cell;
            return map;
        }, {});
    }

    function formatDiggingPattern(pattern) {
        return String(pattern || "")
            .replace(/^ARTEFACT_/, "Artefact ")
            .replace(/_/g, " ")
            .toLowerCase()
            .replace(/\b\w/g, function(letter) {
                return letter.toUpperCase();
            });
    }

    function renderDiggingMenu() {
        const statusEl = document.getElementById('digging-status-card');
        const gridEl = document.getElementById('digging-grid');
        const gridPanel = document.getElementById('digging-grid-panel');
        const buyPanel = document.getElementById('digging-buy-panel');
        const sellPanel = document.getElementById('digging-sell-panel');
        const patternsEl = document.getElementById('digging-patterns');
        const patternCountEl = document.getElementById('digging-pattern-count');
        const autoWrapper = document.getElementById('digging-auto-wrapper');
        if (!statusEl || !gridEl || !patternsEl || !gridPanel || !buyPanel || !sellPanel) {
            return;
        }

        DIGGING_SETTINGS.tab = DIGGING_SETTINGS.tab || "grid";
        DIGGING_SETTINGS.buy = DIGGING_SETTINGS.buy || {};
        DIGGING_SETTINGS.sell = DIGGING_SETTINGS.sell || {};
        const digging = SL_DESERT && SL_DESERT.digging ? SL_DESERT.digging : {};
        const grid = Array.isArray(digging.grid) ? digging.grid : [];
        const patterns = Array.isArray(digging.patterns) ? digging.patterns : [];
        const completed = Array.isArray(digging.completedPatterns) ? digging.completedPatterns : [];
        const extraDigs = parseInt(digging.extraDigs || 0, 10) || 0;
        const cellMap = getDiggingCellMap();
        const totalCells = 100;
        const digsLeft = Math.max(0, totalCells - grid.length) + extraDigs;
        const shovelCount = getInventoryAmount("Sand Shovel");
        const drillCount = getInventoryAmount("Sand Drill");

        statusEl.innerHTML = `
            <div class="digging-stat">
                <div class="digging-stat-label">Opened</div>
                <div class="digging-stat-value">${grid.length}/${totalCells}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="digging-stat">
                <div class="digging-stat-label">Tools</div>
                <div class="digging-stat-value">${shovelCount} shovel / ${drillCount} drill</div>
            </div>
            <div class="digging-stat">
                <div class="digging-stat-label">Digs Left</div>
                <div class="digging-stat-value">${digsLeft}</div>
            </div>
        `;

        ["grid", "buy", "sell"].forEach(function(tab) {
            const btn = document.getElementById(`digging-tab-${tab}`);
            if (btn) {
                btn.classList.toggle("active", DIGGING_SETTINGS.tab === tab);
            }
        });

        gridPanel.style.display = DIGGING_SETTINGS.tab === "grid" ? "block" : "none";
        buyPanel.style.display = DIGGING_SETTINGS.tab === "buy" ? "block" : "none";
        sellPanel.style.display = DIGGING_SETTINGS.tab === "sell" ? "block" : "none";
        if (autoWrapper) {
            autoWrapper.style.display = DIGGING_SETTINGS.tab === "grid" ? "flex" : "none";
        }

        let html = "";
        for (let y = 0; y < 10; y++) {
            for (let x = 0; x < 10; x++) {
                const key = `${x},${y}`;
                const cell = cellMap[key];
                const reward = getDiggingRewardName(cell);
                const rewardAmount = reward && cell.items ? readDecimal(cell.items[reward], 1) : 0;
                const rewardLabel = reward ? `${escapePanelText(reward)}${rewardAmount > 1 ? " x" + rewardAmount : ""}` : "";
                html += `
                    <div class="digging-cell ${cell ? 'dug' : ''}" title="${cell ? rewardLabel : 'Not dug'} (${x}, ${y})">
                        <span class="digging-coord">${x},${y}</span>
                        ${cell ? `
                            <div class="digging-reward">
                                <span class="digging-reward-icon">${getItemIconHtml(reward || 'treasure', 24)}</span>
                                <span class="digging-reward-name">${rewardLabel || 'Opened'}</span>
                            </div>
                        ` : `<span>.</span>`}
                    </div>
                `;
            }
        }
        gridEl.innerHTML = html;

        if (patternCountEl) {
            patternCountEl.textContent = `${patterns.length}`;
        }

        patternsEl.innerHTML = patterns.length ? patterns.map(function(pattern) {
            const done = completed.includes(pattern);
            return `<span class="digging-chip" style="${done ? 'border-color:rgba(34,197,94,0.45);color:#bbf7d0;' : ''}">${done ? 'Done: ' : ''}${escapePanelText(formatDiggingPattern(pattern))}</span>`;
        }).join("") : `<div class="mushroom-empty">No cached digging patterns yet.</div>`;

        const toolCards = Object.keys(TREASURE_TOOL_RULES).map(function(tool) {
            const rule = TREASURE_TOOL_RULES[tool];
            const status = canBuyTreasureTool(tool);
            const stock = getAvailableStock(tool);
            const cfg = getDiggingBuyConfig(tool);
            const target = getDiggingBuyTarget(tool);
            const have = getInventoryAmount(tool);
            const targetText = target > 0 ? `${have}/${target} target` : "no target";
            const ingredients = Object.keys(rule.ingredients).map(function(item) {
                return `${item} ${readDecimal(SL_INVENTORY[item], 0)}/${rule.ingredients[item]}`;
            }).join(" - ");
            return `
                <div class="bait-card ${cfg.active ? 'selected' : ''}" style="min-height:128px;" onclick="window.toggleDiggingBuyTool('${tool}')">
                    <div class="bait-icon">${getItemIconHtml(tool, 26)}</div>
                    <div class="bait-name">${tool}</div>
                    <div class="bait-count" title="Click to set target amount" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); window.setDiggingBuyTarget('${tool}')">${have} in bag / ${Number.isFinite(stock) ? stock : 0} stock<br>${targetText}</div>
                    <div class="panel-sub" style="margin:5px 0 7px 0;">${rule.price} coins<br>${escapePanelText(ingredients)}</div>
                    <button class="tiny-btn" style="width:100%;" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); window.buyDiggingTool('${tool}')">${status.ok ? 'Buy 1' : escapePanelText(status.reason)}</button>
                </div>
            `;
        }).join("");

        buyPanel.innerHTML = `
            <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;gap:10px;margin-bottom:9px;">
                <div>
                    <div class="panel-title" style="margin:0;">Treasure Tools</div>
                    <div class="panel-sub" style="margin:2px 0 0 0;">Auto Buy crafts one tool only when digging needs it.</div>
                </div>
                <div class="mini-switch-wrapper" title="Automatically buys selected digging tools up to target" onclick="window.toggleDiggingAutoBuy()">
                    <label class="switch" onclick="event.preventDefault(); event.stopPropagation(); window.toggleDiggingAutoBuy();">
                        <input type="checkbox" ${DIGGING_SETTINGS.autoBuy ? 'checked' : ''}>
                        <span class="slider"></span>
                    </label>
                    <span class="mini-label">Auto Buy</span>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="fishing-bait-grid">${toolCards}</div>
        `;

        const sellItems = Object.keys(DIGGING_SELL_PRICES);
        sellPanel.innerHTML = `
            <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;gap:10px;margin-bottom:9px;">
                <div>
                    <div class="panel-title" style="margin:0;">Treasure Sell</div>
                    <div class="panel-sub" style="margin:2px 0 0 0;">Select items. Auto Sell sends one selected item per turn.</div>
                </div>
                <div class="mini-switch-wrapper" title="Automatically sells one selected treasure per turn" onclick="window.toggleDiggingAutoSell()">
                    <label class="switch" onclick="event.preventDefault(); event.stopPropagation(); window.toggleDiggingAutoSell();">
                        <input type="checkbox" ${DIGGING_SETTINGS.autoSell ? 'checked' : ''}>
                        <span class="slider"></span>
                    </label>
                    <span class="mini-label">Auto Sell</span>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="fishing-bait-grid">${sellItems.map(function(item) {
                const amount = readDecimal(SL_INVENTORY[item], 0);
                const selected = !!DIGGING_SETTINGS.sell[item];
                return `
                    <div class="bait-card ${selected ? 'selected' : ''}" onclick="window.toggleDiggingSellItem('${item.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">
                        <div class="bait-icon">${getItemIconHtml(item, 26)}</div>
                        <div class="bait-name">${escapePanelText(item)}</div>
                        <div class="bait-count">${amount} in bag<br>${DIGGING_SELL_PRICES[item]} coins</div>
                        <button class="tiny-btn" style="width:100%;margin-top:6px;" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); window.sellDiggingItem('${item.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">Sell 1</button>
                    </div>
                `;
            }).join("")}</div>
        `;
    }

    function renderFishingMenu() {
        const statusEl = document.getElementById('fishing-status-card');
        const baitGrid = document.getElementById('fishing-bait-grid');
        const oddsBody = document.getElementById('fishing-odds-body');
        const logBody = document.getElementById('fishing-log-body');
        if (!statusEl || !baitGrid || !oddsBody || !logBody) {
            return;
        }

        const wharf = (SL_FISHING && SL_FISHING.wharf) ? SL_FISHING.wharf : {};
        const caughtNames = wharf.caught ? Object.keys(wharf.caught) : [];
        const reelsLeft = getFishingReelsLeft();
        const dailyInfo = getDailyFishingLimit();
        const selectedBaits = getSelectedFishingBaits();
        const rodCount = getInventoryAmount("Rod");
        const stateText = caughtNames.length > 0 ? `Caught: ${caughtNames.join(", ")}` : (wharf.castedAt ? "Waiting" : "Ready");

        statusEl.innerHTML = `
            <div class="fish-stat">
                <div class="fish-stat-label">Wharf</div>
                <div class="fish-stat-value">${stateText}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="fish-stat">
                <div class="fish-stat-label">Reels</div>
                <div class="fish-stat-value">${reelsLeft}/${dailyInfo.limit} left</div>
            </div>
            <div class="fish-stat">
                <div class="fish-stat-label">Rod</div>
                <div class="fish-stat-value">${rodCount} available</div>
            </div>
        `;

        baitGrid.innerHTML = FISHING_BAITS.map(function(bait) {
            const selected = !!(FISHING_SETTINGS.selected && FISHING_SETTINGS.selected[bait]);
            const count = readDecimal(SL_INVENTORY[bait], 0);
            const guaranteed = GUARANTEED_FISHING_BAITS[bait] ? "Guaranteed set" : "Random pool";
            const target = getFishingBaitTarget(bait);
            const casted = getFishingBaitCasted(bait);
            const targetText = target > 0 ? `${casted}/${target} target` : "unlimited";
            return `
                <div class="bait-card ${selected ? 'selected' : ''}" onclick="window.toggleFishingBait('${bait.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">
                    <div class="bait-icon">${getBaitIcon(bait)}</div>
                    <div class="bait-name">${bait}</div>
                    <div class="bait-count" title="Click to set target casts" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); window.setFishingBaitTarget('${bait.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">${count} in bag<br>${targetText}</div>
                    <div class="panel-sub" style="margin:5px 0 0 0;">${guaranteed}</div>
                </div>
            `;
        }).join("");

        const oddsArrow = document.getElementById('fishing-odds-arrow');
        const logArrow = document.getElementById('fishing-log-arrow');
        if (oddsArrow) oddsArrow.textContent = FISHING_ODDS_OPEN ? '^' : 'v';
        if (logArrow) logArrow.textContent = FISHING_LOG_OPEN ? '^' : 'v';

        oddsBody.className = `fishing-fold-body ${FISHING_ODDS_OPEN ? 'open' : ''}`;
        logBody.className = `fishing-fold-body ${FISHING_LOG_OPEN ? 'open' : ''}`;

        const guaranteedRows = Object.keys(GUARANTEED_FISHING_BAITS).map(function(bait) {
            return `<div style="margin-bottom:8px;"><b>${bait}</b><br>${GUARANTEED_FISHING_BAITS[bait].map(function(name) {
                return `<span class="fish-chip">${name}</span>`;
            }).join("")}</div>`;
        }).join("");

        const chumRows = Object.keys(FISHING_CHUM_AMOUNTS).slice(0, 24).map(function(item) {
            return `<span class="fish-chip">${item}: ${FISHING_CHUM_AMOUNTS[item]}</span>`;
        }).join("");

        oddsBody.innerHTML = `
            <div style="color:#bae6fd;font-weight:900;margin-bottom:6px;">Known client rules</div>
            <div>Normal bait sends only bait/multiplier/chum. Exact fish is decided by server response.</div>
            <div style="margin-top:8px;"><b>Selected order:</b> ${selectedBaits.length ? selectedBaits.join(" -> ") : "No bait selected"}</div>
            <div style="margin-top:10px;color:#fef3c7;font-weight:900;">Guaranteed bait pools</div>
            ${guaranteedRows}
            <div style="margin-top:10px;color:#d1fae5;font-weight:900;">Chum requirements sample</div>
            <div>${chumRows}</div>
        `;

        const catchNames = Object.keys(FISHING_CATCH_LOG).sort(function(a, b) {
            return (FISHING_CATCH_LOG[b] || 0) - (FISHING_CATCH_LOG[a] || 0);
        });
        logBody.innerHTML = catchNames.length ? catchNames.map(function(name) {
            return `<span class="fish-chip">${name}: ${FISHING_CATCH_LOG[name]}</span>`;
        }).join("") : `<div style="color:#94a3b8;">No bot catches recorded yet.</div>`;
    }
