    function renderForestAndMines() {
        let axeCount = getInventoryAmount("Axe");
        let pickaxeCount = getInventoryAmount("Pickaxe");
        let stonePickCount = getInventoryAmount("Stone Pickaxe");
        let ironPickCount = getInventoryAmount("Iron Pickaxe");
        let now = Date.now();

        let treeGrid = document.getElementById('grid-trees');
        if(treeGrid) {
            let treeHTML = "";
            let treeEntries = Object.entries(SL_TREES);
            for (let i = 0; i < treeEntries.length; i++) {
                let id = treeEntries[i][0];
                let t = treeEntries[i][1];
                let readyAt = getResourceReadyAt(t, TREE_RECOVERY_MS, "wood");
                let isReady = now >= readyAt;
                let leftText = formatTimeLeftMs(readyAt, now);
                let selected = isResourceSelected("trees", id);

                treeHTML += `
                    <div class="resource-box ${selected ? 'selected' : ''}" onclick="window.toggleResourceSelection('trees', '${id}')">
                        <div class="res-id">${id.substr(0,4)}</div>
                        <div class="res-icon">TREE</div>
                        <div class="res-tool">Axe: ${axeCount}</div>
                        <div class="res-status ${isReady ? 'ready' : 'wait'}">${isReady ? 'READY' : leftText}</div>
                    </div>
                `;
            }
            treeGrid.innerHTML = treeHTML || "No trees";
        }

        let stoneGrid = document.getElementById('grid-stones');
        if(stoneGrid) {
            let stoneHTML = "";
            let stoneEntries = Object.entries(SL_STONES);
            for (let i = 0; i < stoneEntries.length; i++) {
                let id = stoneEntries[i][0];
                let s = stoneEntries[i][1];
                let readyAt = getResourceReadyAt(s, STONE_RECOVERY_MS, "stone");
                let isReady = now >= readyAt;
                let leftText = formatTimeLeftMs(readyAt, now);
                let selected = isResourceSelected("stones", id);

                stoneHTML += `
                    <div class="resource-box ${selected ? 'selected' : ''}" onclick="window.toggleResourceSelection('stones', '${id}')">
                        <div class="res-id">${id.substr(0,4)}</div>
                        <div class="res-icon">STONE</div>
                        <div class="res-tool">Pickaxe: ${pickaxeCount}</div>
                        <div class="res-status ${isReady ? 'ready' : 'wait'}">${isReady ? 'READY' : leftText}</div>
                    </div>
                `;
            }
            stoneGrid.innerHTML = stoneHTML || "No stones";
        }

        let ironGrid = document.getElementById('grid-iron');
        if(ironGrid) {
            let ironHTML = "";
            let ironEntries = Object.entries(SL_IRON);
            for (let i = 0; i < ironEntries.length; i++) {
                let id = ironEntries[i][0];
                let iObj = ironEntries[i][1];
                let readyAt = getResourceReadyAt(iObj, IRON_RECOVERY_MS, "stone");
                let isReady = now >= readyAt;
                let leftText = formatTimeLeftMs(readyAt, now);
                let selected = isResourceSelected("iron", id);

                ironHTML += `
                    <div class="resource-box ${selected ? 'selected' : ''}" onclick="window.toggleResourceSelection('iron', '${id}')">
                        <div class="res-id">${id.substr(0,4)}</div>
                        <div class="res-icon">IRON</div>
                        <div class="res-tool">St. Pick: ${stonePickCount}</div>
                        <div class="res-status ${isReady ? 'ready' : 'wait'}">${isReady ? 'READY' : leftText}</div>
                    </div>
                `;
            }
            ironGrid.innerHTML = ironHTML || "No iron";
        }

        let goldGrid = document.getElementById('grid-gold');
        if(goldGrid) {
            let goldHTML = "";
            let goldEntries = Object.entries(SL_GOLD);
            for (let i = 0; i < goldEntries.length; i++) {
                let id = goldEntries[i][0];
                let g = goldEntries[i][1];
                let readyAt = getResourceReadyAt(g, GOLD_RECOVERY_MS, "stone");
                let isReady = now >= readyAt;
                let leftText = formatTimeLeftMs(readyAt, now);
                let selected = isResourceSelected("gold", id);

                goldHTML += `
                    <div class="resource-box ${selected ? 'selected' : ''}" onclick="window.toggleResourceSelection('gold', '${id}')">
                        <div class="res-id">${id.substr(0,4)}</div>
                        <div class="res-icon">GOLD</div>
                        <div class="res-tool">Iron Pick: ${ironPickCount}</div>
                        <div class="res-status ${isReady ? 'ready' : 'wait'}">${isReady ? 'READY' : leftText}</div>
                    </div>
                `;
            }
            goldGrid.innerHTML = goldHTML || "No gold";
        }
    }

    // ==========================================
    // ğŸ›¡ï¸ AÄ DÄ°NLEYÄ°CÄ°SÄ° & KATIK KURALLI YAPAY Ã–ÄRENME
    // ==========================================
    const origFetch = _window.fetch;

    _window.fetch = async function(...args) {
        let reqUrl = args[0];

        if (reqUrl && reqUrl.url) {
            reqUrl = reqUrl.url;
        } else if (!reqUrl) {
            reqUrl = "";
        }

        const options = args[1] || {};
        let requestHeaders = {};

        if (options && options.headers) {
            const h = {};
            if (options.headers instanceof Headers) {
                options.headers.forEach(function(v, k) {
                    h[k] = v;
                });
            } else {
                Object.assign(h, options.headers);
            }
            requestHeaders = h;

            if (h.authorization || h.Authorization) {
                rememberMasterHeaders(h);
            }
        }

        // Ä°stek Giderken Ã–ÄŸrenim Ä°Ã§in Kaydet
        let isAutosaveReq = reqUrl.includes('/autosave');
        if (isAutosaveReq && options && options.body) {
            try {
                const parsed = JSON.parse(options.body);
                if(parsed.actions) {
                    if (parsed.actions.length > 0) {
                        lastSentActions = parsed.actions;
                    }
                }
            } catch(e) {
                // Sessizce yoksay
            }
        }

        const res = await origFetch.apply(this, args);

        let isSessionReq = reqUrl.includes('/session');

        // PHOENIX RESET: Sayfa Yenilendikten Sonra Otomatik BaÅŸla
        if (_window.AUTO_RESUME_PENDING) {
            if (isSessionReq || isAutosaveReq) {
                try {
                    const cloneForId = res.clone();
                    const resData = await cloneForId.json();

                    if (resData.farmId || SL_FARM_ID) {
                        _window.AUTO_RESUME_PENDING = false;
                        localStorage.removeItem('sl_auto_resume');

                        log("âœ… BOT CHECKING... Automation is starting.");

                        let btn = document.getElementById('btn-start-auto');
                        if (btn) {
                            btn.innerText = "â¹ï¸ DURDUR";
                            btn.innerText = "Stop";
                            btn.style.background = "#52525b";
                        }

                        isBotRunning = true;
                        setTimeout(function() { runAutomationLogic(); }, 2000);
                    }
                } catch(e) {
                    // Sessiz
                }
            }
        }

        if (isSessionReq || isAutosaveReq) {
            await res.clone().json().then(function(data) {
                if (isSessionReq) {
                    LAST_SESSION_SNAPSHOT = data;
                }

                if (isAutosaveReq) {
                    LAST_AUTOSAVE_SNAPSHOT = data;
                    recordEyeRequest(reqUrl, options, requestHeaders, options && options.body, data, res.status);
                }

                if (data.farmHash) {
                    runFarmHashTTL(data.farmHash);
                }

                if (isSessionReq) {
                    localStorage.setItem('sl_last_session_refresh_at', Date.now().toString());
                    if (data.deviceTrackerId) {
                        if (masterPayload) {
                            masterPayload.deviceTrackerId = data.deviceTrackerId;
                            if (data.sessionId) {
                                masterPayload.sessionId = data.sessionId;
                            } else {
                                masterPayload.sessionId = "0x0";
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (data.farmId) {
                    SL_FARM_ID = data.farmId;
                    localStorage.setItem('sl_farm_id', SL_FARM_ID);
                }

                // KAHÄ°N Ä°Ã‡Ä°N EÅYA VE ETKÄ°NLÄ°K DATASI
                if (data.farm) {
                    if (data.farm.createdAt) {
                        SL_CREATED_AT = parseInt(data.farm.createdAt);
                        localStorage.setItem('sl_created_at_cache', SL_CREATED_AT.toString());
                    }
                    if (data.farm.bumpkin) {
                        SL_BUMPKIN = data.farm.bumpkin;
                        let stringifiedBumpkin = JSON.stringify(SL_BUMPKIN);
                        localStorage.setItem('sl_bumpkin_cache', stringifiedBumpkin);
                    }
                    if (data.farm.boostsUsedAt) {
                        SL_BOOSTS_USED_AT = data.farm.boostsUsedAt;
                        localStorage.setItem('sl_boosts_used_at_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_BOOSTS_USED_AT));
                    }
                    if (data.farm.events || data.farm.specialEvents) {
                        SL_EVENTS = data.farm.specialEvents || data.farm.events || {};
                        let stringifiedEvents = JSON.stringify(SL_EVENTS);
                        localStorage.setItem('sl_events_cache', stringifiedEvents);
                    }
                }

                // CHANGESET Ã–ÄRENÄ°MÄ°
                if (data.changeset) {
                    if (data.changeset.coins !== undefined) {
                        if (lastSentActions.length > 0) {
                            let coinDiff = parseFloat(data.changeset.coins);
                            let firstActionType = lastSentActions[0].type;

                            let isAllSold = true;
                            for (let i = 0; i < lastSentActions.length; i++) {
                                if (lastSentActions[i].type !== "crop.sold") {
                                    isAllSold = false;
                                    break;
                                }
                            }

                            let isAllBought = true;
                            for (let i = 0; i < lastSentActions.length; i++) {
                                if (lastSentActions[i].type !== "seed.bought") {
                                    isAllBought = false;
                                    break;
                                }
                            }

                            if (isAllSold) {
                                let firstCrop = lastSentActions[0].crop;
                                let isSingleCropType = true;

                                for (let i = 0; i < lastSentActions.length; i++) {
                                    if (lastSentActions[i].crop !== firstCrop) {
                                        isSingleCropType = false;
                                        break;
                                    }
                                }

                                if (isSingleCropType) {
                                    let totalAmount = 0;
                                    lastSentActions.forEach(function(a) {
                                        let parsedAmount = parseInt(a.amount || 1);
                                        totalAmount += parsedAmount;
                                    });

                                    if (totalAmount > 0) {
                                        let newPrice = coinDiff / totalAmount;
                                        if (newPrice > 0) {
                                            if (predictionsMatchActions(lastBotMarketPrediction, lastSentActions)) {
                                                let expectedDiff = lastBotMarketPrediction.coinsDelta;
                                                let diffGap = Math.abs(expectedDiff - coinDiff);
                                                let bonusText = "";
                                                if (lastBotMarketPrediction.boosts.length > 0) {
                                                    bonusText = " [" + lastBotMarketPrediction.boosts.join(", ") + "]";
                                                }

                                                if (diffGap < 0.0001) {
                                                    log(`âœ… [Price Check] Sell accounting matches response: ${formatCoinAmount(expectedDiff)} coin${bonusText}`);
                                                } else {
                                                    log(`âš ï¸ [Price Check] Sell accounting differs. Bot: ${formatCoinAmount(expectedDiff)} / Response: ${formatCoinAmount(coinDiff)}. Live price will be updated from response.`);
                                                }
                                            }

                                            CROP_SELL_PRICES[firstCrop] = newPrice;

                                            let stringifiedPrices = JSON.stringify(CROP_SELL_PRICES);
                                            localStorage.setItem('sl_live_sell_prices', stringifiedPrices);

                                            log(`ğŸ§  [Ã–ÄŸrenim] ${firstCrop} satÄ±ÅŸ fiyatÄ± canlÄ± gÃ¼ncellendi: ${newPrice.toFixed(4)}`);

                                            let marketMenu = document.getElementById('sl-market-menu');
                                            if (marketMenu && marketMenu.style.display === 'block') {
                                                renderMarketTabs();
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            } else if (isAllBought) {
                                let firstSeed = lastSentActions[0].item;
                                let isSingleSeedType = true;

                                for (let i = 0; i < lastSentActions.length; i++) {
                                    if (lastSentActions[i].item !== firstSeed) {
                                        isSingleSeedType = false;

                                    }
                                }

                                if (isSingleSeedType) {
                                    let totalAmount = 0;
                                    lastSentActions.forEach(function(a) {
                                        let parsedAmount = parseInt(a.amount || 1);
                                        totalAmount += parsedAmount;
                                    });

                                    if (totalAmount > 0) {
                                        let newPrice = Math.abs(coinDiff / totalAmount);
                                        if (newPrice > 0) {
                                            if (predictionsMatchActions(lastBotMarketPrediction, lastSentActions)) {
                                                let expectedDiff = lastBotMarketPrediction.coinsDelta;
                                                let diffGap = Math.abs(expectedDiff - coinDiff);

                                                if (diffGap < 0.0001) {
                                                    log(`âœ… [Fiyat Kontrol] AlÄ±ÅŸ hesabÄ± response ile uyuÅŸuyor: ${formatCoinAmount(Math.abs(expectedDiff))} coin`);
                                                } else {
                                                    log(`âš ï¸ [Fiyat Kontrol] AlÄ±ÅŸ hesabÄ± farklÄ±! Bot: ${formatCoinAmount(expectedDiff)} / Response: ${formatCoinAmount(coinDiff)}. CanlÄ± fiyat response'a gÃ¶re gÃ¼ncellenecek.`);
                                                }
                                            }

                                            SEED_PRICES[firstSeed] = newPrice;

                                            let stringifiedPrices = JSON.stringify(SEED_PRICES);
                                            localStorage.setItem('sl_live_seed_prices', stringifiedPrices);

                                            log(`ğŸ§  [Ã–ÄŸrenim] ${firstSeed} alÄ±ÅŸ fiyatÄ± canlÄ± gÃ¼ncellendi: ${newPrice.toFixed(4)}`);

                                            let marketMenu = document.getElementById('sl-market-menu');
                                            if (marketMenu && marketMenu.style.display === 'block') {
                                                renderMarketTabs();
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                // KUSURSUZ COIN GÃœNCELLEMESÄ°
                let updatedCoin = false;

                if (data.farm) {
                    if (data.farm.coins !== undefined) {
                        SL_COINS = parseFloat(data.farm.coins);
                        updatedCoin = true;
                    } else if (data.farm.balance !== undefined) {
                        SL_COINS = parseFloat(data.farm.balance);
                        updatedCoin = true;
                    }
                }

                if (updatedCoin) {
                    localStorage.setItem('sl_coins_cache', SL_COINS.toString());
                    let coinEl = document.getElementById('top-coin-info');
                    if(coinEl) {
                        coinEl.innerText = `${SL_COINS.toFixed(4)} coins`;
                    }
                }

                // KUSURSUZ Ã‡ANTA VE TARLA
                if (data.farm) {
                    if (data.farm.inventory) {
                        SL_INVENTORY = data.farm.inventory;
                        let stringifiedInv = JSON.stringify(SL_INVENTORY);
                        localStorage.setItem('sl_inventory_cache', stringifiedInv);
                    }
                    if (data.farm.crops) {
                        SL_CROPS = data.farm.crops;
                        let stringifiedCrops = JSON.stringify(SL_CROPS);
                        localStorage.setItem('sl_crops_cache', stringifiedCrops);
                        updateHud();
                    }
                    if (data.farm.farmActivity) {
                        SL_FARM_ACTIVITY = data.farm.farmActivity;
                        let stringifiedAct = JSON.stringify(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
                        localStorage.setItem('sl_activity_cache', stringifiedAct);
                    }
                    if (data.farm.stock) {
                        SL_STOCK = data.farm.stock;

                            log("âœ… Bot check completed. Refreshing safely...");

                                window.location.reload();
                            }, 500);
                    } else {
                        masterPayload = parsed;
                        let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(masterPayload);
                        localStorage.setItem('sl_master_payload', stringifiedPayload);
                        localStorage.setItem('sl_master_payload_at', Date.now().toString());
                    }
                }
            } catch(e) {
                // Åablon hatasÄ± sessizce yutulur
            }
        }

        return res;
    };

    function updateHud() {
        if(!SL_CROPS) {
            return;
        }

        let empty = 0;
        let growing = 0;
        let ready = 0;
        let quarantined = 0;

        let plotFilters = getSafeAndQuarantinedPlots();
        let quarantinedPlots = plotFilters.quarantined;

        let cropEntries = Object.entries(SL_CROPS);

        for (let i = 0; i < cropEntries.length; i++) {
            let id = cropEntries[i][0];
            let plot = cropEntries[i][1];

            if (quarantinedPlots.includes(id)) {
                quarantined++;
            } else {
                let status = getCropStatus(plot);
                if (status === "EMPTY") {
                    empty++;
                } else if (status === "GROWING") {
                    growing++;
                } else if (status === "READY") {
                    ready++;
                }
            }
        }

        let emptyType = empty > 0 ? 'ok' : 'err';
        let growingType = growing > 0 ? 'wait' : 'err';
        let readyType = ready > 0 ? 'ok' : 'err';
        let quarantineType = quarantined > 0 ? 'err' : 'ok';

        const el1 = document.getElementById('st-empty');
        if(el1) {
            el1.innerText = empty.toString();
            el1.className = emptyType;
        }

        const el2 = document.getElementById('st-growing');
        if(el2) {
            el2.innerText = growing.toString();
            el2.className = growingType;
        }

        const el3 = document.getElementById('st-ready');
        if(el3) {
            el3.innerText = ready.toString();
            el3.className = readyType;
        }

        const el4 = document.getElementById('st-quarantine');
        if(el4) {
            el4.innerText = quarantined.toString();
            el4.className = quarantineType;
        }

        const profileLevel = document.getElementById('profile-level');
        if (profileLevel) {
            profileLevel.innerText = `Level ${GameRules.getCurrentBumpkinLevel()}`;
        }

        const levelProgress = GameRules.getCurrentBumpkinLevelProgress();
        const profileXpBar = document.getElementById('profile-xp-bar');
        if (profileXpBar) {
            profileXpBar.style.width = `${levelProgress.percent}%`;
        }

        const profileXpText = document.getElementById('profile-xp-text');
        if (profileXpText) {
            profileXpText.innerText = `${levelProgress.current}/${levelProgress.needed} XP`;
        }

        const profileSeason = document.getElementById('profile-season');
        if (profileSeason) {
            profileSeason.innerText = GameRules.getCurrentSeason();
        }

        const profileCoin = document.getElementById('profile-coin');
        if (profileCoin) {
            profileCoin.innerText = `${SL_COINS.toFixed(4)} coins`;
        }
    }

    async function forceRadarRefresh(logReason = '') {
        if (!masterHeaders) { return false; }
        if (!SL_FARM_ID) { return false; }

        const nowMs = Date.now();
        const lastRefreshAt = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('sl_last_session_refresh_at') || "0");
        if (sessionRefreshPromise) {
            if (logReason) {
                log(`ğŸ“¡ Bot check already running; reusing it.`);
            }
            return await sessionRefreshPromise;
        }

        if (lastRefreshAt && nowMs - lastRefreshAt < SESSION_REFRESH_COOLDOWN_MS) {
            if (logReason) {
                log(`ğŸ“¡ Bot check skipped; fresh data already available.`);
            }
            return true;
        }

        if (logReason) {
            log(`ğŸ“¡ Bot checking...`);
        }

        sessionRefreshPromise = (async function() {
            try {
            const cachedPayload = masterPayload || JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sl_master_payload') || 'null') || {};
            let bodyData = {
                "clientVersion": cachedPayload.clientVersion || "2026-06-05T00:55",
                "timezone": "Europe/Istanbul",
                "language": "en"
            };

            let stringifiedBody = JSON.stringify(bodyData);

            const res = await _window.fetch('https://api.sunflower-land.com/session', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                body: stringifiedBody
            });

            if (res.ok) {
                localStorage.setItem('sl_last_session_refresh_at', Date.now().toString());
                if (logReason) {
                    log('âœ… Bot check completed.');
                }
                return true;
            } else {
                return false;
            }
            } catch(e) {
                return false;
            } finally {
                sessionRefreshPromise = null;
            }
        })();

        return await sessionRefreshPromise;
    }

    function refreshThenStopWithNotice(notice) {
        stopRequested = true;
        isBotRunning = false;
        killSwitchActivated = false;
        _window.WAITING_FOR_TEMPLATE_TO_START = false;
        localStorage.removeItem('sl_auto_resume');
        localStorage.setItem('sl_stop_notice', notice);

        const btn = document.getElementById('btn-start-auto');
        if (btn) {
            btn.innerText = "Start";
            btn.style.background = "linear-gradient(90deg,#b91c1c,#ef4444)";
        }

        log("ğŸ”„ Safety refresh started. Bot will stay stopped after refresh.");

        setTimeout(function() {
            window.location.reload();
        }, 1200);
    }

    function stableDebugJson(value) {
        const seen = new WeakSet();
        return JSON.stringify(value, function(key, val) {
            if (typeof val === "object" && val !== null) {
                if (seen.has(val)) {
                    return "[Circular]";
                }
                seen.add(val);
            }
            return val;
        }, 2);
    }

    function redactEyeHeaders(headers) {
        const out = {};
        Object.keys(headers || {}).forEach(function(key) {
            const lower = String(key).toLowerCase();
            if (lower.includes("authorization") || lower.includes("cookie") || lower.includes("token")) {
                out[key] = "[redacted]";
            } else {
                out[key] = headers[key];
            }
        });
        return out;
    }

    function makeEyeCurl(url, options, headers) {
        const parts = ["curl '" + String(url || "").replace(/'/g, "'\\''") + "'"];
        Object.keys(headers || {}).forEach(function(key) {
            parts.push("-H '" + key + ": " + String(headers[key]).replace(/'/g, "'\\''") + "'");
        });
        if (options && options.body) {
            parts.push("--data-raw '" + String(options.body).replace(/'/g, "'\\''") + "'");
        }
        return parts.join(" \\\n  ");
    }

    function getEyeActionSummary(body) {
        const actions = body && Array.isArray(body.actions) ? body.actions : [];
        return actions.map(function(action, index) {
            const out = {
                index: index + 1,
                type: action && action.type ? action.type : ""
            };
            ["item", "crop", "seed", "food", "resource", "amount", "buildingId", "createdAt"].forEach(function(key) {
                if (action && action[key] !== undefined) {
                    out[key] = action[key];
                }
            });
            if (action && action.index !== undefined) {
                out.fieldIndex = action.index;
            }
            return out;
        });
    }

    function formatEyeRecord(record, index) {
        return [
            "DATA " + (index + 1),
            "",
            "SUMMARY",
            stableDebugJson({
                at: record.at,
                method: record.method,
                status: record.status,
                url: record.url,
                actionCount: record.actionCount,
                actions: record.actions
            }),
            "",
            "CURL",
            record.curl,
            "",
            "BODY",
            stableDebugJson(record.body),
            "",
            "RESPONSE PREVIEW",
            stableDebugJson(record.responsePreview),
            "",
            "------------------------------------------------------------",
            ""
        ].join("\n");
    }

    function setEyeMode(active) {
        EYE_MODE_ACTIVE = !!active;
        localStorage.setItem('sl_eye_mode_active', EYE_MODE_ACTIVE ? 'true' : 'false');
        const btn = document.getElementById('btn-eye-mode');
        if (btn) {
            btn.innerText = EYE_MODE_ACTIVE ? "EYE MODE: ON" : "EYE MODE: OFF";
            btn.style.background = EYE_MODE_ACTIVE ? "linear-gradient(90deg,#16a34a,#22c55e)" : "linear-gradient(90deg,#475569,#64748b)";
        }
        if (EYE_MODE_ACTIVE) {
            EYE_RECORDS = [];
            log("Eye mode enabled. Manual autosave requests will be recorded.");
        }
    }

    async function sendEyeRecordsToPanel() {
        if (!EYE_RECORDS.length) {
            log("Eye mode disabled. No records collected.");
            return;
        }
        const files = {};
        for (let start = 0; start < EYE_RECORDS.length; start += 10) {
            const chunk = EYE_RECORDS.slice(start, start + 10);
            const header = [
                "NEXUS EYE DATA",
                "createdAt: " + new Date().toISOString(),
                "farmId: " + (SL_FARM_ID || ""),
                "count: " + chunk.length,
                ""
            ].join("\n");
            files["goz_" + (Math.floor(start / 10) + 1) + ".txt"] = header + chunk.map(formatEyeRecord).join("\n");
        }
        _window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("__NEXUS_DEBUG_FILES_READY__", {
            detail: {
                request_id: "eye_" + Date.now(),
                files: files
            }
        }));
        log("Eye records sent to server: " + Object.keys(files).join(", "));
        EYE_RECORDS = [];
    }

    async function toggleEyeMode() {
        if (EYE_MODE_ACTIVE) {
            setEyeMode(false);
            await sendEyeRecordsToPanel();
        } else {
            setEyeMode(true);
        }
    }

    function recordEyeRequest(url, options, headers, body, responseData, status) {
        if (!EYE_MODE_ACTIVE) {
            return;
        }
        const safeHeaders = redactEyeHeaders(headers || {});
        const parsedBody = (function() {
            try { return body ? JSON.parse(body) : null; } catch(e) { return body || null; }
        })();
        const item = {
            at: new Date().toISOString(),
            url: String(url || ""),
            method: String((options && options.method) || "GET"),
            status: status || null,
            curl: makeEyeCurl(url, options || {}, safeHeaders),
            headers: safeHeaders,
            actionCount: parsedBody && Array.isArray(parsedBody.actions) ? parsedBody.actions.length : 0,
            actions: getEyeActionSummary(parsedBody),
            body: parsedBody,
            responsePreview: responseData
        };
        EYE_RECORDS.push(item);
        if (EYE_RECORDS.length > 100) {
            EYE_RECORDS = EYE_RECORDS.slice(-100);
        }
        log("Eye captured autosave #" + EYE_RECORDS.length);
    }

    function cloneForDebug(value) {
        try {
            return JSON.parse(stableDebugJson(value));
        } catch(e) {
            return null;
        }
    }

    function countDebugKeys(value) {
        if (!value || typeof value !== "object") {
            return 0;
        }
        return Object.keys(value).length;
    }

    function getRedactedHeadersForDebug() {
        const source = masterHeaders || {};
        const redacted = {};
        Object.keys(source).forEach(function(key) {
            const lower = String(key).toLowerCase();
            if (lower.includes("authorization") || lower.includes("token") || lower.includes("cookie")) {
                redacted[key] = "[redacted]";
            } else {
                redacted[key] = source[key];
            }
        });
        return redacted;
    }

    function getLocalStorageDebug(keys) {
        const out = {};
        keys.forEach(function(key) {
            try {
                out[key] = localStorage.getItem(key);
            } catch(e) {
                out[key] = null;
            }
        });
        return out;
    }

    function sleepDebug(ms) {
        return new Promise(function(resolve) {
            setTimeout(resolve, ms);
        });
    }

    function findGameMotorScriptUrl() {
        try {
            const scripts = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll("script[src]")).map(function(script) {
                return script.src || "";
            }).filter(Boolean);
            const exact = scripts.filter(function(src) {
                return /\/assets\/index-[^\/]+\.js(?:\?|$)/.test(src) || /\/index-[^\/]+\.js(?:\?|$)/.test(src);
            });
            if (exact.length) {
                return exact[exact.length - 1];
            }
            const fallback = scripts.filter(function(src) {
                return src.includes("index-") && src.includes(".js");
            });
            return fallback.length ? fallback[fallback.length - 1] : "";
        } catch(e) {
            return "";
        }
    }

    async function fetchGameMotorFile() {
        return "// motor source export disabled\n// captured_at: " + new Date().toISOString() + "\n// note: use session.txt and sablon.txt for farm state/template diagnosis";
    }

    function getMasterPayloadCapturedAt() {
        return parseInt(localStorage.getItem("sl_master_payload_at") || "0", 10) || 0;
    }

    async function prepareDebugExportState(detail) {
        detail = detail || {};
        const requestCreatedAt = Number(detail.created_at || detail.createdAt || 0) || 0;
        const forceTemplate = !!detail.force_template;

        try {
            await forceSessionRefresh();
        } catch(e) {}

        if (forceTemplate && (!getMasterPayloadCapturedAt() || getMasterPayloadCapturedAt() < requestCreatedAt)) {
            masterPayload = null;
            try {
                localStorage.removeItem("sl_master_payload");
                localStorage.removeItem("sl_master_payload_at");
            } catch(e) {}
        }

        if (!masterPayload) {
            try {
                const cached = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("sl_master_payload") || "null");
                if (cached && (!forceTemplate || !requestCreatedAt || getMasterPayloadCapturedAt() >= requestCreatedAt)) {
                    masterPayload = cached;
                }
            } catch(e) {}
        }

        if (!masterPayload && !_window.WAITING_FOR_TEMPLATE_TO_START && !isBotRunning) {
            try {
                log("Panel dosya istedi. Bot template yakalama moduna alindi.");
                setTimeout(function() {
                    const btn = document.getElementById('btn-start-auto');
                    if (btn) {
                        btn.click();
                    } else {
                        toggleAutomation();
                    }
                }, 250);
            } catch(e) {
                _window.WAITING_FOR_TEMPLATE_TO_START = true;
            }
        }

        const startedAt = Date.now();
        while ((!LAST_SESSION_SNAPSHOT || !masterPayload) && Date.now() - startedAt < 25000) {
            await sleepDebug(500);
            if (!masterPayload) {
                try {
                    const cached = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("sl_master_payload") || "null");
                    if (cached && (!forceTemplate || !requestCreatedAt || getMasterPayloadCapturedAt() >= requestCreatedAt)) {
                        masterPayload = cached;
                    }
                } catch(e) {}
            }
        }
    }

    async function buildDebugFilesForPanel(requestId, detail) {
        await prepareDebugExportState(detail);

        const farmCaches = {
            farmId: SL_FARM_ID,
            inventory: cloneForDebug(SL_INVENTORY),
            crops: cloneForDebug(SL_CROPS),
            trees: cloneForDebug(SL_TREES),
            stones: cloneForDebug(SL_STONES),
            iron: cloneForDebug(SL_IRON),
            gold: cloneForDebug(SL_GOLD),
            mushrooms: cloneForDebug(SL_MUSHROOMS),
            fishing: cloneForDebug(SL_FISHING),
            desert: cloneForDebug(SL_DESERT),
            bumpkin: cloneForDebug(SL_BUMPKIN),
            buildings: cloneForDebug(SL_BUILDINGS),
            collectibles: cloneForDebug(SL_COLLECTIBLES),
            home: cloneForDebug(SL_HOME),
            interior: cloneForDebug(SL_INTERIOR),
            aoe: cloneForDebug(SL_AOE),
            buffs: cloneForDebug(SL_BUFFS),
            buds: cloneForDebug(SL_BUDS),
            stock: cloneForDebug(SL_STOCK),
            shipments: cloneForDebug(SL_SHIPMENTS),
            farmActivity: cloneForDebug(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY),
            season: cloneForDebug(SL_SEASON),
            calendar: cloneForDebug(SL_CALENDAR),
            island: cloneForDebug(SL_ISLAND),
            waterWell: cloneForDebug(SL_WATER_WELL)
        };

        const botDebug = {
            createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
            requestId: requestId || "",
            requestCreatedAt: Number((detail && (detail.created_at || detail.createdAt)) || 0) || null,
            farmId: SL_FARM_ID,
            waitingForTemplate: !!_window.WAITING_FOR_TEMPLATE_TO_START,
            botRunning: !!isBotRunning,
            hasMasterPayload: !!masterPayload,
            masterPayloadCapturedAt: getMasterPayloadCapturedAt() || null,
            motorScriptUrl: findGameMotorScriptUrl(),
            coins: SL_COINS,
            bumpkinLevel: (typeof GameRules !== "undefined" && GameRules.getCurrentBumpkinLevel) ? GameRules.getCurrentBumpkinLevel() : null,
            bumpkinExperience: SL_BUMPKIN && SL_BUMPKIN.experience,
            currentSeason: (typeof GameRules !== "undefined" && GameRules.getCurrentSeason) ? GameRules.getCurrentSeason() : null,
            headers: getRedactedHeadersForDebug(),
            botSettings: cloneForDebug(BOT_SETTINGS),
            plotTasks: cloneForDebug(PLOT_TASKS),
            resourceSelections: cloneForDebug(RESOURCE_SELECTIONS),
            counts: {
                inventory: countDebugKeys(SL_INVENTORY),
                crops: countDebugKeys(SL_CROPS),
                trees: countDebugKeys(SL_TREES),
                stones: countDebugKeys(SL_STONES),
                iron: countDebugKeys(SL_IRON),
                gold: countDebugKeys(SL_GOLD),
                mushrooms: countDebugKeys((SL_MUSHROOMS && SL_MUSHROOMS.mushrooms) || SL_MUSHROOMS),
                buildings: countDebugKeys(SL_BUILDINGS),
                collectibles: countDebugKeys(SL_COLLECTIBLES),
                buds: countDebugKeys(SL_BUDS)
            },
            caches: farmCaches,
            lastAutosave: cloneForDebug(LAST_AUTOSAVE_SNAPSHOT),
            localStorage: getLocalStorageDebug([
                "sl_farm_id",
                "sl_inventory_cache",
                "sl_crops_cache",
                "sl_trees_cache",
                "sl_stones_cache",
                "sl_iron_cache",
                "sl_gold_cache",
                "sl_bumpkin_cache",
                "sl_buildings_cache",
                "sl_collectibles_cache",
                "sl_mushrooms_cache",
                "sl_fishing_cache",
                "sl_desert_cache",
                "sl_master_payload",
                "sl_master_payload_at",
                "sl_master_headers",
                "sl_plot_tasks",
                "sl_resource_selections",
                "sl_bot_settings"
            ])
        };

        const session = {
            createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
            requestId: requestId || "",
            session: LAST_SESSION_SNAPSHOT || {
                note: "No live /session response captured yet. Using current bot caches.",
                farmId: SL_FARM_ID,
                farm: farmCaches
            },
            lastAutosave: cloneForDebug(LAST_AUTOSAVE_SNAPSHOT),
            botDebug: botDebug
        };

        let sablon = masterPayload;
        if (!sablon) {
            try {
                sablon = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("sl_master_payload") || "null");
            } catch(e) {
                sablon = null;
            }
        }

        return {
            "motor.txt": stableDebugJson(botDebug),
            "session.txt": stableDebugJson(session),
            "sablon.txt": stableDebugJson(sablon || {})
        };
    }

    async function sendDebugFilesToPanel(detail) {
        detail = detail || {};
        const requestId = detail.request_id || detail.requestId || "";
        try {
            if (!requestId) {
                log("Panel dosya istegi geldi ama request id yok.");
            }
            const files = await buildDebugFilesForPanel(requestId, detail);
            _window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("__NEXUS_DEBUG_FILES_READY__", {
                detail: {
                    request_id: requestId,
                    files: files
                }
            }));
            log("Debug dosyalari panele gonderildi.");
            return true;
        } catch(e) {
            log("Debug dosyalari hazirlanamadi: " + (e && e.message ? e.message : e));
            return false;
        }
    }

    if (!_window.__NEXUS_DEBUG_FILE_EXPORT_READY__) {
        _window.__NEXUS_DEBUG_FILE_EXPORT_READY__ = true;
        _window.__NEXUS_FORCE_DEBUG_EXPORT__ = sendDebugFilesToPanel;
        _window.addEventListener("__NEXUS_COLLECT_DEBUG_FILES__", async function(event) {
            const detail = event && event.detail ? event.detail : {};
            await sendDebugFilesToPanel(detail);
        });
    }

    function stopForMissingSelectedSeeds(seedNames) {
        const uniqueSeeds = Array.from(new Set((seedNames || []).filter(Boolean)));
        const seedText = uniqueSeeds.length ? uniqueSeeds.join(', ') : 'selected seed';
        refreshThenStopWithNotice(`ğŸ›‘ Bot stopped: selected field seed is out of stock (${seedText}). Add this seed to the Market buy list or change the field assignment, then press Start again.`);
    }

    function stopForInsufficientCoins(seed, requiredCoins) {
        refreshThenStopWithNotice(`ğŸ›‘ Bot stopped: insufficient coins to buy ${seed}. Required: ${formatCoinAmount(requiredCoins)} coin. Sell crops or lower the buy target, then press Start again.`);
    }

    // ==========================================
    // âš™ï¸ OTOMASYON MOTORU & KUSURSUZ DENETÃ‡Ä°
    // ==========================================
    async function toggleAutomation() {
        const btn = document.getElementById('btn-start-auto');

        if (isBotRunning || _window.WAITING_FOR_TEMPLATE_TO_START || killSwitchActivated) {
            stopRequested = true;
            isBotRunning = false;
            _window.WAITING_FOR_TEMPLATE_TO_START = false;
            killSwitchActivated = false;
            hasLoggedQuarantine = false;

            localStorage.removeItem('sl_master_payload');
            localStorage.removeItem('sl_master_payload_at');
            masterPayload = null;

            if (btn) {
                btn.innerText = "Start";
                btn.style.background = "linear-gradient(90deg,#b91c1c,#ef4444)";
            }
            log("Automation stopped. Memory cleared.");
        } else {
            stopRequested = false;
            killSwitchActivated = false;
            hasLoggedQuarantine = false;

            if (!masterPayload) {
                _window.WAITING_FOR_TEMPLATE_TO_START = true;
                if (btn) {
                    btn.innerText = "Waiting...";
                    btn.style.background = "#d97706";
                }
                log(`<span style="display:block; color:#fde047; font-weight:900; font-size:13px; text-align:center; letter-spacing:0.3px;">TO START THE BOT, PLEASE PLANT OR HARVEST ONCE.</span>`);
                return;
            }

            isBotRunning = true;
            if (btn) {
                btn.innerText = "Stop";
                btn.style.background = "#52525b";
            }
            log("Bot checking...");
            await forceRadarRefresh();
            if (stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                return;
            }
            log("âœ… Bot check completed. Starting automation.");
            runAutomationLogic();
        }
    }

    function getReadyMushroomEntries() {
        const source = SL_MUSHROOMS && SL_MUSHROOMS.mushrooms ? SL_MUSHROOMS.mushrooms : {};
        return Object.entries(source).filter(function(entry) {
            const mushroom = entry[1];
            return mushroom && mushroom.name && parseFloat(mushroom.amount || 0) > 0;
        });
    }

    function getReadyMushroomActions(startAtMs) {
        if (!BOT_SETTINGS.autoMushroom || !SL_MUSHROOMS || !SL_MUSHROOMS.mushrooms) {
            return [];
        }

        const entries = shuffleArray(getReadyMushroomEntries());
        let actions = [];
        let actionTime = Number.isFinite(startAtMs) ? startAtMs : Date.now();

        for (let i = 0; i < entries.length; i++) {
            const id = entries[i][0];
            const mushroom = SL_MUSHROOMS.mushrooms[id];
            if (!mushroom) {
                continue;
            }

            const amount = parseFloat(mushroom.amount || 0);
            const name = mushroom.name;

            actions.push({
                type: "mushroom.picked",
                id: id,
                createdAt: new Date(actionTime).toISOString()
            });

            modifyInventory(name, amount);
            delete SL_MUSHROOMS.mushrooms[id];
            actionTime += randInt(650, 1400);
        }

        if (actions.length > 0) {
            SL_MUSHROOMS_CACHE_AT = Date.now();
            localStorage.setItem('sl_mushrooms_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_MUSHROOMS));
            localStorage.setItem('sl_mushrooms_cache_at', SL_MUSHROOMS_CACHE_AT.toString());
        }

        return actions;
    }

    async function refreshCoreAccountingHashes(payload) {
        payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
        payload.stateHash.stock = await computeSHA256(SL_STOCK);
        payload.stateHash.coins = await computeSHA256(SL_COINS);
        payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
        payload.stateHash.trees = await computeSHA256(SL_TREES);
        payload.stateHash.stones = await computeSHA256(SL_STONES);
        payload.stateHash.iron = await computeSHA256(SL_IRON);
        payload.stateHash.gold = await computeSHA256(SL_GOLD);
        payload.stateHash.crops = await computeSHA256(SL_CROPS);
        payload.stateHash.mushrooms = await computeSHA256(SL_MUSHROOMS);
        await refreshVolatileStateHashes(payload);
    }

    function getReadyResourceTargets(type, source, recoveryMs, resourceKey) {
        const selectedEntries = getSelectedResourceEntries(type, source || {});
        const pool = selectedEntries.length > 0 ? selectedEntries : Object.entries(source || {});
        const ready = [];
        const now = Date.now();

        for (let i = 0; i < pool.length; i++) {
            const id = pool[i][0];
            const node = pool[i][1];
            if (now >= getResourceReadyAt(node, recoveryMs, resourceKey)) {
                ready.push([id, node]);
            }
        }

        const shuffled = shuffleArray(ready);
        return selectedEntries.length > 0 ? shuffled : shuffled.slice(0, 1);
    }

    function getCraftableToolAmount(tool, needed) {
        const recipe = CRAFTING_RECIPES[tool];
        if (!recipe || needed <= 0) {
            return 0;
        }

        let max = needed;
        Object.keys(recipe).forEach(function(item) {
            const cost = recipe[item];
            if (item === "coins") {
                max = Math.min(max, Math.floor(SL_COINS / cost));
            } else {
                max = Math.min(max, Math.floor(getInventoryAmount(item) / cost));
            }
        });

        const stock = Math.floor(parseFloat(SL_STOCK[tool] || 0));
        if (Number.isFinite(stock)) {
            max = Math.min(max, stock);
        }
        return Math.max(0, max);
    }

    function applyServerFarmSnapshot(data) {
        if (!data || !data.farm) {
            return;
        }
        const farm = data.farm;
        if (farm.inventory) {
            SL_INVENTORY = farm.inventory;
            localStorage.setItem('sl_inventory_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_INVENTORY));
        }
        if (farm.farmActivity) {
            SL_FARM_ACTIVITY = farm.farmActivity;
            localStorage.setItem('sl_activity_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY));
        }
        if (farm.stock) {
            SL_STOCK = farm.stock;
            localStorage.setItem('sl_stock_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_STOCK));
        }
        if (farm.coins !== undefined) {
            SL_COINS = parseFloat(farm.coins);
            localStorage.setItem('sl_coins_cache', SL_COINS.toString());
        }
        if (farm.boostsUsedAt) {
            SL_BOOSTS_USED_AT = farm.boostsUsedAt;
            localStorage.setItem('sl_boosts_used_at_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_BOOSTS_USED_AT));
        }
        if (farm.aoe) {
            SL_AOE = farm.aoe;
            localStorage.setItem('sl_aoe_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_AOE));
        }
        if (farm.trees) {
            SL_TREES = farm.trees;
            localStorage.setItem('sl_trees_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_TREES));
        }
        if (farm.stones) {
            SL_STONES = farm.stones;
            localStorage.setItem('sl_stones_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_STONES));
        }
        if (farm.iron) {
            SL_IRON = farm.iron;
            localStorage.setItem('sl_iron_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_IRON));
        }
        if (farm.gold) {
            SL_GOLD = farm.gold;
            localStorage.setItem('sl_gold_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_GOLD));
        }
        if (farm.crops) {
            SL_CROPS = farm.crops;
            localStorage.setItem('sl_crops_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_CROPS));
        }
        if (farm.mushrooms) {
            SL_MUSHROOMS = farm.mushrooms;
            SL_MUSHROOMS_CACHE_AT = Date.now();
            localStorage.setItem('sl_mushrooms_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_MUSHROOMS));
            localStorage.setItem('sl_mushrooms_cache_at', SL_MUSHROOMS_CACHE_AT.toString());
        }
    }

    async function sendBotResourcePayload(actions, reason) {
        if (!actions || actions.length === 0 || !masterPayload || !SL_FARM_ID) {
            return false;
        }

        const payload = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(masterPayload));
        payload.actions = actions;
        await refreshCoreAccountingHashes(payload);

        log(`ğŸ“¦ ${reason}: sending package... (${actions.length} action${actions.length > 1 ? "s" : ""})`);

        try {
            const res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                method: "POST",
                headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                body: JSON.stringify(payload)
            });

            if (res.ok) {
                try {
                    const data = await res.clone().json();
                    applyServerFarmSnapshot(data);
                } catch(e) {
                    // Response snapshot is best-effort; the fetch hook also learns it.
                }
                await refreshCoreAccountingHashes(payload);
                masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                log(`âœ… ${reason} package accepted.`);
                return true;
            }

            triggerKillSwitch(`${reason} rejected by server.`, res.status);
            return false;
        } catch(e) {
            triggerKillSwitch(`Network error (${reason}).`, "NETWORK");
            return false;
        }
    }

    async function craftToolBatch(tool, amount) {
        const qty = getCraftableToolAmount(tool, amount);
        if (qty <= 0) {
            return 0;
        }

        const recipe = CRAFTING_RECIPES[tool];
        const actions = [];
        let actionTime = beginBotActionBatch();
        for (let i = 0; i < qty; i++) {
            actions.push({
                type: "tool.crafted",
                tool: tool,
                amount: 1,
                createdAt: new Date(actionTime).toISOString()
            });
            actionTime = nextBotActionTime(actionTime);
        }

        modifyInventory(tool, qty);
        Object.keys(recipe).forEach(function(item) {
            const cost = recipe[item] * qty;
            if (item === "coins") {
                SL_COINS -= cost;
                modifyActivity("Coins Spent", cost);
            } else {
                modifyInventory(item, -cost);
            }
        });
        modifyActivity(tool + " Crafted", qty);
        modifyStock(tool, -qty);

        const ok = await sendBotResourcePayload(actions, `Blacksmith ${tool}`);
        return ok ? qty : 0;
    }

    async function runTreeBatchPhase() {
        if (!BOT_SETTINGS.autoTree || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
            return false;
        }

        const targets = getReadyResourceTargets("trees", SL_TREES, TREE_RECOVERY_MS, "wood");
        if (targets.length === 0) {
            return false;
        }

        let axeCount = getInventoryAmount("Axe");
        const neededAxes = targets.length;
        if (axeCount < neededAxes && BOT_SETTINGS.autoCraftAxe) {
            const crafted = await craftToolBatch("Axe", neededAxes - axeCount);
            if (crafted > 0) {
                axeCount += crafted;
                const keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch("blacksmith -> forest");
                if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) return true;
            }
        }

        const usable = Math.min(axeCount, targets.length);
        if (usable <= 0) {
            return false;
        }

        const actions = [];
        let actionTime = beginBotActionBatch();
        for (let i = 0; i < usable; i++) {
            const id = targets[i][0];
            actions.push({
                type: "timber.chopped",
                index: id,
                item: "Axe",
                createdAt: new Date(actionTime).toISOString()
            });
            modifyInventory("Axe", -1);
            modifyInventory("Wood", 1);
            modifyActivity("Tree Chopped", 1);
            modifyActivity("Basic Tree Chopped", 1);
            if (SL_TREES[id]) {
                SL_TREES[id].wood = { choppedAt: actionTime };
            }
            actionTime = nextBotActionTime(actionTime);
        }
        localStorage.setItem('sl_trees_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_TREES));

        const ok = await sendBotResourcePayload(actions, "Forest");
        if (ok) renderForestAndMines();
        return ok;
    }

    function getMiningRequirement(node) {
        return Math.max(1, Math.floor(parseFloat(node && node.multiplier || 1)));
    }

    async function runMiningBatchPhase(type, source, recoveryMs, resourceKey, tool, autoCraftFlag, actionType, rewardItem, activityName, cacheKey) {
        if (stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
            return false;
        }

        const targets = getReadyResourceTargets(type, source, recoveryMs, resourceKey);
        if (targets.length === 0) {
            return false;
        }

        let toolCount = getInventoryAmount(tool);
        let neededTools = 0;
        for (let i = 0; i < targets.length; i++) {
            neededTools += getMiningRequirement(targets[i][1]);
        }

        if (toolCount < neededTools && autoCraftFlag) {
            const crafted = await craftToolBatch(tool, neededTools - toolCount);
            if (crafted > 0) {
                toolCount += crafted;
                const keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch("blacksmith -> miner");
                if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) return true;
            }
        }

        const actions = [];
        let actionTime = beginBotActionBatch();
        for (let i = 0; i < targets.length; i++) {
            const id = targets[i][0];
            const node = targets[i][1];
            const required = getMiningRequirement(node);
            if (toolCount < required) {
                break;
            }

            actions.push({
                type: actionType,
                index: id,
                createdAt: new Date(actionTime).toISOString()
            });

            const amount = parseFloat(node && node.stone && node.stone.amount ? node.stone.amount : 1);
            modifyInventory(tool, -required);
            modifyInventory(rewardItem, amount);
            modifyActivity(activityName, required);
            modifyActivity((node && node.name ? node.name : rewardItem + " Rock") + " Mined", 1);
            toolCount -= required;

            if (source[id]) {
                source[id][resourceKey] = { minedAt: actionTime, boostedTime: 0 };
            }
            actionTime = nextBotActionTime(actionTime);
        }

        if (actions.length === 0) {
            return false;
        }

        localStorage.setItem(cacheKey, JSON.stringify(source));
        const ok = await sendBotResourcePayload(actions, `${rewardItem} miner`);
        if (ok) renderForestAndMines();
        return ok;
    }

    async function runResourceBatchPhase() {
        let didWork = false;

        if (BOT_SETTINGS.autoTree) {
            didWork = await runTreeBatchPhase() || didWork;
            if (didWork && (stopRequested || killSwitchActivated)) return didWork;
            if (didWork && (BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineStone || BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineIron || BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineGold)) {
                const keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch("forest -> miner");
                if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) return didWork;
            }
        }
        if (BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineStone) {
            const stoneDidWork = await runMiningBatchPhase("stones", SL_STONES, STONE_RECOVERY_MS, "stone", "Pickaxe", BOT_SETTINGS.autoCraftPickaxe, "stoneRock.mined", "Stone", "Stone Mined", "sl_stones_cache");
            didWork = stoneDidWork || didWork;
            if (didWork && (stopRequested || killSwitchActivated)) return didWork;
            if (stoneDidWork && (BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineIron || BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineGold)) {
                const keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch("stone miner -> ore miner");
                if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) return didWork;
            }
        }
        if (BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineIron) {
            const ironDidWork = await runMiningBatchPhase("iron", SL_IRON, IRON_RECOVERY_MS, "stone", "Stone Pickaxe", BOT_SETTINGS.autoCraftStonePick, "ironRock.mined", "Iron", "Iron Mined", "sl_iron_cache");
            didWork = ironDidWork || didWork;
            if (didWork && (stopRequested || killSwitchActivated)) return didWork;
            if (ironDidWork && BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineGold) {
                const keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch("iron miner -> gold miner");
                if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) return didWork;
            }
        }
        if (BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineGold) {
            didWork = await runMiningBatchPhase("gold", SL_GOLD, GOLD_RECOVERY_MS, "stone", "Iron Pickaxe", BOT_SETTINGS.autoCraftIronPick, "goldRock.mined", "Gold", "Gold Mined", "sl_gold_cache") || didWork;
        }

        return didWork;
    }

    async function refreshVolatileStateHashes(payload) {
        if (!payload || !payload.stateHash) {
            return;
        }
        if (payload.stateHash.fishing) {
            payload.stateHash.fishing = await computeSHA256(SL_FISHING);
        }
        if (payload.stateHash.desert) {
            payload.stateHash.desert = await computeSHA256(SL_DESERT);
        }
    }

    async function refreshFishingHash(payload) {
        if (payload.stateHash && payload.stateHash.fishing) {
            payload.stateHash.fishing = await computeSHA256(SL_FISHING);
        }
        payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
        payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
        if (payload.stateHash.boostsUsedAt) {
            payload.stateHash.boostsUsedAt = await computeSHA256(SL_BOOSTS_USED_AT);
        }
        await refreshVolatileStateHashes(payload);
    }

    function hasPendingFishingReel() {
        const wharf = SL_FISHING && SL_FISHING.wharf;
        if (!wharf || !wharf.caught) {
            return false;
        }
        return Object.keys(wharf.caught).some(function(name) {
            return parseFloat(wharf.caught[name] || 0) > 0;
        });
    }

    async function runFishingPhase() {
        if (!BOT_SETTINGS.autoFishing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
            return false;
        }
        if (!masterPayload || !SL_FARM_ID) {
            return false;
        }

        SL_FISHING = SL_FISHING || { wharf: {}, dailyAttempts: {}, extraReels: { count: 0 } };
        SL_FISHING.wharf = SL_FISHING.wharf || {};
        SL_FISHING.dailyAttempts = SL_FISHING.dailyAttempts || {};
        SL_FISHING.extraReels = SL_FISHING.extraReels || { count: 0 };

        const wharf = SL_FISHING.wharf;
        const caught = wharf.caught || {};
        const caughtNames = Object.keys(caught);

        if (caughtNames.length > 0) {
            let payload = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(masterPayload));
            payload.actions = [{ type: "rod.reeled", createdAt: new Date().toISOString() }];

            caughtNames.forEach(function(name) {
                const amount = parseFloat(caught[name] || 0);
                if (amount > 0) {
                    modifyInventory(name, amount);
                    modifyActivity(name + " Caught", amount);
                }
            });
            recordFishingCatch(caught);

            if (wharf.maps) {
                Object.keys(wharf.maps).forEach(function(name) {
                    modifyActivity(name + " Map Piece Found", parseFloat(wharf.maps[name] || 0));
                });
            }

            delete SL_FISHING.wharf.castedAt;
            delete SL_FISHING.wharf.caught;
            delete SL_FISHING.wharf.chum;
            delete SL_FISHING.wharf.multiplier;
            delete SL_FISHING.wharf.guaranteedCatch;
            delete SL_FISHING.wharf.maps;
            delete SL_FISHING.wharf.shrimpOnesieBonus;
            localStorage.setItem('sl_fishing_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_FISHING));

            await refreshFishingHash(payload);
            log(`ğŸ£ Reeling catch: ${caughtNames.join(", ")}`);

            try {
                let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                    body: JSON.stringify(payload)
                });
                if (!res.ok) {
                    triggerKillSwitch("Server rejected fishing reel.", res.status);
                    return false;
                }
                masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                renderFishingMenu();
                log(`âœ… Fishing reel completed.`);
                return true;
            } catch(e) {
                triggerKillSwitch("Network failed during fishing reel.", "NETWORK");
                return false;
            }
        }

        if (wharf.castedAt) {
            log("ğŸ£ Fishing cast is waiting for server catch state.");
            return false;
        }

        if (getFishingReelsLeft() <= 0) {
            log("ğŸ£ Fishing skipped: no reels left today.");
            return false;
        }

        const rodCost = getFishingRodCost(1);
        if (rodCost > 0 && readDecimal(SL_INVENTORY.Rod, 0) < rodCost) {
            log("ğŸ£ Fishing skipped: no Rod in inventory.");
            return false;
        }

        const bait = getNextFishingBait();
        if (!bait) {
            log("ğŸ£ Fishing skipped: no selected bait available.");
            return false;
        }

        let payload = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(masterPayload));
        const createdAtMs = Date.now();
        payload.actions = [{
            type: "rod.casted",
            bait: bait,
            multiplier: 1,
            createdAt: new Date(createdAtMs).toISOString()
        }];

        if (rodCost > 0) {
            modifyInventory("Rod", -rodCost);
        }
        modifyInventory(bait, -1);
        modifyActivity("Rod Casted", 1);
        const today = getTodayKey();
        SL_FISHING.dailyAttempts[today] = (parseInt(SL_FISHING.dailyAttempts[today] || 0, 10) || 0) + 1;
        SL_FISHING.wharf = {
            castedAt: createdAtMs,
            bait: bait,
            multiplier: 1
        };
        localStorage.setItem('sl_fishing_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_FISHING));

        await refreshFishingHash(payload);
        log(`ğŸ£ Casting rod with ${bait}...`);

        try {
            let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                body: JSON.stringify(payload)
            });
            if (!res.ok) {
                triggerKillSwitch("Server rejected fishing cast.", res.status);
                return false;
            }
            recordFishingBaitCast(bait);
            masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
            renderFishingMenu();
            log("âœ… Fishing cast sent. Catch will be read from response.");
            return true;
        } catch(e) {
            triggerKillSwitch("Network failed during fishing cast.", "NETWORK");
            return false;
        }
    }

    function applyTreasureToolBuyLocally(tool, amount) {
        const rule = getTreasureToolRule(tool);
        if (!rule) {
            return 0;
        }
        const qty = Math.max(1, parseInt(amount, 10) || 1);
        const ingredients = rule.ingredients || {};
        Object.keys(ingredients).forEach(function(item) {
            modifyInventory(item, -ingredients[item] * qty);
        });
        modifyInventory(tool, qty);
        modifyActivity(tool + " Crafted", qty);
        modifyActivity("Coins Spent", rule.price * qty);
        modifyStock(tool, -qty);
        SL_COINS -= rule.price * qty;
        return rule.price * qty;
    }

    async function sendTreasureToolBuy(tool, amount = 1, reason = "auto") {
        if (!masterPayload || !SL_FARM_ID) {
            log("Digging buy requires bot control first.");
            return false;
        }
        const status = canBuyTreasureTool(tool);
        if (!status.ok) {
            log(`Digging buy skipped: ${tool} - ${status.reason}.`);
            return false;
        }

        let payload = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(masterPayload));
        const qty = Math.max(1, parseInt(amount, 10) || 1);
        payload.actions = [{
            type: "tool.crafted",
            tool: tool,
            amount: qty,
            createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
        }];

        applyTreasureToolBuyLocally(tool, qty);
        payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
        payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
        payload.stateHash.stock = await computeSHA256(SL_STOCK);
        if (payload.stateHash.coins) {
            payload.stateHash.coins = await computeSHA256(SL_COINS);
        }

        log(`Digging ${reason}: buying ${qty}x ${tool}...`);
        try {
            let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                body: JSON.stringify(payload)
            });
            if (!res.ok) {
                triggerKillSwitch("Server rejected digging tool buy.", res.status);
                return false;
            }
            masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
            renderDiggingMenu();
            log(`Digging tool bought: ${tool}.`);
            return true;
        } catch(e) {
            triggerKillSwitch("Network failed during digging tool buy.", "NETWORK");
            return false;
        }
    }

    async function sendTreasureSell(item, amount = 1, reason = "auto") {
        if (!masterPayload || !SL_FARM_ID) {
            log("Digging sell requires bot control first.");
            return false;
        }
        if (!(item in DIGGING_SELL_PRICES)) {
            log(`Digging sell skipped: unknown item ${item}.`);
            return false;
        }
        const available = readDecimal(SL_INVENTORY[item], 0);
        const qty = Math.min(Math.max(1, parseInt(amount, 10) || 1), Math.floor(available));
        if (qty <= 0) {
            log(`Digging sell skipped: no ${item} in bag.`);
            return false;
        }

        let payload = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(masterPayload));
        payload.actions = [{
            type: "treasure.sold",
            item: item,
            amount: qty,
            createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
        }];

        const coinsEarned = DIGGING_SELL_PRICES[item] * qty;
        modifyInventory(item, -qty);
        modifyActivity(item + " Sold", qty);
        modifyActivity("Coins Earned", coinsEarned);
        SL_COINS += coinsEarned;
        payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
        payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
        if (payload.stateHash.coins) {
            payload.stateHash.coins = await computeSHA256(SL_COINS);
        }

        log(`Digging ${reason}: selling ${qty}x ${item}...`);
        try {
            let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                body: JSON.stringify(payload)
            });
            if (!res.ok) {
                triggerKillSwitch("Server rejected digging treasure sell.", res.status);
                return false;
            }
            masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
            renderDiggingMenu();
            log(`Digging treasure sold: ${item}.`);
            return true;
        } catch(e) {
            triggerKillSwitch("Network failed during digging treasure sell.", "NETWORK");
            return false;
        }
    }

    function getRandomUndugCell() {
        const dug = getDiggingCellMap();
        const cells = [];
        for (let y = 0; y < 10; y++) {
            for (let x = 0; x < 10; x++) {
                if (!dug[`${x},${y}`]) {
                    cells.push({ x: x, y: y });
                }
            }
        }
        return shuffleArray(cells)[0] || null;
    }

    async function sendDiggingAction() {
        if (!masterPayload || !SL_FARM_ID) {
            log("Digging requires bot control first.");
            return false;
        }
        if (getInventoryAmount("Sand Shovel") < 1) {
            log("Digging skipped: no Sand Shovel.");
            return false;
        }
        const cell = getRandomUndugCell();
        if (!cell) {
            log("Digging skipped: no cached empty grid cell left.");
            return false;
        }

        let payload = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(masterPayload));
        payload.actions = [{
            type: "desert.dug",
            x: cell.x,
            y: cell.y,
            createdAt: new Date().toISOString()
        }];

        log(`Digging: digging (${cell.x}, ${cell.y})...`);
        try {
            let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                body: JSON.stringify(payload)
            });
            if (!res.ok) {
                triggerKillSwitch("Server rejected desert dig.", res.status);
                return false;
            }
            payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
            payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
            if (payload.stateHash.desert) {
                payload.stateHash.desert = await computeSHA256(SL_DESERT);
            }
            masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
            renderDiggingMenu();
            log("Digging sent. Reward will be read from response.");
            return true;
        } catch(e) {
            triggerKillSwitch("Network failed during desert dig.", "NETWORK");
            return false;
        }
    }

    async function runDiggingPhase() {
        if (!BOT_SETTINGS.autoDigging || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
            return false;
        }

        if (getInventoryAmount("Sand Shovel") >= 1) {
            return await sendDiggingAction();
        }

        if (DIGGING_SETTINGS.autoBuy) {
            const toolToBuy = getNextDiggingToolToBuy();
            if (toolToBuy) {
                return await sendTreasureToolBuy(toolToBuy, 1, "auto buy");
            }
        }

        if (DIGGING_SETTINGS.autoSell) {
            const selected = Object.keys(DIGGING_SETTINGS.sell || {}).filter(function(item) {
                return DIGGING_SETTINGS.sell[item] && readDecimal(SL_INVENTORY[item], 0) > 0;
            });
            if (selected.length > 0) {
                return await sendTreasureSell(shuffleArray(selected)[0], 1, "auto sell");
            }
        }

        log("Digging auto idle: no shovel, no valid buy, no selected sell item.");
        return false;
    }

    async function runAutomationLogic() {
        if (stopRequested) {
            isBotRunning = false;
            return;
        }

        if (!masterPayload) {
            isBotRunning = false;
            return;
        }

        isBotRunning = true;

        let rulesOk = await GameRules.ensureClientRulesSafe();
        if (!rulesOk) {
            isBotRunning = false;
            return;
        }

        let accountingRisk = GameRules.getUnsupportedAccountingReason();
        if (accountingRisk) {
            triggerKillSwitch("Client motoru ile birebir olmayan kural tespit edildi: " + accountingRisk, "ACCOUNTING_GUARD");
            return;
        }

        // --- 0. KAHÄ°N GÃœVENLÄ°K TARAMASI ---
        let riskStatus = checkKillSwitchStatus();
        if (riskStatus) {
            triggerKillSwitch(riskStatus, "ORACLE");
            return;
        }

        let plotFilters = getSafeAndQuarantinedPlots();
        let safePlots = plotFilters.safe;
        let quarantinedPlots = plotFilters.quarantined;

        if (quarantinedPlots.length > 0 && !hasLoggedQuarantine) {
            log(`<span style="color:#f87171; font-weight:bold;">ğŸš§ Quarantine protocol: ${quarantinedPlots.length} unsafe field(s) detected and locked.</span>`);
            hasLoggedQuarantine = true;
        }

        let actionPerformed = false;
        let lastCompletedPhase = null;

        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated && BOT_SETTINGS.autoFishing && hasPendingFishingReel()) {
            log("Fishing reel is pending after refresh. Reeling before farm actions...");
            let fishingDidWork = await runFishingPhase();
            if (fishingDidWork) {
                actionPerformed = true;
                lastCompletedPhase = 'fishing';
                let keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch('fishing -> farm');
                if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                    return;
                }
            }
        }

        // ---------------------------------------------------------
        // 1. HASAT AÅAMASI (DÃœZELTÄ°LDÄ°: TEKLÄ° ONAY BEKLÄ°YOR)
        // ---------------------------------------------------------
        let cropEntries = BOT_SETTINGS.autoFields ? Object.entries(SL_CROPS) : [];
        let readyPlots = [];

        for (let i = 0; i < cropEntries.length; i++) {
            let id = cropEntries[i][0];
            let p = cropEntries[i][1];
            if (safePlots.includes(id) && getCropStatus(p) === "READY") {
                readyPlots.push(id);
            }
        }
        readyPlots = shuffleArray(readyPlots);

        if (readyPlots.length > 0 && !stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
            let nowMs = Date.now();
            let harvestWindowMs = 60000;
            let waitForNearbyMs = 0;

            for (let i = 0; i < cropEntries.length; i++) {
                let id = cropEntries[i][0];
                let p = cropEntries[i][1];

                if (!safePlots.includes(id) || readyPlots.includes(id) || getCropStatus(p) !== "GROWING") {
                    continue;
                }

                let readyAt = getCropReadyAt(p);
                let remainingMs = readyAt - nowMs;

                if (remainingMs > 0 && remainingMs <= harvestWindowMs) {
                    waitForNearbyMs = Math.max(waitForNearbyMs, remainingMs);
                }
            }

            if (waitForNearbyMs > 0) {
                let waitMs = waitForNearbyMs + randInt(700, 1800);
                let waitSecs = Math.ceil(waitMs / 1000);
                log(`Harvest window: a crop matures within 1 minute. Waiting ${waitSecs}s for batch harvest.`);

                let keepGoing = await controlledSleep(waitMs);
                if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                    return;
                }

                cropEntries = Object.entries(SL_CROPS);
                readyPlots = [];

                for (let i = 0; i < cropEntries.length; i++) {
                    let id = cropEntries[i][0];
                    let p = cropEntries[i][1];
                    if (safePlots.includes(id) && getCropStatus(p) === "READY") {
                        readyPlots.push(id);
                    }
                }
                readyPlots = shuffleArray(readyPlots);
            }
        }

        if (readyPlots.length > 0 && !stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
            actionPerformed = true;
            let isHarvestBatch = BOT_SETTINGS.harvestMax <= 4500;

            let modText = isHarvestBatch ? 'Batch' : 'Single';
            log(`ğŸŒ¾ Harvest starting... (${readyPlots.length} fields) [Mode: ${modText}]`);

            let stringifiedMaster = JSON.stringify(masterPayload);
            let payload = JSON.parse(stringifiedMaster);
            payload.actions = [];
            let mushroomActions = [];

            for (let i = 0; i < readyPlots.length; i++) {
                if (stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                    break;
                }

                let plotId = readyPlots[i];
                let cropName = null;

                if (SL_CROPS[plotId] && SL_CROPS[plotId].crop) {
                    cropName = SL_CROPS[plotId].crop.name;
                }

                let dateIso = new Date().toISOString();

                payload.actions.push({
                    type: "crop.harvested",
                    index: plotId,
                    createdAt: dateIso
                });

                if (cropName) {
                    modifyInventory(cropName, 1);
                    let actName = cropName + " Harvested";
                    modifyActivity(actName, 1);
                }
