                if (SL_CROPS[plotId]) {
                    delete SL_CROPS[plotId].crop;
                    let stringifiedCrops = JSON.stringify(SL_CROPS);
                    localStorage.setItem('sl_crops_cache', stringifiedCrops);
                }

                if (typeof renderPlotGrid === 'function') {
                    renderPlotGrid();
                }

                if (!isHarvestBatch) {
                    payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
                    payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
                    payload.stateHash.crops = await computeSHA256(SL_CROPS);
                    await refreshVolatileStateHashes(payload);

                    log(`ğŸ“¦ [Single] Sending harvest...`);

                    try {
                        let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(payload);
                        let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                            method: 'POST',
                            headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                            body: stringifiedPayload
                        });

                        if (res.ok) {
                            log(`âœ… Ä°ÅŸlem BaÅŸarÄ±lÄ±!`);
                            masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                        } else {
                            triggerKillSwitch("Sunucu tekli hasadÄ± reddetti.", res.status);
                            return;
                        }
                    } catch(e) {
                        triggerKillSwitch("AÄŸ baÄŸlantÄ±sÄ± koptu (Hasat).", "NETWORK");
                        return;
                    }
                    payload.actions = [];
                }

                if (i < readyPlots.length - 1) {
                    let waitMs = randInt(BOT_SETTINGS.harvestMin, BOT_SETTINGS.harvestMax);
                    await controlledSleep(waitMs);
                }
            }

            if (isHarvestBatch) {
                if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
                    mushroomActions = getReadyMushroomActions(Date.now() + randInt(450, 1300));
                    if (mushroomActions.length > 0) {
                        payload.actions = payload.actions.concat(mushroomActions);
                        log(`Collect Mushrooms added after harvest actions... (${mushroomActions.length})`);
                    }
                }

                if (payload.actions.length > 0) {
                    if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
                        payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
                        payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
                        payload.stateHash.crops = await computeSHA256(SL_CROPS);
                        await refreshVolatileStateHashes(payload);
                        if (payload.stateHash.mushrooms || mushroomActions.length > 0) {
                            payload.stateHash.mushrooms = await computeSHA256(SL_MUSHROOMS);
                        }

                        log(`ğŸ“¦ [Toplu Paket] Hasat sepeti fÄ±rlatÄ±lÄ±yor... (${payload.actions.length} eylem)`);

                        try {
                            let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(payload);
                            let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                                method: 'POST',
                                headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                                body: stringifiedPayload
                            });

                            if (res.ok) {
                                log(`âœ… Ä°ÅŸlem BaÅŸarÄ±lÄ±!`);
                                masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                            } else {
                                triggerKillSwitch("Sunucu toplu hasadÄ± reddetti.", res.status);
                                return;
                            }
                        } catch(e) {
                            triggerKillSwitch("AÄŸ baÄŸlantÄ±sÄ± koptu (Toplu Hasat).", "NETWORK");
                            return;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        if (actionPerformed && !stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
            lastCompletedPhase = 'harvest';
        }

        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
            if (lastCompletedPhase === 'harvest' && hasCookingWorkPending()) {
                let keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch('hasat â†’ fire pit');
                if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                    return;
                }
            }

            let cookedSomething = await runCookingAutomationPhase();
            if (cookedSomething) {
                actionPerformed = true;
                lastCompletedPhase = 'firepit';
            }
        }

        let sellEntriesArr = Object.entries(MARKET_SETTINGS.sell || {});
        let hasSellTargets = false;
        for (let i = 0; i < sellEntriesArr.length; i++) {
            if (sellEntriesArr[i][1] && sellEntriesArr[i][1].active) {
                hasSellTargets = true;
                break;
            }
        }

        let buyEntriesArr = Object.entries(MARKET_SETTINGS.buy || {});
        let hasBuyTargets = false;
        for (let i = 0; i < buyEntriesArr.length; i++) {
            if (buyEntriesArr[i][1] && buyEntriesArr[i][1].active) {
                hasBuyTargets = true;
                break;
            }
        }

        let plotTaskKeys = Object.keys(PLOT_TASKS || {});
        let hasPlotTasks = BOT_SETTINGS.autoFields && plotTaskKeys.length > 0;

        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
            if (actionPerformed) {
                if (hasSellTargets || hasBuyTargets || hasPlotTasks) {
                    let fromPhaseName = lastCompletedPhase === 'firepit' ? 'fire pit' : 'hasat';
                    let nextPhaseName = hasSellTargets ? 'satÄ±ÅŸ' : (hasBuyTargets ? 'alÄ±ÅŸ' : 'ekim');
                    let transitionName = fromPhaseName + ' â†’ ' + nextPhaseName;
                    let keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch(transitionName);
                    if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                        return;
                    }
                }
            }

        }

        // ---------------------------------------------------------
        // 2. SATIÅ AÅAMASI
        // ---------------------------------------------------------
        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
            let activeSells = [];

            for (let i = 0; i < sellEntriesArr.length; i++) {
                if (sellEntriesArr[i][1] && sellEntriesArr[i][1].active) {
                    activeSells.push(sellEntriesArr[i]);
                }
            }

            if (activeSells.length > 0) {
                let salePayloadsSent = 0;

                for (let i = 0; i < activeSells.length; i++) {
                    let crop = activeSells[i][0];
                    let cfg = activeSells[i][1];
                    let amt = parseInt(SL_INVENTORY[crop] || "0");

                    let minNeed = 1;
                    if (cfg && cfg.minEnabled) {
                        let parsedMin = parseInt(cfg.min || 1);
                        minNeed = Math.max(1, parsedMin);
                    }

                    if (amt >= minNeed) {
                        let reservedForCooking = getCookingReservedIngredients()[crop] || 0;
                        if (reservedForCooking > 0) {
                            amt = Math.max(0, amt - reservedForCooking);
                        }

                        if (amt < minNeed) {
                            if (reservedForCooking > 0) {
                                log(`ğŸ² ${crop} Fire Pit icin saklandi (${reservedForCooking} adet). Satis atlandi.`);
                            }
                            continue;
                        }

                        let dateIso = new Date().toISOString();

                        let sellAction = {
                            type: "crop.sold",
                            crop: crop,
                            amount: amt.toString(),
                            createdAt: dateIso
                        };

                        let basePrice = CROP_SELL_PRICES[crop] || defaultSellPrices[crop] || 0.02;
                        let priceInfo = calculateClientSellPrice(crop, basePrice, dateIso);
                        let cropPrice = priceInfo.price;
                        let kazanc = amt * cropPrice;
                        let sellBoostsUsed = [];

                        if (priceInfo.boosts.length > 0) {
                            priceInfo.boosts.forEach(function(boostName) {
                                if (!sellBoostsUsed.includes(boostName)) {
                                    sellBoostsUsed.push(boostName);
                                }
                            });
                        }

                        let sellPredictedAction = {
                            type: "crop.sold",
                            crop: crop,
                            amount: amt.toString()
                        };

                        modifyInventory(crop, -amt);
                        let actName = crop + " Sold";
                        modifyActivity(actName, amt);
                        modifyActivity("Coins Earned", kazanc);

                        actionPerformed = true;
                        log(`Sale preparing: ${amt}x ${crop}`);

                        let stringifiedMaster = JSON.stringify(masterPayload);
                        let payload = JSON.parse(stringifiedMaster);
                        payload.actions = [sellAction];

                        SL_COINS += kazanc;
                        lastBotMarketPrediction = {
                            type: "sell",
                            actions: [sellPredictedAction],
                            coinsDelta: kazanc,
                            boosts: sellBoostsUsed
                        };

                        payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
                        payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
                        if (payload.stateHash.coins) {
                            payload.stateHash.coins = await computeSHA256(SL_COINS);
                        }
                        await refreshVolatileStateHashes(payload);

                        log(`Sending sale payload... (${amt}x ${crop})`);

                        try {
                            let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(payload);
                            let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                                method: 'POST',
                                headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                                body: stringifiedPayload
                            });

                            if (res.ok) {
                                log(`Sale completed.`);
                                masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                                refreshBuyBudgetLocks();
                                lastCompletedPhase = 'sell';
                                salePayloadsSent++;
                            } else {
                                triggerKillSwitch("Sunucu satÃ„Â±Ã…Å¸Ã„Â± reddetti.", res.status);
                                return;
                            }
                        } catch(e) {
                            triggerKillSwitch("AÃ„Å¸ baÃ„Å¸lantÃ„Â±sÃ„Â± koptu (SatÃ„Â±Ã…Å¸).", "NETWORK");
                            return;
                        }

                        if (salePayloadsSent > 0 && i < activeSells.length - 1) {
                            let keepGoing = await controlledSleep(randInt(900, 1800));
                            if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                                return;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (false && sellActions.length > 0) {
                    actionPerformed = true;
                    let joinedInfo = soldInfo.join(", ");
                    log(`ğŸ’° Preparing sell basket: ${joinedInfo}`);

                    let stringifiedMaster = JSON.stringify(masterPayload);
                    let payload = JSON.parse(stringifiedMaster);

                    payload.actions = sellActions;
                    SL_COINS += coinsEarned;
                    lastBotMarketPrediction = {
                        type: "sell",
                        actions: sellPredictedActions,
                        coinsDelta: coinsEarned,
                        boosts: sellBoostsUsed
                    };

                    payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
                    payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
                    if (payload.stateHash.coins) {
                        payload.stateHash.coins = await computeSHA256(SL_COINS);
                    }

                    log(`ğŸ“¦ Sending sell payload...`);

                    try {
                        let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(payload);
                        let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                            method: 'POST',
                            headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                            body: stringifiedPayload
                        });

                    if (res.ok) {
                        log(`âœ… Ä°ÅŸlem BaÅŸarÄ±lÄ±!`);
                        masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                        refreshBuyBudgetLocks();
                        lastCompletedPhase = 'sell';
                    } else {
                        triggerKillSwitch("Server rejected sell action.", res.status);
                        return;
                    }
                    } catch(e) {
                        triggerKillSwitch("Network connection lost (Sell).", "NETWORK");
                        return;
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
            if (lastCompletedPhase === 'sell') {
                if (hasBuyTargets || hasPlotTasks) {
                    let nextPhaseName = hasBuyTargets ? 'alÄ±ÅŸ' : 'ekim';
                    let keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch('satÄ±ÅŸ â†’ ' + nextPhaseName);
                    if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                        return;
                    }
                }
            }

        }

        // ---------------------------------------------------------
        // 3. SATIN ALMA AÅAMASI
        // ---------------------------------------------------------
        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
            refreshBuyBudgetLocks();

            let activeBuys = [];

            for (let i = 0; i < buyEntriesArr.length; i++) {
                if (buyEntriesArr[i][1] && buyEntriesArr[i][1].active) {
                    activeBuys.push(buyEntriesArr[i]);
                }
            }

            let restockedShipment = await runAutoShipmentRestockPhase(buyEntriesArr);
            if (restockedShipment) {
                actionPerformed = true;
                lastCompletedPhase = 'buy';
            }

            if (activeBuys.length > 0) {
                let buyActions = [];
                let coinsSpent = 0;
                let buyPredictedActions = [];
                let chunksToProcess = [];
                let currentBudget = SL_COINS;

                for (let i = 0; i < activeBuys.length; i++) {
                    let seed = activeBuys[i][0];
                    let cfg = activeBuys[i][1];
                    if (!GameRules.isSeedInCurrentSeason(seed)) {
                        log(`âš ï¸ ${seed} buy skipped: not available in ${GameRules.getCurrentSeason()} season.`);
                        continue;
                    }

                    if (!GameRules.canBuySeed(seed)) {
                        log(`âš ï¸ ${seed} buy skipped: Bumpkin level ${GameRules.getSeedLevelRequirement(seed)} required.`);
                        continue;
                    }

                    let current = parseInt(SL_INVENTORY[seed] || "0");

                    let lockedBudget = parseFloat(buyBudgetLocks[seed] || 0);
                    if (lockedBudget > 0) {
                        if (SL_COINS < lockedBudget) {
                            continue;
                        }

                        clearBuyBudgetLock(seed);
                    }

                    let parsedMin = parseInt(cfg.min || 1);
                    let min = Math.max(1, parsedMin);

                    let parsedMax = parseInt(cfg.max || min);
                    let max = Math.max(min, parsedMax);

                    if (current < min) {
                        let target = randInt(min, max);
                        let needed = Math.max(0, target - current);

                        if (needed > 0) {
                            let ignoreStockLimit = !!cfg.ignoreStockLimit;
                            let availableStock = ignoreStockLimit ? Infinity : getAvailableStock(seed);
                            if (ignoreStockLimit) {
                                log(`âš ï¸ ${seed} market limit bypass is ON (Risk). Stock cap ignored.`);
                            }
                            if (!ignoreStockLimit && cfg.autoShipmentRestock && Number.isFinite(availableStock) && availableStock < needed && GameRules.canRestockShipment()) {
                                log(`ğŸ›’ Free shipment restock is ready. Boosting market limit before buying ${seed}.`);
                                let restocked = await sendShipmentRestockIfFree();
                                if (restocked) {
                                    availableStock = getAvailableStock(seed);
                                }
                            }
                            if (!ignoreStockLimit && !Number.isFinite(availableStock)) {
                                log(`âš ï¸ ${seed} seed limit reached or stock is unknown. Enable Market Limit (Risk) to buy.`);
                                continue;
                            }
                            if (availableStock <= 0) {
                                log(`âš ï¸ ${seed} seed limit reached. Buy skipped.`);
                                continue;
                            }

                            if (Number.isFinite(availableStock) && needed > availableStock) {
                                log(`âš ï¸ ${seed} market stock limit: ${availableStock}. Buy amount capped.`);
                            }

                            let chunks = buildBuyChunks(needed, availableStock);
                            for (let j = 0; j < chunks.length; j++) {
                                let c = chunks[j];
                                chunksToProcess.push({ seed: seed, amount: c });
                            }
                        }
                    } else {
                        exhaustedSeedWarnings.delete(seed);
                    }
                }

                if (chunksToProcess.length > 0) {
                    actionPerformed = true;
                    log(`ğŸ›’ Fast buy starting... (Budget guard active)`);

                    for (let i = 0; i < chunksToProcess.length; i++) {
                        if (stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                            break;
                        }

                        let item = chunksToProcess[i];
                        let basePrice = SEED_PRICES[item.seed] || defaultSeedPrices[item.seed] || 0.01;
                        let knownPrice = calculateOraclePrice(item.seed, basePrice, "buy");
                        let masraf = item.amount * knownPrice;

                        if (currentBudget < masraf) {
                            let requestedAmount = item.amount;
                            let maxAffordable = Math.floor(currentBudget / knownPrice);
                            if (maxAffordable > 0) {
                                item.amount = maxAffordable;
                                masraf = item.amount * knownPrice;
                                let remainingAmount = requestedAmount - maxAffordable;
                                if (remainingAmount > 0) {
                                    rememberBuyBudgetLock(item.seed, remainingAmount * knownPrice);
                                }
                                log(`âš ï¸ BÃ¼tÃ§e yetersiz! Sadece ${maxAffordable}x ${item.seed} alÄ±nÄ±yor.`);
                            } else {
                                rememberBuyBudgetLock(item.seed, masraf);
                                log(`â¸ï¸ Insufficient coins for ${item.seed}. Waiting until ${formatCoinAmount(masraf)} coin is available.`);
                                continue;
                            }
                        }

                        let dateIso = new Date().toISOString();

                        buyActions.push({
                            type: "seed.bought",
                            item: item.seed,
                            amount: item.amount,
                            createdAt: dateIso
                        });
                        buyPredictedActions.push({
                            type: "seed.bought",
                            item: item.seed,
                            amount: item.amount
                        });

                        currentBudget -= masraf;
                        coinsSpent += masraf;

                        modifyInventory(item.seed, item.amount);
                        let actName = item.seed + " Bought";
                        modifyActivity(actName, item.amount);
                        modifyActivity("Coins Spent", masraf);
                        modifyStock(item.seed, -item.amount);

                        if (i < chunksToProcess.length - 1) {
                            let waitMs = randInt(200, 500);
                            await controlledSleep(waitMs);
                        }
                    }

                    if (buyActions.length > 0 && !stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
                        let stringifiedMaster = JSON.stringify(masterPayload);
                        let payload = JSON.parse(stringifiedMaster);

                        payload.actions = buyActions;
                        SL_COINS -= coinsSpent;
                        lastBotMarketPrediction = {
                            type: "buy",
                            actions: buyPredictedActions,
                            coinsDelta: -coinsSpent,
                            boosts: []
                        };

                        payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
                        payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
                        payload.stateHash.stock = await computeSHA256(SL_STOCK);
                        if (payload.stateHash.coins) {
                            payload.stateHash.coins = await computeSHA256(SL_COINS);
                        }
                        await refreshVolatileStateHashes(payload);

                        log(`ğŸ“¦ AlÄ±m paketi fÄ±rlatÄ±lÄ±yor... (${buyActions.length} eylem)`);

                        try {
                            let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(payload);
                            let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                                method: 'POST',
                                headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                                body: stringifiedPayload
                            });

                            if (res.ok) {
                                log(`âœ… Ä°ÅŸlem BaÅŸarÄ±lÄ±!`);
                                masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                                lastCompletedPhase = 'buy';
                            } else {
                                triggerKillSwitch("Sunucu alÄ±mÄ± reddetti.", res.status);
                                return;
                            }
                        } catch(e) {
                            triggerKillSwitch("AÄŸ baÄŸlantÄ±sÄ± koptu (AlÄ±m).", "NETWORK");
                            return;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
            if (lastCompletedPhase === 'buy') {
                if (hasPlotTasks) {
                    let keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch('alÄ±ÅŸ â†’ ekim');
                    if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                        return;
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        // ---------------------------------------------------------
        // 4. EKÄ°M AÅAMASI
        // ---------------------------------------------------------
        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated && BOT_SETTINGS.autoFields) {
            await forceRadarRefresh('bot control');
            if (stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                return;
            }

            let cropEntries = Object.entries(SL_CROPS);
            let emptyPlots = [];

            for (let i = 0; i < cropEntries.length; i++) {
                let id = cropEntries[i][0];
                let p = cropEntries[i][1];
                if (safePlots.includes(id) && getCropStatus(p) === "EMPTY") {
                    emptyPlots.push(id);
                }
            }
            emptyPlots = shuffleArray(emptyPlots);

            if (emptyPlots.length > 0) {
                let stringifiedMaster = JSON.stringify(masterPayload);
                let payload = JSON.parse(stringifiedMaster);
                payload.actions = [];

                let plantCount = 0;
                let lastPlantedSeed = null;
                let isPlantBatch = true;

                for (let i = 0; i < emptyPlots.length; i++) {
                    if (stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                        break;
                    }

                    let plotId = emptyPlots[i];
                    let targetSeed = PLOT_TASKS[plotId];

                    if (targetSeed) {
                        if (!GameRules.isSeedInCurrentSeason(targetSeed)) {
                            log(`âš ï¸ ${targetSeed} cannot be planted in ${GameRules.getCurrentSeason()} season. Plot skipped.`);
                            continue;
                        }

                        if (!GameRules.canBuySeed(targetSeed)) {
                            log(`âš ï¸ ${targetSeed} cannot be planted. Bumpkin level ${GameRules.getSeedLevelRequirement(targetSeed)} required.`);
                            continue;
                        }

                        let currentStock = parseInt(SL_INVENTORY[targetSeed] || "0");

                        if (currentStock >= 1) {
                            if (plantCount === 0) {
                                actionPerformed = true;
                                let modText = isPlantBatch ? 'Batch' : 'Single';
                                log(`ğŸŒ± Mixed planting starting... [Mode: ${modText}]`);
                            }

                            exhaustedSeedWarnings.delete(targetSeed);

                            if (plantCount > 0) {
                                let waitMs = 0;
                                if (isPlantBatch) {
                                    waitMs = getHumanBatchPlantDelay(lastPlantedSeed, targetSeed, plantCount);
                                } else if (lastPlantedSeed && lastPlantedSeed !== targetSeed) {
                                    waitMs = randInt(800, 1400);
                                } else {
                                    waitMs = randInt(BOT_SETTINGS.plantMin, BOT_SETTINGS.plantMax);
                                }
                                await controlledSleep(waitMs);
                            }

                            try {
                                let randId = Math.random().toString(16).substr(2, 8);
                                let dateIso = new Date().toISOString();

                                payload.actions.push({
                                    type: "seed.planted",
                                    index: plotId,
                                    item: targetSeed,
                                    cropId: randId,
                                    createdAt: dateIso
                                });

                                let cropSade = targetSeed.replace(" Seed", "");
                                modifyInventory(targetSeed, -1);

                                let actName = cropSade + " Planted";
                                modifyActivity(actName, 1);

                                let currentMs = Date.now();
                                const cropTimeInfo = GameRules.getCropGrowTimeMs(cropSade, SL_CROPS[plotId], currentMs);
                                const cropBaseMs = LEARNED_CROP_TIMES[cropSade] || BASE_CROP_TIMES[cropSade] || cropTimeInfo.ms;
                                const cropBoostedTime = Math.max(0, cropBaseMs - cropTimeInfo.ms);
                                const scarecrowBoost = GameRules.getBasicScarecrowBoost(cropSade, SL_CROPS[plotId]);
                                SL_CROPS[plotId].crop = {
                                    name: cropSade,
                                    plantedAt: currentMs - cropBoostedTime,
                                    boostedTime: cropBoostedTime
                                };
                                if (scarecrowBoost.active) {
                                    SL_AOE["Basic Scarecrow"] = SL_AOE["Basic Scarecrow"] || {};
                                    SL_AOE["Basic Scarecrow"][scarecrowBoost.dx] = SL_AOE["Basic Scarecrow"][scarecrowBoost.dx] || {};
                                    SL_AOE["Basic Scarecrow"][scarecrowBoost.dx][scarecrowBoost.dy] = currentMs + cropTimeInfo.ms;
                                    localStorage.setItem('sl_aoe_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_AOE));
                                }
                            } catch(e) {
                                triggerKillSwitch(`Ekim muhasebesi bozuldu: ${e && e.message ? e.message : e}`, "PLANT_ACCOUNTING");
                                return;
                            }

                            plantCount++;
                            lastPlantedSeed = targetSeed;

                            let stringifiedCrops = JSON.stringify(SL_CROPS);
                            localStorage.setItem('sl_crops_cache', stringifiedCrops);

                            if (!isPlantBatch) {
                                safeRenderPlotGrid('single plant');
                            } else if (isPlantBatch && plantCount % 5 === 0) {
                                log(`ğŸŒ± [Batch] Preparing plant payload... (${plantCount} seeds)`);
                            }

                            if (!isPlantBatch) {
                                payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
                                payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
                                payload.stateHash.crops = await computeSHA256(SL_CROPS);
                                if (payload.stateHash.aoe) {
                                    payload.stateHash.aoe = await computeSHA256(SL_AOE);
                                }
                                await refreshVolatileStateHashes(payload);

                                log(`ğŸ“¦ [Single] Sending plant...`);

                                try {
                                    let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(payload);
                                    let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                                        method: 'POST',
                                        headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                                        body: stringifiedPayload
                                    });

                                    if (res.ok) {
                                        log(`âœ… Ä°ÅŸlem BaÅŸarÄ±lÄ±!`);
                                        masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                                        lastCompletedPhase = 'plant';
                                    } else {
                                        triggerKillSwitch("Sunucu tekli ekimi reddetti.", res.status);
                                        return;
                                    }
                                } catch(e) {
                                    triggerKillSwitch("AÄŸ baÄŸlantÄ±sÄ± koptu (Ekim).", "NETWORK");
                                    return;
                                }
                                payload.actions = [];
                            }
                        } else {
                            if (!exhaustedSeedWarnings.has(targetSeed)) {
                                exhaustedSeedWarnings.add(targetSeed);
                                log(`âš ï¸ ${targetSeed} bitti. Pas geÃ§iliyor.`);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (isPlantBatch) {
                    if (payload.actions.length > 0) {
                        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
                            log(`ğŸ§® [Toplu Paket] Ekim muhasebesi hazÄ±rlanÄ±yor... (${plantCount} tohum)`);
                            payload.stateHash.inventory = await computeSHA256(SL_INVENTORY);
                            payload.stateHash.farmActivity = await computeSHA256(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
                            payload.stateHash.crops = await computeSHA256(SL_CROPS);
                            if (payload.stateHash.aoe) {
                                payload.stateHash.aoe = await computeSHA256(SL_AOE);
                            }
                            await refreshVolatileStateHashes(payload);

                            log(`ğŸ“¦ [Toplu Paket] Ekim sepeti fÄ±rlatÄ±lÄ±yor... (${plantCount} tohum)`);

                            try {
                                let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(payload);
                                let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                                    method: 'POST',
                                    headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                                    body: stringifiedPayload
                                });

                                if (res.ok) {
                                    log(`âœ… Ä°ÅŸlem BaÅŸarÄ±lÄ±!`);
                                    masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                                    lastCompletedPhase = 'plant';
                                    safeRenderPlotGrid('toplu ekim');
                                } else {
                                    triggerKillSwitch("Sunucu toplu ekimi reddetti.", res.status);
                                    return;
                                }
                            } catch(e) {
                                triggerKillSwitch("AÄŸ baÄŸlantÄ±sÄ± koptu (Toplu Ekim).", "NETWORK");
                                return;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
            if (lastCompletedPhase === 'plant' && hasCharacterFeedPending()) {
                let keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch('ekim â†’ karakter');
                if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                    return;
                }

                let fedSomething = await runCharacterFeedPhase();
                if (fedSomething) {
                    actionPerformed = true;
                    lastCompletedPhase = 'character';
                }
            }
        }

        // =========================================================
        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated && BOT_SETTINGS.autoFishing) {
            let keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch('farm -> fishing');
            if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                return;
            }

            let fishingDidWork = await runFishingPhase();
            if (fishingDidWork) {
                actionPerformed = true;
                lastCompletedPhase = 'fishing';

                if (hasCharacterFeedPending()) {
                    let feedSwitchOk = await waitTaskSwitch('fishing -> character');
                    if (!feedSwitchOk || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                        return;
                    }
                    let fedSomething = await runCharacterFeedPhase();
                    if (fedSomething) {
                        lastCompletedPhase = 'character';
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated && BOT_SETTINGS.autoDigging) {
            let keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch('farm -> digging');
            if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                return;
            }

            let diggingDidWork = await runDiggingPhase();
            if (diggingDidWork) {
                actionPerformed = true;
                lastCompletedPhase = 'digging';
            }
        }

        // ğŸš€ 5. ORMAN VE MADEN AÅAMASI (TEKLÄ° GÃ–NDERÄ°M VE ONAYLI SÄ°STEM)
        // =========================================================
        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated && (BOT_SETTINGS.autoTree || BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineStone || BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineIron || BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineGold)) {
            let keepGoing = await waitTaskSwitch('farm -> resources');
            if (!keepGoing || stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                return;
            }

            let resourcesDidWork = await runResourceBatchPhase();
            if (resourcesDidWork) {
                actionPerformed = true;
                lastCompletedPhase = 'resources';
            }
        }

        if (false && !stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
            let now = Date.now();

            // --- ğŸŒ² AÄAÃ‡ KESÄ°MÄ° VE BALTA CRAFTING ---
            if (BOT_SETTINGS.autoTree) {
                let treeEntries = getSelectedResourceEntries("trees", SL_TREES || {});

                for (let i = 0; i < treeEntries.length; i++) {
                    if (stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                        break;
                    }

                    let id = treeEntries[i][0];
                    let t = treeEntries[i][1];

                    let treeReadyTime = getResourceReadyAt(t, TREE_RECOVERY_MS, "wood");

                    if (now >= treeReadyTime) {
                        let axeCount = Math.floor(parseFloat(SL_INVENTORY["Axe"] || 0));
                        let reqCoins = CRAFTING_RECIPES["Axe"].coins;

                        // 1. ADIM: EÄER BALTA YOKSA, Ã–NCE BALTA AL VE ONAY BEKLE!
                        if (axeCount < 1 && BOT_SETTINGS.autoCraftAxe && SL_COINS >= reqCoins) {
                            let stringifiedMaster = JSON.stringify(masterPayload);
                            let payload = JSON.parse(stringifiedMaster);

                            let dateIso = new Date().toISOString();
                            payload.actions = [{
                                type: "tool.crafted",
                                tool: "Axe",
                                amount: 1,
                                createdAt: dateIso
                            }];

                            modifyInventory("Axe", 1);
                            SL_COINS -= reqCoins;
                            modifyActivity("Axe Crafted", 1);
                            modifyActivity("Coins Spent", reqCoins);
                            modifyStock("Axe", -1);

                            await refreshCoreAccountingHashes(payload);

                            log(`ğŸ“¦ Blacksmith order: 1x Axe (Cost: ${reqCoins} coin)`);

                            try {
                                let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(payload);
                                let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                                    method: 'POST',
                                    headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                                    body: stringifiedPayload
                                });

                                if (res.ok) {
                                    log(`âœ… Blacksmith success. Axe bought.`);
                                    masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                                    axeCount++;
                                    actionPerformed = true;

                                    await waitManualForestPace('Blacksmith â†’ Forest');
                                } else {
                                    triggerKillSwitch("Server rejected blacksmith axe request.", res.status);
                                    return;
                                }
                            } catch(e) {
                                triggerKillSwitch("Network error (Blacksmith-Axe)", "NETWORK");
                                return;
                            }
                        }

                        // 2. ADIM: EÄER BALTA VARSA, AÄACI KES VE ONAY BEKLE!
                        if (axeCount >= 1 && !stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
                            let stringifiedMaster = JSON.stringify(masterPayload);
                            let payload = JSON.parse(stringifiedMaster);

                            let dateIso = new Date().toISOString();
                            payload.actions = [{
                                type: "timber.chopped",
                                index: id,
                                item: "Axe",
                                createdAt: dateIso
                            }];

                            modifyInventory("Axe", -1);
                            modifyInventory("Wood", 1);
                            modifyActivity("Tree Chopped", 1);
                            modifyActivity("Basic Tree Chopped", 1);

                            SL_TREES[id].wood = { choppedAt: now };
                            let stringifiedTrees = JSON.stringify(SL_TREES);
                            localStorage.setItem('sl_trees_cache', stringifiedTrees);

                            await refreshCoreAccountingHashes(payload);

                            log(`ğŸ“¦ Forest: chopping tree ${id.substr(0,4)}...`);

                            try {
                                let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(payload);
                                let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                                    method: 'POST',

                                    body: stringifiedPayload
                                });

                                    log(`âœ… Tree chopped.`);

                                    actionPerformed = true;
                                } else {

                            await waitManualForestPace('Forest -> next action');

            // --- ğŸª¨ TAÅ KAZIMI VE KAZMA CRAFTING ---
            if (BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineStone) {

                        if (pickCount >= 1 && !stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {

            if (BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineIron) {

                    let ironNode = ironEntries[i][1];

                    if (now >= ironReadyTime) {
                        let stonePickCount = Math.floor(parseFloat(SL_INVENTORY["Stone Pickaxe"] || 0));
                        let requiredPickaxes = Math.max(1, Math.floor(parseFloat(ironNode.multiplier || 1)));

                        if (stonePickCount < requiredPickaxes && BOT_SETTINGS.autoCraftStonePick) {
                            let recipe = CRAFTING_RECIPES["Stone Pickaxe"];
                            let missingPicks = requiredPickaxes - stonePickCount;
                            let woodCount = Math.floor(parseFloat(SL_INVENTORY["Wood"] || 0));
                            let stoneCount = Math.floor(parseFloat(SL_INVENTORY["Stone"] || 0));
                            let maxByWood = Math.floor(woodCount / recipe["Wood"]);
                            let maxByStone = Math.floor(stoneCount / recipe["Stone"]);
                            let maxByCoins = Math.floor(SL_COINS / recipe["coins"]);
                            let maxByStock = Math.floor(parseFloat(SL_STOCK["Stone Pickaxe"] || 0));
                            let craftAmount = Math.min(missingPicks, maxByWood, maxByStone, maxByCoins, maxByStock);

                            if (craftAmount > 0) {
                                let stringifiedMaster = JSON.stringify(masterPayload);
                                let payload = JSON.parse(stringifiedMaster);

                                payload.actions = [];
                                for (let craftIndex = 0; craftIndex < craftAmount; craftIndex++) {
                                    payload.actions.push({
                                        type: "tool.crafted",
                                        tool: "Stone Pickaxe",
                                        amount: 1,
                                        createdAt: new Date(Date.now() + craftIndex * randInt(700, 1300)).toISOString()
                                    });
                                }

                                modifyInventory("Stone Pickaxe", craftAmount);
                                modifyInventory("Wood", -recipe["Wood"] * craftAmount);
                                modifyInventory("Stone", -recipe["Stone"] * craftAmount);
                                SL_COINS -= recipe["coins"] * craftAmount;
                                modifyActivity("Stone Pickaxe Crafted", craftAmount);
                                modifyActivity("Coins Spent", recipe["coins"] * craftAmount);
                                modifyStock("Stone Pickaxe", -craftAmount);

                                await refreshCoreAccountingHashes(payload);

                                log(`ÄŸÅ¸â€œÂ¦ Blacksmith order: ${craftAmount}x Stone Pickaxe`);

                                try {
                                    let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(payload);
                                    let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                                        method: 'POST',
                                        headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                                        body: stringifiedPayload
                                    });

                                    if (res.ok) {
                                        log(`Ã¢Å“â€¦ Blacksmith success. Stone Pickaxe ready.`);
                                        masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                                        stonePickCount += craftAmount;
                                        actionPerformed = true;

                                        await waitTaskSwitch('Blacksmith Ã¢â€ â€™ Iron Miner');
                                    } else {
                                        triggerKillSwitch("Server rejected blacksmith stone pickaxe request.", res.status);
                                        return;
                                    }
                                } catch(e) {
                                    triggerKillSwitch("Network error (Blacksmith-Stone Pickaxe)", "NETWORK");
                                    return;
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        if (stonePickCount >= requiredPickaxes && !stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
                            let stringifiedMaster = JSON.stringify(masterPayload);
                            let payload = JSON.parse(stringifiedMaster);

                            let dateIso = new Date().toISOString();
                            payload.actions = [{
                                type: "ironRock.mined",
                                index: id,
                                createdAt: dateIso
                            }];

                            let ironAmount = parseFloat(ironNode.stone && ironNode.stone.amount ? ironNode.stone.amount : 1);
                            modifyInventory("Stone Pickaxe", -requiredPickaxes);
                            modifyInventory("Iron", ironAmount);
                            modifyActivity("Iron Mined", requiredPickaxes);
                            modifyActivity((ironNode.name || "Iron Rock") + " Mined", 1);

                            if (SL_IRON[id]) {
                                SL_IRON[id].stone = { minedAt: now };
                                localStorage.setItem('sl_iron_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_IRON));
                            }

                            await refreshCoreAccountingHashes(payload);

                            log(`ğŸ“¦ Miner: mining iron ${id.substr(0,4)}...`);

                            try {
                                let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(payload);
                                let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                                    method: 'POST',
                                    headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                                    body: stringifiedPayload
                                });

                                if (res.ok) {
                                    log(`âœ… Iron mined.`);
                                    masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                                    stonePickCount -= requiredPickaxes;
                                    actionPerformed = true;
                                } else {
                                    triggerKillSwitch("Server rejected iron mining action.", res.status);
                                    return;
                                }
                            } catch(e) {
                                triggerKillSwitch("Network error (Iron Miner)", "NETWORK");
                                return;
                            }

                            let waitMs = randInt(800, 1500);
                            await controlledSleep(waitMs);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            if (BOT_SETTINGS.autoMineGold) {
                let goldEntries = getSelectedResourceEntries("gold", SL_GOLD || {});

                for (let i = 0; i < goldEntries.length; i++) {
                    if (stopRequested || killSwitchActivated) {
                        break;
                    }

                    let id = goldEntries[i][0];
                    let goldNode = goldEntries[i][1];
                    let goldReadyTime = getResourceReadyAt(goldNode, GOLD_RECOVERY_MS, "stone");

                    if (now >= goldReadyTime) {
                        let ironPickCount = Math.floor(parseFloat(SL_INVENTORY["Iron Pickaxe"] || 0));
                        let requiredPickaxes = Math.max(1, Math.floor(parseFloat(goldNode.multiplier || 1)));

                        if (ironPickCount < requiredPickaxes && BOT_SETTINGS.autoCraftIronPick) {
                            let recipe = CRAFTING_RECIPES["Iron Pickaxe"];
                            let missingPicks = requiredPickaxes - ironPickCount;
                            let woodCount = Math.floor(parseFloat(SL_INVENTORY["Wood"] || 0));
                            let ironCount = Math.floor(parseFloat(SL_INVENTORY["Iron"] || 0));
                            let maxByWood = Math.floor(woodCount / recipe["Wood"]);
                            let maxByIron = Math.floor(ironCount / recipe["Iron"]);
                            let maxByCoins = Math.floor(SL_COINS / recipe["coins"]);
                            let maxByStock = Math.floor(parseFloat(SL_STOCK["Iron Pickaxe"] || 0));
                            let craftAmount = Math.min(missingPicks, maxByWood, maxByIron, maxByCoins, maxByStock);

                            if (craftAmount > 0) {
                                let stringifiedMaster = JSON.stringify(masterPayload);
                                let payload = JSON.parse(stringifiedMaster);

                                payload.actions = [];
                                for (let craftIndex = 0; craftIndex < craftAmount; craftIndex++) {
                                    payload.actions.push({
                                        type: "tool.crafted",
                                        tool: "Iron Pickaxe",
                                        amount: 1,
                                        createdAt: new Date(Date.now() + craftIndex * randInt(700, 1300)).toISOString()
                                    });
                                }

                                modifyInventory("Iron Pickaxe", craftAmount);
                                modifyInventory("Wood", -recipe["Wood"] * craftAmount);
                                modifyInventory("Iron", -recipe["Iron"] * craftAmount);
                                SL_COINS -= recipe["coins"] * craftAmount;
                                modifyActivity("Iron Pickaxe Crafted", craftAmount);
                                modifyActivity("Coins Spent", recipe["coins"] * craftAmount);
                                modifyStock("Iron Pickaxe", -craftAmount);

                                await refreshCoreAccountingHashes(payload);

                                log(`ÄŸÅ¸â€œÂ¦ Blacksmith order: ${craftAmount}x Iron Pickaxe`);

                                try {
                                    let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(payload);
                                    let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                                        method: 'POST',
                                        headers: makeBotHeaders(),
                                        body: stringifiedPayload
                                    });

                                    if (res.ok) {
                                        log(`Ã¢Å“â€¦ Blacksmith success. Iron Pickaxe ready.`);
                                        masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                                        ironPickCount += craftAmount;
                                        actionPerformed = true;

                                        await waitTaskSwitch('Blacksmith Ã¢â€ â€™ Gold Miner');
                                    } else {
                                        triggerKillSwitch("Server rejected blacksmith iron pickaxe request.", res.status);
                                        return;
                                    }
                                } catch(e) {
                                    triggerKillSwitch("Network error (Blacksmith-Iron Pickaxe)", "NETWORK");
                                    return;
                                }

                        }

                        if (ironPickCount >= requiredPickaxes && !stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
                            let stringifiedMaster = JSON.stringify(masterPayload);
                            let payload = JSON.parse(stringifiedMaster);

                            let dateIso = new Date().toISOString();
                            payload.actions = [{
                                type: "goldRock.mined",
                                index: id,
                                createdAt: dateIso
                            }];

                            let goldAmount = parseFloat(goldNode.stone && goldNode.stone.amount ? goldNode.stone.amount : 1);
                            modifyInventory("Iron Pickaxe", -requiredPickaxes);
                            modifyInventory("Gold", goldAmount);
                            modifyActivity("Gold Mined", requiredPickaxes);
                            modifyActivity((goldNode.name || "Gold Rock") + " Mined", 1);

                            if (SL_GOLD[id]) {
                                SL_GOLD[id].stone = { minedAt: now };
                                localStorage.setItem('sl_gold_cache', JSON.stringify(SL_GOLD));

                                let stringifiedPayload = JSON.stringify(payload);
                                let res = await _window.fetch(`https://api.sunflower-land.com/autosave/${SL_FARM_ID}`, {
                                    method: 'POST',

                                    masterPayload.stateHash = payload.stateHash;
                                    ironPickCount -= requiredPickaxes;
                                    actionPerformed = true;

                                    triggerKillSwitch("Server rejected gold mining action.", res.status);

        }

        // ---------------------------------------------------------
        // 6. OTO-TEDAVÄ° VE NOKTA ATIÅI UYANIÅ (PRECISION WAKE) VE MUHASEBE DENETÃ‡Ä°SÄ°
        // ---------------------------------------------------------
        if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {

            if (!actionPerformed) {
                let nextReadyIn = Infinity;
                let hasReadyHarvest = false;
                let hasPlantableTask = false;
                let hasBlockedPlantTask = false;
                let hasGrowingCrop = false;
                let hasSellWaiting = false;
                let blockedSeeds = [];

                let cropEntries = BOT_SETTINGS.autoFields ? Object.entries(SL_CROPS) : [];

                for (let i = 0; i < cropEntries.length; i++) {
                    let id = cropEntries[i][0];
                    let plot = cropEntries[i][1];

                    if (!safePlots.includes(id)) {
                        continue;
                    }

                    let status = getCropStatus(plot);

                    if (status === "READY") {
                        hasReadyHarvest = true;
                    } else if (status === "EMPTY") {
                        let assignedSeed = PLOT_TASKS[id];
                        if (assignedSeed) {
                            let currentStock = getInventoryAmount(assignedSeed);
                            if (currentStock > 0) {
                                hasPlantableTask = true;
                            } else {
                                hasBlockedPlantTask = true;
                                blockedSeeds.push(assignedSeed);
                            }
                        }
                    } else if (status === "GROWING") {
                        hasGrowingCrop = true;
                        let readyAt = getCropReadyAt(plot);
                        let currentTime = Date.now();
                        let timeRemaining = readyAt - currentTime;

                        if (timeRemaining > 0 && timeRemaining < nextReadyIn) {
                            nextReadyIn = timeRemaining;
                        }
                    }
                }

                let sellEntries = Object.entries(MARKET_SETTINGS.sell || {});
                for (let i = 0; i < sellEntries.length; i++) {
                    let crop = sellEntries[i][0];
                    let cfg = sellEntries[i][1];
                    if (!cfg || !cfg.active) {
                        continue;
                    }

                    let invAmount = getInventoryAmount(crop);
                    let minKeep = parseInt(cfg.min || 0);
                    if (invAmount > minKeep) {
                        hasSellWaiting = true;
                        break;
                    }
                }

                if (hasReadyHarvest || hasSellWaiting || hasPlantableTask) {
                    await controlledSleep(randInt(1800, 3200));
                } else if (nextReadyIn !== Infinity) {
                    let waitSecs = Math.ceil(nextReadyIn / 1000);
                    log(`ğŸ’¤ Tarlada iÅŸ yok. En erken ekin ${waitSecs} saniye sonra hazÄ±r olacak. Alarm kuruldu! â°`);
                    let alarmTime = nextReadyIn + 1000;
                    await controlledSleep(alarmTime);
                } else if (hasBlockedPlantTask && !hasGrowingCrop) {
                    stopForMissingSelectedSeeds(blockedSeeds);
                    return;
                } else {
                    log(`ğŸ’¤ Tarlalar boÅŸ ve gÃ¶rev yok. Bekleniyor...`);
                    await controlledSleep(randInt(8000, 14000));
                }

                if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
                    setTimeout(function() { runAutomationLogic(); }, 100);
                }

                return;
            }

            log(`ğŸ”„ Bot checking...`);

            let expectedCoins = SL_COINS;
            let expectedInv = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(SL_INVENTORY));
            let expectedAct = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY));

            let syncSuccess = await forceRadarRefresh('bot control');

            if (syncSuccess) {
                if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
                    let diffs = [];

                    let coinDiffValue = Math.abs(expectedCoins - SL_COINS);
                    if (coinDiffValue > 0.0001) {
                        diffs.push(`Coins (Expected: ${expectedCoins.toFixed(4)}, Fresh: ${SL_COINS.toFixed(4)})`);
                    }

                    let expectedInvKeys = Object.keys(expectedInv);
                    let actualInvKeys = Object.keys(SL_INVENTORY);
                    let allInvKeys = new Set(expectedInvKeys.concat(actualInvKeys));

                    allInvKeys.forEach(function(k) {
                        let e = parseInt(expectedInv[k] || "0");
                        let a = parseInt(SL_INVENTORY[k] || "0");
                        if (e !== a) {
                            diffs.push(`Inventory -> ${k} (Expected: ${e}, Fresh: ${a})`);
                        }
                    });

                    let expectedActKeys = Object.keys(expectedAct);
                    let actualActKeys = Object.keys(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY);
                    let allActKeys = new Set(expectedActKeys.concat(actualActKeys));

                    allActKeys.forEach(function(k) {
                        let e = parseFloat(expectedAct[k] || 0);
                        let a = parseFloat(SL_FARM_ACTIVITY[k] || 0);
                        if (e !== a) {
                            diffs.push(`Activity -> ${k} (Expected: ${e}, Fresh: ${a})`);
                        }
                    });

                    if (diffs.length === 0) {
                        log(`<span style="color:#4ade80; font-weight:bold;">âœ… ACCOUNTING OK.</span>`);
                    } else {
                        log(`<span style="color:#f87171; font-weight:bold;">âš ï¸ ACCOUNTING MISMATCH:</span><br>- ` + diffs.join('<br>- '));
                        triggerKillSwitch("Accounting mismatch detected.", "SYNC_MISMATCH");
                        return;
                    }
                }
            }

            if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
                log(`ğŸ’¤ Ä°ÅŸlem arasÄ± mola veriliyor...`);
                await waitTaskSwitch('tur tamamlandÄ±');

                if (!stopRequested && !killSwitchActivated) {
                    setTimeout(function() { runAutomationLogic(); }, 100);
                }
            }
        }

        isBotRunning = false;
    }
})();
